ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　读书于邑城金溪。作品：夜听双瀑同刘方叔毛虞卿联句。双瀑赋。题双峰。对月同方叔联句。怀归预别同舍。<div id='poem_65691' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65691' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65691?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夜听双瀑同刘方叔毛虞卿联句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65691'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65691'>夜静双瀑喧，遥闻疑雨来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65691'>润壑生清风，襟宇捐纤埃<span class='inlineComment2'>（龟龄）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65691'>飞鸣撼半空，暗想飘琼瑰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65691'>前观阻步屧，侧耳成徘徊<span class='inlineComment2'>（虞卿）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_65691'>萧然山馆间，此兴何悠哉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_65691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_65691'>子晋不复见，月白空箫台<span class='inlineComment2'>（方叔）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_65691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_65691'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_65691_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1249834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249834?labeling=true' target='_blank'>双瀑赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249834")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249834'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249834'>王子游箫峰之下，访鼻祖于仙籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249834_comment'></div>驻杖屦于金溪，观双瀑之千尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249834_comment'></div>于时骤雨初歇，飘风迅击，飞泉汹涌，怒流湍激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249834_comment'></div>喷烟雾于苍岚，吼蛟龙于大泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249834_comment'></div>百川震而澎湃，万类纷其辟易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249834_comment'></div>疑若倾崖转壑，变丘谷而为陵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249834_comment'></div>又类万马千兵，奏鼓鼙而赴敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249834_comment'></div>久之，狂潦微杀，巨流顺适，灵源复寻于故道，双派交驰于绝脊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249834_comment'></div>势偶殊而卒合，路虽分而稍迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249834_comment'></div>玉箸垂兮拂轻寒，长绅拖兮蘸深碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249834_comment'></div>疑若鲸鲵斗怒兮，力未决而方酣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249834_comment'></div>干镆争锋兮，光交腾而互射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249834_comment'></div>嗟天匠之施巧兮，作胜事于泉石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249834_comment'></div>顾一派之罕有兮，岂双流之易得？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249834_comment'></div>不见夫银河落于半天兮，破庐阜之山色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249834_comment'></div>梅雨飞于石门兮，敞芝田之灵迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249834_comment'></div>潭千丈于石桥兮，渺仙凡之路隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249834_comment'></div>龙雨湫于雁荡兮，分大小而异宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249834_comment'></div>彼独溜而孤飞兮，犹擅名于今昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249834_comment'></div>况并峙而争流兮，作人间之连璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249834_comment'></div>吾欲穷千里之源兮，问化工之始辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249834_comment'></div>思汉使之不复见兮，怅灵槎之难觅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1249834_comment'></div>独终日而登临兮，寄吾怀于幽寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1249834_comment'></div>兴虽尽而忘归兮，犹待乎风清而月白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1249834_comment'></div>于是目瞬飞流之末，耳洗寒潭之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1249834_comment'></div>思往事之微茫，仰遗风而叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1249834_comment'></div>灶中烟冷，难寻入竹之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1249834_comment'></div>峰顶台荒，不见吹箫之客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1249834_comment'></div>赋罢，乃歌而归，曰：双瀑之水从何来，灵源千尺高崔嵬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1249834_comment'></div>飞流喷沫飘琼瑰，空山落日鸣春雷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1249834_comment'></div>有客来游独徘徊，枕流嗽石兴悠哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1249834_comment'></div>尘襟濯罢飘然回，风清月白空箫台。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1249834_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_92665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_92665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/92665?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_2_92665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_92665'>今宵对婵娟，莫放酣歌绝<span class='inlineComment2'>（龟龄）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_92665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_92665'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_92665_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>怀归预别同舍</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_0_541376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541376'>溪山虽好何如归，吾心已逐秋云飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541376'>欲别良朋重呜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>咽，催人啼鸟声何切。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541376'>明日琴书随我东，何如尊酒重相逢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541376'></div><div id='poem_note_541376_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月9日</a>　重阳节与父亲以及同学登左原东山。作品：赏菊。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1134')">1132-1134年</a>　读书于邑城金溪。作品：送刘方叔简全之。送陈商霖。孙子尚过明庆以诗见招。怀子尚。潘歧哥。南浦老人诗序。读亲征诏书二首。乐清僧寮有过客钱之翰题二绝，有伤时之叹，因次其韵。闻韩帅退保丹阳，远近忧惧，州县议结乡兵以备不虞。次韵题曹大夫怀忠阁。送曹大夫赴行在所。潜涧严闍黎文集序。<div id='poem_541369' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541369' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541369?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送刘方叔兼简全之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541369")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541369'>断魂梅的皪，过眼柳萧疏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541369'>疋马来时路，征鸿别后书。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541369'>君归见温叟，为我问何如。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541369'></div><div id='poem_sentence_1_541348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541348'>思君一日成三岁，寄我行书直万金。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_541350'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541350'>满眼干戈行路难，故人千里驻征鞍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541350'>几劳终日驰魂梦，安得乘风插羽翰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541350'>水北山南春寂寂，天涯海角路漫漫。<div href='/Writing/541344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潘岐哥</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_541344'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541344'>君不见凤之雏，骥之子，潘家岐哥无乃是。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541344'>鹤溪仙子降英灵，雁荡名山钟秀美。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541344'>颜色纯明白玉璞，精神皎洁秋江水。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541344'>胸中之气已<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_541344", 541344, id='poem_sentence_4_541344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541344'>宁非汉代偷桃朔，别是唐家谪仙李。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541344'>愚知先生百不忧，但患此儿名盛耳。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541344'>先生才高爵未绾，赖渠力振家声起。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541344'>鹿岩他日筑高门，车马煌煌塞闾里。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_541344_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1250132' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250132' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250132?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南浦老人诗集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250132")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250132_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250132'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250132'>绍兴壬子秋，南浦翁丧于横阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250132_comment'></div>讣至，某哭之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250132_comment'></div>已而发囊中，得其遗稿，有诗数十首，皆手所亲书，视之叹曰：「虽无老成人，尚有典刑，吾不复见此翁矣，此稿其典刑乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250132_comment'></div>某恨生太晚，不及识翁壮年时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250132_comment'></div>见乡人言：「翁昔年豪气可掬，常坐屈辈行，直出其上，有不可其意，辄以气排之，尤简世俗辈，视之若无人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250132_comment'></div>性嗜酒，不治生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250132_comment'></div>晚年偃蹇不遇，家贫无资，饘粥是累，东役西驰，有酸寒可怜态，前日之气使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250132_comment'></div>子不见去时得一醉，扬眉瞬目，高谈雄辩，尚有壮年之风」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250132_comment'></div>某年少狂妄，幸得以诗礼与翁接，获陪绪馀之论，乘间以乡人语问之，翁微颔而笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1250132_comment'></div>予又问：「昔年制作，尚能记否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1250132_comment'></div>翁曰：「尽亡矣，吾壮年不独豪于气，亦豪于诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1250132_comment'></div>今日气穷，诗亦然也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1250132_comment'></div>予悲其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1250132_comment'></div>翁虽老，作诗不辍，一日常不下数首，皆信口成，不加鍜鍊而有自然气象，然随作随亡，不复顾惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1250132_comment'></div>予既一二年与之游，惧其老而死，不可复得，屡求之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1250132_comment'></div>一日，以稿示予，皆近作所藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1250132_comment'></div>岁馀而翁死，遂出之，合平日所记与儿曹所传，录成一集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1250132_comment'></div>然尚有恨者，所得止暮年之一二，多穷愁抑郁之气，壮年豪迈语无一字留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1250132_comment'></div>吁可惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1250132_comment'></div>翁姓刘，讳光，字谦仲，本南浦人，久寓居乐清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1250132_comment'></div>乡人以其老也，呼之曰老刘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1250132_comment'></div>予命其集曰《南浦老人集》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1250132_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541353' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541353' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541353?labeling=true' "poem_title_541364")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541364_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541364'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541364'>西北连年杀气高，群盗横行如猬毛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541364'>廉颇李牧不世出，吾皇侧席心焦劳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541364'>汾阳自古多壮士，曹侯意气千人豪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541364'>年今四十犹偃蹇，拊髀长叹淹龙韬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541364'>慨然挥袂谒行在，报国已淬腰间刀。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541364'>登坛拜将预指日，看君举手清风涛<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《梅溪先生文集》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541364'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_541364_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1250133' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250133' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250133?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潜涧严阇梨文集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250133")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250133_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250133'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250133'>某始总角，见祖母贾常道其兄严阇梨之为人，必继之以欷歔涕泣，某幼而未识之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250133_comment'></div>及稍成童，出游乡校，见先辈老成，多能道其事，且称其文翰俱妙，不独冠绝于其徒，往往吾儒中亦鲜能及者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250133_comment'></div>某时既闻其言而得其为人，且私慕之，恨乎生之晚，不及一见焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250133_comment'></div>迨今又十年馀，始获见其诗文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250133_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250133_comment'></div>师真非常人，惜乎遁迹于桑门，无贤士大夫与之游，推扬而夸大之，遂使其名泯灭而无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250133_comment'></div>某见古之隐者逃名而名益彰，晦身而身益显，是无他，有贤士大夫推扬而夸大之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250133_comment'></div>佛之徒本无求于世，真所谓逃名而晦身者，然古之高僧皆能垂名于不朽，盖其所与游尽当世知名之士，如晋、宋、李唐道林、道安、惠远、惠休、文畅、皎然之徒，其所与游则王逸少、谢安石、习凿齿、谢灵运、鲍明远、柳子厚、韦应物诸公，皆一时选，议论所加，天下以为轻重，遂能使幽潜隐遁之迹蔼然发挥于当世，而垂耀于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250133_comment'></div>以师之聪明高学，卓然过人，使得王、谢之徒与之游，假其吹嘘奖拔之力，则声名振世，未必不如古之高人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1250133_comment'></div>师尝作《温州开元天王殿记》，文词雄伟，脍炙人口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1250133_comment'></div>有俞清老者，一时名士，见而叹服，以书来告曰：「不意今人中复见古人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1250133_comment'></div>然其人誉望非安石、逸少诸公比，亦不能成师之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1250133_comment'></div>师少出游江湖，历遍山川，飞锡帝都，振衣嵩、洛，览古人之遗迹，徘徊于其间，然其志节甚高，未尝甚屈以求王公大人之知己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1250133_comment'></div>其言有曰：「古之桑门上首与士大夫游，非求之也，道自合焉尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1250133_comment'></div>既而还东嘉，隐潜涧，诛茅结庐于山林间，赋诗鼓琴以自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1250133_comment'></div>顾世莫己知者，其诗有「欲言重叹无余和」之句，某一读而三悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1250133_comment'></div>师之没今二十三年矣，平生制述甚多，旋已<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1250133", 1250133, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>遗亡</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1250133_comment'></div>某顷游明庆，访师之旧庐而求其遗文，师之弟子曰：「宗要者，某之叔父也，得其古律诗杂文通数十篇，为一卷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1250133_comment'></div>出以相示，某既自五岁而知师之名，十岁而爱慕其为人，又叹其不遇知己而没世无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1250133_comment'></div>今喜见其文，如见其人，遂丐以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1250133_comment'></div>又自顾晚学小子无声名势力可以动人，能重师之文于世，姑叙而藏之，以俟知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1250133_comment'></div>师名处严，字伯威，其诗醇重典实，不尚浮靡，他文皆如之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1250133_comment'></div>绍兴甲寅仲冬望日序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1250133_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年8月</a>　读书于邑城金溪，乐清县学落成，参加落成祭奠。作品：县学落成百韵。<div id='poem_541385' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541385' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541385?labeling=true' target='_blank'>县学落成百韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541385")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_541385_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541385'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541385'>炎正中微后，皇家再造年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541385'>斯文天未丧，吾道圣相传。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541385'>黼扆端周冕，岩廊拱舜弦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541385'>宸章丽朝日，奎画焕中天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541385'>贾马朝丹阙，皇夔捧御筵。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541385'>云龙庆相遇，星凤快争先。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541385'>金马袍披锦，戎亭帐褫毡。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541385'>崇儒符汉武，复古慕周宣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541385'>方议成均制，仍增博士员。<div id='poem_sentence_8_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_541385'>伫观旂茷茷，行贲帛戋戋。<div id='poem_sentence_9_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_541385'>词赋扬群彦，贤良策万全。<div id='poem_sentence_10_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_541385'>圜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>桥汉亿万，鼓箧鲁三千。<div id='poem_sentence_11_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_541385'>狂客休歌凤，骚人肯钓鳊。<div id='poem_sentence_12_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_541385'>文风畅蛮貊，士气压腥膻。<div id='poem_sentence_13_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_541385'>王化诚无外，吾邦素自偏。<div id='poem_sentence_14_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_541385'>鱼盐人竞习，刀笔世相沿。<div id='poem_sentence_15_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_541385'>甘学樊迟稼，纷求许汜田。<div id='poem_sentence_16_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_541385'>揶揄戏缝掖，膜呗奉真诠。<div id='poem_sentence_17_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_541385'>未振寒乡陋，那经杀气缠。<div id='poem_sentence_18_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_541385'>闾阎森白刃，庠序燎寒烟。<div id='poem_sentence_19_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_541385'>断简嗟何考，青衿痛自怜。<div id='poem_sentence_20_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_541385'>诗存伤瓠叶，礼废忆豚肩。<div id='poem_sentence_21_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_541385'>磬碎交州石，弓焚矍相弦。<div id='poem_sentence_22_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_541385'>水流空涣涣，草碧自芊芊。<div id='poem_sentence_23_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_541385'>有识思兴起，无知分弃捐。<div id='poem_sentence_24_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_541385'>桑弧谁复射，城阙孰思还。<div id='poem_sentence_25_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_541385'>弟子贫原宪，先生冷郑虔。<div id='poem_sentence_26_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_541385'>嗣音几泯灭，素业遂迍邅。<div id='poem_sentence_27_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_541385'>屡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>应三年诏，曾微万选钱。<div id='poem_sentence_28_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_541385'>龙门无几到，虎榜不多联。<div id='poem_sentence_29_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_541385'>愈赋徒伤感，郊肠厌炒煎。<div id='poem_sentence_30_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_541385'>儒冠空叹误，铁砚莫知研。<div id='poem_sentence_31_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_541385'>白日非偏照，寒灰自不然。<div id='poem_sentence_32_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_541385'>百年嗟委靡，今日幸夤缘。<div id='poem_sentence_33_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_541385'>令尹真人杰，同僚命世贤。<div id='poem_sentence_34_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_541385'>崔丞老文<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>学，梅尉旧神仙。<div id='poem_sentence_35_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_541385'>乐善诚何笃，承流志更专。<div id='poem_sentence_36_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_541385'>下车伤弊俗，修泮慕遗编。<div id='poem_sentence_37_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_541385'>浮议畴能夺，良谋断不愆。<div id='poem_sentence_38_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_541385'>商财方萃聚，卜日肯迁延。<div id='poem_sentence_39_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_541385'>役命诸生董，基谋爽垲迁。<div id='poem_sentence_40_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_541385'>邓林搜蓊郁，淇竹剪婵娟。<div id='poem_sentence_41_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_541385'>秘殿雄千尺，脩廊跨百廛。<div id='poem_sentence_42_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_541385'>虹梁挂天宇，云栋轶星躔。<div id='poem_sentence_43_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_541385'>缥缥飞鸳瓦，沉沉耀采椽。<div id='poem_sentence_44_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_541385'>沚茂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>春色早，坛杏午阴圆。<div id='poem_sentence_45_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_541385'>方沼分寒溜，明窗瞰碧涟。<div id='poem_sentence_46_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_541385'>前山昂马首，胜地夺龙眠。<div id='poem_sentence_47_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_541385'>瀑水灵源近，箫峰秀色妍。<div id='poem_sentence_48_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_541385'>规模何廓廓，气象更绵绵。<div id='poem_sentence_49_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_541385'>先圣风流远，新宫象貌鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_50_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_541385'>森罗龙衮列，肃穆雁行连。<div id='poem_sentence_51_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_541385'>剑佩星辰上，丹青日月边。<div id='poem_sentence_52_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_541385'>衣裳明黼黻，冠冕饰纮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>綖。<div id='poem_sentence_53_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_541385'>祀事脩崇报，心斋务至蠲。<div id='poem_sentence_54_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_541385'>新仪仍再习，吉日已重涓。<div id='poem_sentence_55_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_541385'>漏箭催庭燎，鸾刀待饩牵。<div id='poem_sentence_56_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_541385'>充庭端弁服，夹道拥车骈。<div id='poem_sentence_57_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_541385'>秉笏趍帷幄，升阶省豆笾。<div id='poem_sentence_58_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_541385'>馨香登黍稷，肥腯荐牲牷。<div id='poem_sentence_59_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_541385'>蔬撷罗芹藻，鱼羞备薧鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_60_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_541385'>牺尊澄玉液，宝篆喷龙涎。<div id='poem_sentence_61_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_541385'>荐裸仍更貌，观瞻竞曲拳。<div id='poem_sentence_62_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_541385'>礼文稽戴郑，乐舞奏韶卷。<div id='poem_sentence_63_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_541385'>设礼筵初秩，登门屦已填。<div id='poem_sentence_64_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_541385'>盍簪联桂玉，纫佩杂兰荃<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作全，据四库本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_65_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_541385'>饰喜捐丝竹，论文具管笺。<div id='poem_sentence_66_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_541385'>献酬咸偻伛，进退各周旋。<div id='poem_sentence_67_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_541385'>挥麈<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>谈飞屑，濡毫思涌泉。<div id='poem_sentence_68_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_541385'>妙词歌郢<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑺</sup>客，醉墨洒张颠。<div id='poem_sentence_69_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_70_541385'>共喜从于迈，俱忘咏式遄。<div id='poem_sentence_70_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_541385'>武纷堂上接，衣拥坐隅褰。<div id='poem_sentence_71_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_541385'>父鄙金籯满，师誇腹笥便。<div id='poem_sentence_72_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_541385'>雩风开性柳，教雨长材楩。<div id='poem_sentence_73_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_541385'>鼓瑟求<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑻</sup>曾点，攀鳞至闵骞。<div id='poem_sentence_74_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_541385'>水平翻振鹭，天阔戾飞鸢。<div id='poem_sentence_75_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_541385'>莺思友<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作友思）</span>迁木，骅群尽著鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_76_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_541385'>草空收七壁，雀过堕三鳣。<div id='poem_sentence_77_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_541385'>道也将行矣，辰乎盍勉旃。<div id='poem_sentence_78_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_541385'>搜寻罗简札，点勘费丹铅。<div id='poem_sentence_79_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_541385'>洁净穷爻象，温柔考注笺。<div id='poem_sentence_80_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_541385'>典谟稽古学，仓<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑼</sup>制究残编。<div id='poem_sentence_81_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_541385'>异教排韩子，遗绖抱玉川。<div id='poem_sentence_82_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_541385'>壮夫羞篆刻，童子悟幽玄。<div id='poem_sentence_83_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_541385'>道德勤钻仰，文章变俨骈。<div id='poem_sentence_84_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_541385'>科名真溷尔，翰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑽</sup>墨盖游焉。<div id='poem_sentence_85_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_86_541385'>雪耻终兴越，成功必霸燕。<div id='poem_sentence_86_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_541385'>真成两阙里，别是一陶甄。<div id='poem_sentence_87_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_541385'>化出文翁表，功居范宁前。<div id='poem_sentence_88_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_89_541385'>声莘终不朽，琬琰岂须镌。<div id='poem_sentence_89_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_90_541385'>未<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作末）</span>学成鸠拙，穷居类兔跧。<div id='poem_sentence_90_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_91_541385'>肠枯无锦绣，门冷乏貂蝉。<div id='poem_sentence_91_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_541385'>箪食虽云乐，藜床已厌穿。<div id='poem_sentence_92_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_93_541385'>室空司马壁，食窘鲁公饘。<div id='poem_sentence_93_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_94_541385'>误拜殽陵赐，长怀渭水畋。<div id='poem_sentence_94_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_95_541385'>断弦音寂寞，抱玉涕潺湲。<div id='poem_sentence_95_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_96_541385'>览镜时犹在，焚舟志益坚。<div id='poem_sentence_96_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_97_541385'>燕归欣遇厦，鱼得敢忘筌。<div id='poem_sentence_97_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_98_541385'>愿赴功名会，终归造化权。<div id='poem_sentence_98_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_99_541385'>唯凭大炉火，早晚铸颜渊。<div id='poem_sentence_99_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_100_541385'></div><div id='poem_sentence_100_541385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_35_541385_0'>⑶ 原重文字，据四库本删</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_45_541385_0'>⑷ 四库本作蘋，雍正本、光绪本作莪</div></div><div class='inline1'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_85_541385_0'>⑽ 原作输，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541385_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1136')">1135-1136年</a>　就读乐清县学。作品：至乐斋读书。用前韵酬昌龄弟。游灵岩辉老索诗至灵峰寄数语。送表叔贾元范赴省试。游西岑遇雨。<div id='poem_541399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>至乐斋读书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541399")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_541399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541399'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541399'>权门迹不到，颜巷自安贫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541399'>独与圣贤对，更于灯火亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541399'>夜观常及子，昼讽直从寅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541399'>莫恨成名晚，诗书不负人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541399'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_541399_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>用前韵酬昌龄弟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541400")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_541400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541400'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541400'>原宪曾非病，陈平岂久贫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541400'>路遥骐骥困，原近鹡鸰亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541400'>窗几坐穷夕，更筹听报寅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541400'>田园劳尔辈，愧是素餐人<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541400'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_541400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_541400'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_541400_0'>⑴ 自注：予拙于治生，每以田园劳二弟，昌龄诗云：诗书满肠腹，应笑带经人。予愧其言，故云。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541400_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_541934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游灵岩辉老索诗至灵峰寄数语</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541934")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541934'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541934'>雁荡冠天下，灵岩尤绝奇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541934'>烟霞列屏障<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：烟霞障。）</span>，日月明旌旗<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：屏旗峰。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541934'>岩前有卓笔<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：卓笔峰。）</span>，可以书雄词。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541934'>天聪况非遥<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：天聪洞。）</span>，𣶈<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>然听无疑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541934'>愿起灵湫龙，霖雨行何为。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541934'>愿用真柱石<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：天柱峰。）</span>，永支廊庙危。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541934'>愿煽造化炉<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：煽韛炉。）</span>，四海归淳熙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541934'>愿招鸾凤友<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：双鸾峰。）</span>，朝廷相羽仪。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541934'>何人梦石室<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：石室属灵峰。）</span>，妄诞夸一时。<div id='poem_sentence_8_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_541934'>那能了世缘，未兑贪嗔痴。<div id='poem_sentence_9_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_541934'>名山误见污<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，公议安可欺。<div id='poem_sentence_10_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_541934'>愿借灵湫水，一洗了堂碑。<div id='poem_sentence_11_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_541934'>诗以寄老禅，狂言勿吾嗤。<div id='poem_sentence_12_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_541934'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_541934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_541934'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_541934_0'>⑴ 雍正本、光绪本作洞</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_541934_0'>⑵ 原作汗，据四库本、雍正本、光绪本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541934_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_541365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541365?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送表叔贾元范赴省试</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541365")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541365'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541365'>河东先生才行高，昔游太学联烝髦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541365'>雄文伟论万人敌，糠秕歆向奴刘曹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541365'>抟风自许九万里，肯作斥鴳游蓬蒿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541365'>礼闱一战果得隽，妙割不折庖丁刀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541365'>礼部无端抑韩子，至今士论犹嗷嗷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541365'>霜蹄暂蹶志益锐，不学郊岛徒悲号。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541365'>圣君图治方侧席，兹复下诏求贤豪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541365'>壮怀思雪会稽耻，广场猛效兰皋鏖。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541365'>焚舟决胜在此举，乡闾属望心焦劳。<div id='poem_sentence_8_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_541365'>天庭射策决素蕴，忠言为国驱腥臊。<div id='poem_sentence_9_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_541365'>区区一第溷君耳，要将事业窥伊皋。<div id='poem_sentence_10_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_541365'>琼林宴罢跃归骑，薰风拂面吹恩袍。<div id='poem_sentence_11_541365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_541365'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_541365_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541387?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游西岑遇雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541387")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541387'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541387'>西岑风物秋更嘉，杖藜出郭欢无涯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541387'>深村有酒隔烟渚，共乘小艇穿芦花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541387'>罗裙绰约越溪女，茅舍迫窄吴侬家。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541387'>床头新酿喜正熟，千金倒瓮倾流霞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541387'>天公妒我一日乐，俄然雨脚来如麻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541387'>醉归扶路泥没股，冠巾不整头鬖髿。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541387'>人生贵在适意耳，安能局缩身如蜗。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541387'>杖头有钱即相觅，明日更泛仙源槎。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541387'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_541387_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a115d03e883744b28c585f1a069b32e8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a115d03e883744b28c585f1a069b32e8");'><span id='a115d03e883744b28c585f1a069b32e8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1145')">1138-1145年</a>，27-34岁</div><div id='a115d03e883744b28c585f1a069b32e8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　读书于鹿岩书院，从潘翼先生学。作品：寄僧觉无象。<div id='poem_541377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄僧觉无象</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541377")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541377'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541377'>我昔居鹿岩，时来潜涧游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541377'>西坡访觉老，终日为迟留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541377'>高谈穷古今，满坐风生秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541377'>令我名利心，一听浑欲休。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541377'>论诗出古律，有唱无不酬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541377'>篇章溢缣素，锦绣烂然浮。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541377'>此老岂易得，当于前辈求。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541377'>吾生限太晚，见师已白头。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541377'>儒释道不同，相从苦无由。<div id='poem_sentence_8_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_541377'>三年游金溪，兀坐颜常愀。<div id='poem_sentence_9_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_541377'>出门无游从，独赋临清流。<div id='poem_sentence_10_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_541377'>金溪可<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>无僧，孰是西坡俦。<div id='poem_sentence_11_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_541377'>深房锁花木，妙供罗珍羞。<div id='poem_sentence_12_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_541377'>益作潜涧思，刚肠如转辀。<div id='poem_sentence_13_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_541377'>魂梦不自禁，夜夜飞山陬。<div id='poem_sentence_14_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_541377'>前日遇诸涂，一笑忘百忧。<div id='poem_sentence_15_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_541377'>相视未及语，归袖风飕飕。<div id='poem_sentence_16_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_541377'>别来能几时，不觉岁月遒。<div id='poem_sentence_17_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_541377'>闻师结莲社，旦莫事真修。<div id='poem_sentence_18_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_541377'>我狂似灵运，此志那能投。<div id='poem_sentence_19_541377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 雍正本、光绪本作讵</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541377_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　读书于鹿岩书院，娶夫人贾氏，长子闻诗出生。作品：孟甲生日。<div id='poem_541645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_4_542059_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1142')">1141-1142年</a>　居乡。作品：毛虞卿见过。读孙子尚旧所寄书。咏柳。前诗送三乡丈行，虽各献芹，然非所以勉子大夫茂明大对之意，更为古诗一章。<div id='poem_541415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>毛虞卿见过</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541415")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541415'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541415'>故人访吾庐，况是清和节。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541415'>高槐绿成阴，芳草碧未歇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541415'>携手山间行，清兴浩然发。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541415'>呼童具鸡黍，浊酒醅初泼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541415'>贫居愧荒凉，野蔌草罗列。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541415'>盘实饤梅豆，蔬餐荐薇蕨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541415'>主礼虽甚微，客色未尝觖。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541415'>醉翁山水意，不为壶觞设。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541415'>蟹眼煎新汲，雀舌烹春撷。<div id='poem_sentence_8_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_541415'>浇君文字肠，掉我清谈舌。<div id='poem_sentence_9_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_541415'>人生会面难，岁月易飘忽。<div id='poem_sentence_10_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_541415'>君姑为我留，匆匆莫言别。<div id='poem_sentence_11_541415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_541415'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_541415_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读孙子尚旧所寄书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541416")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541416'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541416'>故人之书不易得，片纸只字皆可惜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541416'>收拾永为巾笥藏，纵得千金不愿易。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541416'>开缄展转时一读，读未能终泪横臆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541416'>之人门地盛衣冠，万里家居帝王宅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541416'>干戈缭绕飘吾乡，倾盖论交似畴昔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541416'>我年初冠君犹少，握手游从忝联璧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541416'>金溪风月供醉吟，君唱我酬常即席。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541416'>君诗句句清且新，高压曹刘倒元白。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541416'>我才短浅何足论，彊伴宁容小生敌。<div id='poem_sentence_8_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_541416'>追风骏足横海鳞，暂困盐车与污泽。<div id='poem_sentence_9_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_541416'>掉头一去不可寻，南北茫茫烟水隔。<div id='poem_sentence_10_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_541416'>往年雁字时复传，近日诗筒杳难觅。<div id='poem_sentence_11_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_541416'>眼中不见故人面，纸上空怀故人迹。<div id='poem_sentence_12_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_541416'>人生会合能几回，一别八年同瞬息。<div id='poem_sentence_13_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_541416'>我去无由君不来，尊酒相逢更何夕。<div id='poem_sentence_14_541416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_541416'></div><div id='poem_content_541781'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541781'>读书窥古今，掩卷成叱咤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541781'>唐虞昔垂衣，禹稷起躬稼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541781'>人材各超绝，王业迭兴谢。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541781'>典谟光日月，雅颂蔼兰麝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541781'>孟轲<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作子舆）</span>论易地，颜回堪并驾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541781'>穷达虽殊途，圣贤实同价。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541781'>避就乡邻斗，泣笑疏戚谢。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541781'>甘心惟饮瓢，没齿不谈霸。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541781'>斯人嗟已亡，末<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>俗遂多诈。<div id='poem_sentence_8_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_541781'>禄从枉道求，气为权门下。<div id='poem_sentence_9_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_541781'>争为邑犬吠，翻取猎师骂。<div id='poem_sentence_10_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_541781'>幽人思隐盘，高士欲耕灞。<div id='poem_sentence_11_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_541781'>予生苦多难，安迹殊未暇。<div id='poem_sentence_12_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_541781'>冬行皲两足，夜坐痹双髂。<div id='poem_sentence_13_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_541781'>黄卷徒自劳，青云未能跨。<div id='poem_sentence_14_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_541781'>借势乏王公，成名无仆射。<div id='poem_sentence_15_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_541781'>大学厌齑盐，亲闱疏脍炙。<div id='poem_sentence_16_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_541781'>眷眷日怀归，区区每求假。<div id='poem_sentence_17_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_541781'>飞同鹢过宋，闲若马归华。<div id='poem_sentence_18_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_541781'>陋巷怀哲人，短檠烧午夜。<div id='poem_sentence_19_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_541781'>对床有兄弟，通家足姻娅。<div id='poem_sentence_20_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_541781'>谈笑开芳尊，尘劳释征靶。<div id='poem_sentence_21_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_541781'>篇章日盈囊，卷帙时抽架。<div id='poem_sentence_22_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_541781'>咏歌同舞雩，叹息殊观蜡。<div id='poem_sentence_23_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_541781'>有田聊代禄，无谪不祈赦。<div id='poem_sentence_24_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_541781'>未为雄草玄，谩学愈苴罅。<div id='poem_sentence_25_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_541781'>啸傲穷朝曛，弦歌达冬夏。<div id='poem_sentence_26_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_541781'>头角姑自藏，齿牙谁肯借。<div id='poem_sentence_27_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_541781'>眠从弟子嘲，醉不金吾怕。<div id='poem_sentence_28_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_541781'>心知得失妄，眼见炎凉乍。<div id='poem_sentence_29_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_541781'>造物岂吾苦，交情勿渠讶。<div id='poem_sentence_30_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_541781'>马来未为福，火尽安足藉。<div id='poem_sentence_31_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_541781'>孝弟傥自脩，长幼必能化。<div id='poem_sentence_32_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_541781'>力耕西畴禾，剩种东皋柘。<div id='poem_sentence_33_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_541781'>旨甘奉盘餐，温凊饰台榭。<div id='poem_sentence_34_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_541781'>斗粟鉴汉谣，一爨共崔舍。<div id='poem_sentence_35_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_541781'>仰效慈乌哺，俯笑寒鸱吓。<div id='poem_sentence_36_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_541781'>但令尊不空，莫厌客频迓。<div id='poem_sentence_37_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_541781'>风篁观掩冉，山禽听娇姹。<div id='poem_sentence_38_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_541781'>困穷乃吾幸，此祸不须嫁。<div id='poem_sentence_39_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_541781'></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_541781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_541781'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_541781_0'>⑴ 原作未，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541781_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年11月11日</a>　过万桥,会饮万先之家。作品：和韩诗醉赠张秘书寄万大年先之中之。<div id='poem_541780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和韩醉赠张秘书寄万大年先之申之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年11月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541780")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541780'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541780'>良友不易得，清谈苦难闻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541780'>前夕知何夕，我来访诸君。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541780'>共对灯烛光，芳尊细论文。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541780'>通家忝孔李，促席联机云。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541780'>杯盘略荷礼，气味同清芬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541780'>一盏洗穷愁，三杯话离群。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541780'>春舟会稽别<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：孟夏别大年于会稽。）</span>，秋袂钱塘分<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：七月先之归，八月申之归。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541780'>顾我与三友，新当败孤军。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541780'>飘零各南北，对酒无复醺。<div id='poem_sentence_8_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_541780'>客况饱牢落，时光负氤氲。<div id='poem_sentence_9_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_541780'>聚散实堪恨，荣枯何足云。<div id='poem_sentence_10_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_541780'>归来已三月，俗状日纷纷。<div id='poem_sentence_11_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_541780'>幸此同一笑，盘餐饤腥荤。<div id='poem_sentence_12_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_541780'>蚝山荐巨房，龟脚烹脩裙。<div id='poem_sentence_13_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_541780'>良辰属严冬，败欢无蝇蚊。<div id='poem_sentence_14_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_541780'>痛饮竟长夜，高歌和南薰。<div id='poem_sentence_15_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_541780'>虽非韩孟张，所饮亦典坟。<div id='poem_sentence_16_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_541780'>何时脱场屋，南亩同耕耘。<div id='poem_sentence_17_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_541780'>昼为鸡豚社，夜策诗酒勋。<div id='poem_sentence_18_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_541780'>此言宜早践，勿待桑榆曛。<div id='poem_sentence_19_541780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_541780'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_541780_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年1月11日</a>　左原家居。作品：己巳元日度送杨郎中贺正诗因和其韵。<div id='poem_541791' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541791' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541791?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己巳元日读韩送杨郎中贺正诗因和其韵</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_541791'>晓<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>日五更鸡咿喔，银缸明灭烧馀脂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541791_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541791'>家家呼牛逐耗鬼，牛归谁家鬼何之。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541791_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541791'>皇都朝会我无与，西畴春事行及期。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541791_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541791'>弟兄成行拜亲老，犹胜去年身未归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541791_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541791'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_541791_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_541791'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_541791_0'>⑴ 原作鸡，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541791_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年3月30日</a>　左原家居，与同舍送春于梅溪。作品：三月晦日与同舍送春于梅溪因诵贾阆仙诗云三月更当三十日风光别我苦吟身共君今夜不须睡未到晓钟犹是春时有二十八人遂以齿序分韵。<div id='poem_541474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541474' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541474?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三月晦日与同舍送春于梅溪因诵贾阆仙诗云三月更当三十日，风光别我苦吟身共君今夜不须睡未到晓钟犹是春时有二十八人遂以齿序分韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年3月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541474")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_541474_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541474'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541474'>却因送别还惊我，老境如蚕已食三。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541474'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_541474_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　左原家居。作品：和答柳柳州食虾蟇。<div id='poem_541795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541795' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541795?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和韩答柳柳州食虾蟆</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541795")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541795_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541795'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541795'>虫鱼千万族，一一异状貌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541795'>飞潜同一性，巨细何必校。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541795'>彼微水中蛙，四足伛而疱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541795'>自从科蚪初，生育在泥淖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541795'>好鸣乃其性，非故欲喧闹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541795'>蝈氏职洒灰，恐非圣人教。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541795'>吾闻人间世，生死同梦觉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541795'>杀物伤吾仁，忍听声熚爆。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541795'>况我儒衣冠，弦诵生乡校。<div id='poem_sentence_8_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_541795'>彼亦呼子曰，有意欲吾效<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_541795'>人虫各好生，奚用苦相挠。<div id='poem_sentence_10_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_541795'>退之惮食蛇，得得释笼罩。<div id='poem_sentence_11_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_541795'>子厚放鹧鸪，仁心亦稍稍。<div id='poem_sentence_12_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_541795'>胡为于此虫，未尽忘嗜乐。<div id='poem_sentence_13_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_541795'>荐祠用枭獍，穿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>阱诛虎豹。<div id='poem_sentence_14_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_541795'>古人岂妄杀，去害除不孝。<div id='poem_sentence_15_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_541795'>愿留兹鼓吹，驻我寒溪棹<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《梅溪先生文集》卷九）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_541795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 自注：谚云住近孔堂，虾蟆呼子曰，故以为戏。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_541795_0'>⑵ 二字原缺，据四库本补。雍正本、光绪本作鸱陷</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541795_comment'></div></div><br /><a id='poem_sentence_0_541489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541489'>身名未就耕桑废，何日投闲老此湖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_541490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541490'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541490'>弟兄身事各茫然，赖有先人二顷田。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541490'>他日青山映黄发，长如今夜对床眠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541490'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541490_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d974e1e1a5c5488b9c0af77d44859bb0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d974e1e1a5c5488b9c0af77d44859bb0");'><span id='d974e1e1a5c5488b9c0af77d44859bb0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年4？</a>　母病，归乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年7月26日</a>　居家。作品：四友录。<div id='poem_1250219' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250219' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250219?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四友录</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年7月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250219")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250219_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250219'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250219'>语曰：「君子以文会友」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250219_comment'></div>予文会梅溪，有友四人焉，皆佳士也，然各有少疵：罗文性坚刚而贪墨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250219_comment'></div>毛颖工文词，动如人意，而不耐久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250219_comment'></div>楮先生为人洁白，而轻薄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250219_comment'></div>子墨客卿有渐磨之功，而好变白为黑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250219_comment'></div>四友与予文会久矣，予常取其能而不议其疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250219_comment'></div>数年间客上庠，陪俊游，果赖四友之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250219_comment'></div>然予老矣，四友方进未休，他日竹帛间慎毋相忘，子当掩予疵，如予今日之不废子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250219_comment'></div>庚午六月丙寅书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1250219_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年9月</a>　母病卒。作品：青词。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年10月28日</a>　居家，悼亡。作品：十月二十八日母氏劬劳之日也，哀痛中书二十八字。<div id='poem_541512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>十月二十八日母氏劬劳之日也哀痛中书二十八字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年10月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541512")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541512_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541512'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541512'>县弧<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>谩喜生良月，看镜堪嗟已二毛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541512_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541512'>不见双亲空泣血，此生无计报劬劳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541512_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541512'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541512_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_541512'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_541512_0'>⑴ 原作孤，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541512_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>　居家。作品：岩松记。<div id='poem_1250249' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250249' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250249?labeling=true' target='_blank'>岩松记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250249")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250249_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250249'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250249'>野人有以岩松至梅溪者，异质丛生，根衔拳石，茂焉匪孤，森焉匪乔，柏叶桧身而松气象焉，藏参天覆地之意于盈握间，亦草木之英奇者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250249_comment'></div>予颇爱之，植以瓦盆，置之小成室，稽古之暇，寓陶先生郑先生之趣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250249_comment'></div>是日与同舍饮茗谈故事，因共观之，咸有欲得之色，予曰：「有能赏之以言者，予不敢吝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250249_comment'></div>俄篇章争先而并至，皆佳作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250249_comment'></div>予不暇品第之，莫知所赠，因徙至于会趣堂，与八斋之众共之，且告之曰：「诸友讲于斯，食于斯，游息于斯，是松也常在眼焉，奚必几案间然后为吾物耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250249_comment'></div>虽然，是松之意不可不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250249_comment'></div>岩产质松，肖形诸友不凡之姿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250249_comment'></div>青青之色，凌傲霜雪，诸友岁寒之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250249_comment'></div>郁密轮囷，若偃若伸，爪距奋而鳞鬣生，诸友变化之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1250249_comment'></div>今日之观，岂曰玩物而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1250249_comment'></div>唐人之诗曰『勖君青松心』，予于诸友亦云」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1250249_comment'></div>绍兴辛未四月晦日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1250249_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='88701ec183ab4ad788eb4adbe6432916_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("88701ec183ab4ad788eb4adbe6432916");'><span id='88701ec183ab4ad788eb4adbe6432916_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>，41岁</div><div id='88701ec183ab4ad788eb4adbe6432916' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>居母丧，结庐讲学。<br href='/Writing/541528?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哭孟丙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541528")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541528_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541528'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541528'>三岁甜酸学语儿，能来壁下看题诗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541528_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541528'>当时戏发十年问，添我无穷今日悲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541528_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541528'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541528_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_541528'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_541528_0'>⑴ 自注：予戊辰年题西轩壁，令甲乙二子研墨捧砚，孟丙儿戏于侧（原作则，据四库本改）始三岁。予问之曰，汝十年后能诗乎？应曰能。二子顾予而笑，因记之。壬申六月二十四日观旧题时，孟丙死已一月矣，予旧有和韩诗云：学语二（雍正本、光绪本作三）岁儿，笑味生甜酸。盖谓孟丙也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541528_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_541529' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541529' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541529?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541529_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541529'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541529'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541529_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541530?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541531' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541531?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541531_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541531'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541531'>偃蹇衰翁四十馀，梅花溪上结茅庐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541531_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541531'>窗明几净还如旧，不见儿来觅纸书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541531_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541531'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541531_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541532'
