class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541532_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541532'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541532'>偶作吾儿真梦寐，暂来人世误娄罗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541532'>虽然修短由天命，致汝无辜我罪多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541532'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541532_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541533' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541533' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541533?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541533_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541533'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541533'>七年娇姹慰衰翁，回首追思一梦中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541533_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541533'>与汝夙缘如未断，重来当似顾非熊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541533_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541533'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541533_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1250333' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250333' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250333?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭孟丙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250333")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250333_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250333'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250333'>嗟嗟孟丙，吾幼儿也，七岁而亡，吁可悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250333_comment'></div>汝生而眉目分明，神气清秀，骨有伏犀之奇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250333_comment'></div>声音琅琅，语话了了，而世事稍稍能知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250333_comment'></div>吾与朋友讲习，二兄侍立，而汝必随也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250333_comment'></div>吾徒数十人，汝类能识其姓第名字，退而品藻之于其私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250333_comment'></div>吾谓汝早慧如许，他日必未易量，岂意止于斯也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250333_comment'></div>吾之所饮恨者，玩汝之病，救汝之迟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250333_comment'></div>初亦谓汝起止轻健，岂数日之间，遽至弗支也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250333_comment'></div>生于村落，所恨苦者无妙药良医也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1250333_comment'></div>致汝无辜，由我之罪，茹苦抱痛，无穷时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1250333_comment'></div>当汝之死，家祸方稔，而仲兄之势尤危也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1250333_comment'></div>吾方怆惶惊怖，不得尽下殇之礼以葬汝，绕坟三匝以苦汝，情虽钟而恩已亏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1250333_comment'></div>汝今死已百日矣，汝母方获视汝之坟，而吾方获祭汝以词也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1250333_comment'></div>汝昔在襁褓，婆钟爱汝，今祔葬于侧，魂魄必有依也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1250333_comment'></div>汝父母亲戚，朝夕哭泣以思汝，夜常梦寐以见汝，冀汝有再生之期也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1250333_comment'></div>天地鬼神，傥悯汝之横夭，释我之罪愆，使汝复为吾子，以慰莫景之思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1250333_comment'></div>汝或夤缘未断，魂识有知，当随父母以归也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1250333_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赴太学。作品：予自乙丑冬如临安赴补，逮今凡五经矣。是行也，痛慈孝之不见，伤幼儿之早死，登途法然。<div id='poem_541568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>予自乙丑冬如临安赴补逮今凡五往矣是行也痛慈亲之不见伤幼儿之蚤死登途泫然因成是诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541568")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_541568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541568'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541568'>八岁五行役，兹行最感伤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541568'>思亲啼血泪，忆子断刚肠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541568'>游远有遗恨，钟情难遽忘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541568'>离家两夜梦，长绕白岩旁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541568'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_541568_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ed99ce99b1054a2184a7320e39b29925_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ed99ce99b1054a2184a7320e39b29925");'><span id='ed99ce99b1054a2184a7320e39b29925_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>，41岁</div><div id='ed99ce99b1054a2184a7320e39b29925' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　从太学返乡。作品：西征。<div id='poem_541578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西征</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541578")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541578'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541578'>绍兴建元二十二，良月壬午时丁未。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541578'>王家辞弟游帝都<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作京）</span>，出门满眼思亲泪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541578'>鹡鸰送我过原隰，朋友携尊宿萧寺。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541578'>朝离黄塘惜分别，莫宿青山嗟独自。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541578'>初心满拟游雁山，行止非人辄乖异。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541578'>黄岩留连越三宿，故旧过从日沈醉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541578'>郑生伴我千里行，近世人无此风义。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541578'>皇华亭上一回首，陡觉眉头起乡思。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541578'>西江十里浮桥边，把酒登楼吟拥鼻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_541578'>山行初逢建子月，入眼梅花已春意。<div id='poem_sentence_9_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_541578'>前观三渡觉非旧，下视两滩真可畏。<div id='poem_sentence_10_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_541578'>渡头仙人还笑我，髭须如棘犹名利。<div id='poem_sentence_11_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_541578'>欲入天台观石桥，行来匆匆未能遂。<div id='poem_sentence_12_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_541578'>途中邂逅张老丞<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：廷玉。）</span>，十五年前乐清尉。<div id='poem_sentence_13_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_541578'>自嗟吾非沈谢辈，面目从来苦难记。<div id='poem_sentence_14_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_541578'>飞泉枕上梦成魔，达旦思家何曾睡。<div id='poem_sentence_15_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_541578'>细雨濛濛入关岭，旅邸重寻旧题字。<div id='poem_sentence_16_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_541578'>雨脚微收过天姥，洗出峰峦叠苍翠。<div id='poem_sentence_17_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_541578'>刘阮祠荒土犹赤，溪山真是神仙地。<div id='poem_sentence_18_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_541578'>道旁石现小金仙，传舍荒凉谁废置。<div id='poem_sentence_19_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_541578'>柘溪竹染儿女痕，石岭松含栋梁器。<div id='poem_sentence_20_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_541578'>路入南明观石佛，楼阁岧峣更深邃。<div id='poem_sentence_21_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_541578'>八年行役两来游，岩上题诗记前事。<div id='poem_sentence_22_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_541578'>乘兴剡溪寻故人，久别相逢杂悲喜。<div id='poem_sentence_23_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_541578'>义风吹水送行舟，越国江山满瞻视。<div id='poem_sentence_24_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_541578'>十四岁娥孝且烈，三百里湖明更媚。<div id='poem_sentence_25_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_541578'>千岩竞秀壑争流，终日贪看趣遥寄。<div id='poem_sentence_26_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_541578'>西兴渡口声如雷，银浪崔嵬魄惊悸。<div id='poem_sentence_27_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_541578'>江神为我风色平，天阙煌煌瞻象魏。<div id='poem_sentence_28_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_541578'>贤关访旧话酸辛，更食齑盐旧滋味。<div id='poem_sentence_29_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_541578'>学官欲以职事留，自愧非才力辞避。<div id='poem_sentence_30_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_541578'>观台云物端可书，宫线初长日南至。<div id='poem_sentence_31_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_541578'>龙山僦舍观大礼，仪仗森然典文备。<div id='poem_sentence_32_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_541578'>人臣贵盛古今无，秦公父子俱为使。<div id='poem_sentence_33_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_541578'>景灵告谢乐声回，鹓鹭花枝侈君赐。<div id='poem_sentence_34_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_541578'>西游连日睹天颜，和气氤氲散憔悴。<div id='poem_sentence_35_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_541578'>岁云莫矣却归来，捉笔书为于役志<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《梅溪先生文集》卷五）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_36_541578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_541578'></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_541578_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='20690c09967b46a98077305fff043586_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("20690c09967b46a98077305fff043586");'><span id='20690c09967b46a98077305fff043586_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1156')">1153-1156年</a>，42-45岁</div><div id='20690c09967b46a98077305fff043586' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年8月2日</a>　离开剡溪返乡途中。作品：白岩遇水。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年8月</a>　返回左原，结庐讲学，改梅溪书馆为梅溪书院。作品：书院挂额筵雅会也戏集诸堂轩斋名作诗。<div id='poem_541641' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541641' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541641?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书院挂额展筵雅会也戏集诸堂轩斋名作诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541641")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_541641_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541641'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541641'>黉馆名初挂，银钩势欲翻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541641'>人才蕴秀异，学业扣渊源。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541641'>俊彦方群集，文章可细论。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541641'>辉声迈前辈，擢秀蔼诸孙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541641'>心友居兰室，天香满桂轩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541641'>兹为学者富，难与俗流言。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541641'>恢义高风倡，同襟旧好敦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541641'>池中神鲤足，一一上龙门。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541641'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_541641_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年9月12日</a>　居家讲学。作品：九月十二日夜独步梅溪玩月人迹悄然秋色满眼微风不懂岩桂自香初不劳思偶得四句盖心境中静时语也归小成室对短灯靓素纸书之。<div id='poem_541560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九月十二夜独步梅溪玩月人迹悄然秋色满眼微风不动岩桂自香初不劳思偶得四句盖心境中静时语也归小成室对短灯檠索纸书之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年9月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541560")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541560'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541560'>独步溪头夜初寂，扫空尘念心清凉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541560'>月明眼底见秋色，境静鼻根闻桂香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541560'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541560_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　王十朋岳父贾如讷与夫人陈氏合葬于左原。作品：贾府君行状。<div id='poem_1250314' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250314' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250314?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贾府君行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250314")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250314_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250314'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250314'>公讳如讷，字元辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250314_comment'></div>其先福州长溪人，五世祖徙温之乐清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250314_comment'></div>曾祖皓、祖靖、父奭，皆有潜德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250314_comment'></div>公温雅恺悌，持重寡言，为儿时嶷若成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250314_comment'></div>十二岁而孤，事后母至孝，抚育弟娣恩意均壹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250314_comment'></div>母病，涕泣尝药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250314_comment'></div>及卒，执丧如礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250314_comment'></div>伯母钱性严，子侄有过必痛绳之，公善承顺，未尝忤意，在诸子中最以谨厚称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250314_comment'></div>初，伯父奕以弦诵先里闬，从兄弟愚、如晦俱美才，有声庠序间，公尤嗜学，每谓弟如石、如规曰：「吾二兄才名如许，若等可不自勉耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1250314_comment'></div>以身率之，故二弟皆力学，能自立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1250314_comment'></div>如规既冠，学益进，公勉其游太学，且躬任其家事，厚资给之，务成其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1250314_comment'></div>及举进士，捷音至，时兄如晦同战艺，公意其俱中，喜甚，既而闻其不利，郁郁不乐，贺者方集，公却之曰：「吾兄亲老，方籍此以慰其意，今见黜，何贺我为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1250314_comment'></div>人服其不私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1250314_comment'></div>如规今慰建昌军广昌县，以德誉取重缙绅，公之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1250314_comment'></div>公善治家，井井有法，不务兼并，而生产日肥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1250314_comment'></div>性仁慈，尤睦宗族，见贫者心悯之，常发廪以济，每言：「彼吾宗也，吾忍独温饱也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1250314_comment'></div>有尤窘者四族人，以膏腴三十亩赈之，仍给谷暨牛，资其播殖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1250314_comment'></div>又捐百亩饭僧徒之往来者，及分惠里人之寠者，凡割田二顷馀，而金谷之惠叵计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1250314_comment'></div>谒丐踵门，必周恤之，至解衣以赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1250314_comment'></div>其敦宗好施盖天性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1250314_comment'></div>乡人燕其宗，耻以贫贱者与，公曰：「是岂两姓耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1250314_comment'></div>每家宴，合疏近长幼贫富均礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1250314_comment'></div>舅氏家不振，悉力瞻之，岁时登其门，省事如父母，去必感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1250314_comment'></div>舅卒，厚礼以葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1250314_comment'></div>公素友爱兄弟，异居非其志，当析财，命宗人区处，未尝顾视，务推逊以化媮俗，季感其德，复义聚至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1250314_comment'></div>乐教子弟，屡延致名儒，厚其礼，终始周旋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1250314_comment'></div>喜宾客，馆无虚日，雅不好饮，遇宾醉则为之极欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1250314_comment'></div>敦尚礼法，遇人无厚薄必尽恭，泛爱乡党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1250314_comment'></div>至所交必择长者，寡嗜欲，不好杀，喜与释子游谈无生之理，务忘身世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1250314_comment'></div>不幸婴痼疾，仁而不寿，享年才四十有二，以建炎三年五月九日卒，遗言「有私负者悉弃之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1250314_comment'></div>远近闻讣，无不涕泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1250314_comment'></div>娶同邑陈氏，处士景芳之女，姿婉淑，奉姑以孝谨称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1250314_comment'></div>始奁具颇厚，公喜周急而夫人不吝，故公得以私田活其宗数百指，阴德在人为多，盖夫人之助云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1250314_comment'></div>后公六年而卒，年四十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1250314_comment'></div>男一人，曰循以，业进士，克守家训，与季父同居几三十年，服劳不惮，乡里难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1250314_comment'></div>女一人，归表侄王某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1250314_comment'></div>孙二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1250314_comment'></div>公与夫人丧久在殡，弟县慰君尝言：「吾兄嫂事吾母尽孝，吾当择地改葬吾母，以兄嫂祔焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1250314_comment'></div>屡以卜，后得邑之左原，其岗维吉，躬治坟茔以奉窀穸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1250314_comment'></div>绍兴癸酉秋，循似泣谓某曰：「吾将以冬十一月十有七日合葬吾父母，欲丐铭大手笔以发其幽光，子盍状之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1250314_comment'></div>某不佞，获以通家子自幼登公门，荷知遇不浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1250314_comment'></div>及公殁，又辱为子婿，知隐德为详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1250314_comment'></div>尝访遗事于故老，咸曰：「公仁者也，今无是人矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1250314_comment'></div>某遂撰次所闻，俟贤而有文者书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1250314_comment'></div>谨状<span class='inlineComment2'>（《梅溪先生文集》卷二○。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1250314_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1250314'>循似：前文作「循以」，未知孰是。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1250314_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　居家执教梅溪书院。作品：林下十二子诗。纳凉偶得。<div id='poem_541655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541655' class='poemTitle class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541667")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541667'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541667'>东园小小花木稀，西园廓廓规模奇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541667'>更约南园好事人，酒盏诗篇日相续。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541710'>芹芳泮水声蜚早，花满河阳迹到稀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541710'>方外客携因果去，道旁人汲义泉归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541710'>柳川池馆规模壮，一夕花妖世已非<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《梅溪先生文集》卷七）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541710'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_541710_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　家居讲授，乐清万叔永葬于岐山之阴，十朋作行状。作品：东平万府君行状。<div id='poem_1250312' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250312' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250312?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东平万府君行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250312")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250312_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250312'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250312'>君讳世延，字叔永，世为温之乐清人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250312_comment'></div>曾大父惟监、大父周、父鸿，皆晦德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250312_comment'></div>君幼警悟，敏记诵，初属文思捷而佳，为师友所奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250312_comment'></div>年十四而孤，奉母谨甚，处家事若成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250312_comment'></div>舍法中游郡庠，业修行饬，蔚为善士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250312_comment'></div>宣和间邑大夫兴乡校，以乡先生郑君邦彦主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250312_comment'></div>郑学术渊粹，为时名儒，从之游者以百数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250312_comment'></div>君一日谒同志，会其课诸生，戏即其题涉笔而就，郑见之抚几叹曰：「之人词藻如是，一第唾手取尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250312_comment'></div>然君以兄弟终鲜，志颛甘旨，讫不事进取，抱才不试，乡人惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1250312_comment'></div>性宽博，与物无忤，尤善宗族，每先其急难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1250312_comment'></div>遇长幼慈爱均壹，无纤芥嫌隙，族众多间有违言，君周旋其间，开释以理，众皆愧服，协比如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1250312_comment'></div>由是阖族内外咸钦而爱之，称为长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1250312_comment'></div>善治生，蓄而能散，亲故有不振者，每纲纪其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1250312_comment'></div>其弟子有美质，困不能自业，给饮食师资费以教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1250312_comment'></div>处女贫无以归，躬为择配，奁而遣者凡数人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1250312_comment'></div>居之左右细民寠族，资衣食埋葬者数十家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1250312_comment'></div>缁素叩门，随所谒而获者叵计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1250312_comment'></div>岁凶廪饥，每为富室倡，敕具以馆，宾席无虚日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1250312_comment'></div>笃于教子，尝葺屋数楹，积书其间，厚礼以致名师，训督点窜之劳，率分其半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1250312_comment'></div>长子庚最美才，始冠游太学，君勉之以诗曰：「莫放山亏篑，终教井及泉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1250312_comment'></div>庚益自励，果优中考选，连预荐书，屡为多士先，声誉籍籍，用上舍免省登进士科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1250312_comment'></div>次子庠亦以妙龄预乡贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1250312_comment'></div>万氏以弦诵先里闬，历四世，儒冠益盛，业贤关、举进士者数人，登科第自庚始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1250312_comment'></div>乐清自舍法罢，阅二十年无举于乡者，里巷靳之，邑人复取乡贡自庠始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1250312_comment'></div>先是，监察御史睢阳李君蔼扈驾南巡，闻君有乡誉，访其居，名其轩曰「必大」，且赋诗极言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1250312_comment'></div>至是二子俱有成，人以为荣，咸谓君种德乐教之报，且嘉李之先知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1250312_comment'></div>君夙有喘疾，晚岁弥剧，濒死语不乱，巍坐正色而卒，实绍兴甲戌十月二十有三日也，年五十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1250312_comment'></div>乡里闻讣，无不伤嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1250312_comment'></div>初娶孙氏，先君二十四年而卒，继室以赵氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1250312_comment'></div>子六人：庚，左迪功郎、处州缙州缙云慰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1250312_comment'></div>次曰庠，曰廙，曰廓，曰庶，曰唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1250312_comment'></div>孙男三，女二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1250312_comment'></div>庚与庠既以儒学名家，馀皆服义方，其进未量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1250312_comment'></div>乡人以君有阴德，且多男子，比之燕山窦氏，恨其不足于寿，不获尽见云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1250312_comment'></div>君仁而好施，志于济众者未艾也，尝割膏腴三十亩，储其入以济亲戚之贫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1250312_comment'></div>死之岁，语诸子曰：「吾为是恨未广，自是而后，宜资其人，岁一易之，庶几悉周」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1250312_comment'></div>且枚举其所当与者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1250312_comment'></div>家之西距大江，实为要津，势湍而恶，涉者病之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1250312_comment'></div>君叔祖东平先生始倾家资，跨江为桥，济人于险，垂六十年往来蒙其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1250312_comment'></div>俄一夕烬于火，东平子主簿君欲新之，未遂而卒，君毅然以桥为任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1250312_comment'></div>然事艰役钜，既捐己资以半其费，又经营其馀于乡党间以佐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1250312_comment'></div>桥成有日矣，而君卧病弥岁，属纩语不及他，顾谓诸子：「吾以桥累若等矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1250312_comment'></div>诸子涕泣请继志，颔而瞑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1250312_comment'></div>君虽早厌场屋，未尝废书，每开卷意有所会，必标识以谨不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1250312_comment'></div>所为诗文虽不多，皆平淡造理，峻洁可爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1250312_comment'></div>尤属意于简翰，虽贻子弟，不率然作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1250312_comment'></div>卒之又明年，诸孤卜以春正月十有九日葬于岐山之阴，泣血相谓曰：「吾父以善人君子称于乡，其潜德有足书者，将乞铭于荐绅先生以永厥垂，宜得知其详者状而授之，庶乎其不诬」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1250312_comment'></div>以属某，某万出也，每登门辱顾为厚，且与庚同舍上庠，又获与诸子游，盖知其详而不诬者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1250312_comment'></div>虽芜陋，其何敢辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1250312_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1250312_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　居家讲授。作品：觅海棠。札上人许赠山丹花且云此花三月尽开俟蕊移去至上巳日以诗索之。<div id='poem_541697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>觅海棠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541697")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_541697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541697'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541697'>好事高人重海棠，两株分植舫斋旁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541697'>恰当燕子来时放，更向禅房深处芳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541697'>道眼想应怜不俗，痴人何苦恨无香。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541697'>梅溪野叟曾经眼，欲觅一根栽草堂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541697'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_541697_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>札上人许赠山丹花且云此花三月尽开俟蕊成移去至上巳日以诗索之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541699")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_541699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541699'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541699'>人间花木眼曾经，未识兹花状与名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541699'>丹却青山暮春色，续他红树堕时英。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541699'>梅溪野老栽成癖，莲社高人诺不轻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541699'>小小园林绿将暗，早移芳蕊看敷荣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541699'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_541699_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年3月</a>　居家讲授，访寿昌寺之净慧法师，其居于舫斋。作品：舫斋记。<div id='poem_1250253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250253?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舫斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250253")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250253_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250253'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250253'>知进而不知退者，非特缙绅坐斯患也，虽出世之士亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250253_comment'></div>佛之徒本逃名晦身，若无意于世者，然世之善知识，其道学有馀，可以淑诸人，应缘而出，有不能自已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250253_comment'></div>其间好进之徒怵于利欲，往往贿以求进，老而不休，讼而不去者，盖纷如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250253_comment'></div>惟昌寿净慧师则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250253_comment'></div>师少游锡异方，潜心佛陇，志识学问出人一头，业成而还，为缁林所推服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250253_comment'></div>始传教于永嘉之开元，再传于福圣，既而以疾求还故山，住寿昌教院，凡若干载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250253_comment'></div>年愈尊，德愈隆，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1250253", 1250253, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>道俗</span>愈归重，然即未尝一日不以退居养老为怀，世缘挽之而莫能自脱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250253_comment'></div>某与师有二十年之旧，一日访师，而师已获遂其退老之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250253_comment'></div>居所谓舫斋者，欣然见颜色间，指是斋谓某曰：「子为我记之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1250253_comment'></div>某曰：「师昔尝乘无量大法舫，游无边大海中，出大誓愿力，济百亿万大众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1250253_comment'></div>今兹舫也，其形模似矣，然而閤焉而不能浮，静焉而不能济，隘焉而不能容，师独善其身可也，如众生何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1250253_comment'></div>师笑曰：「吾师乘法舫而游，人以为无量也，吾不知其为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1250253_comment'></div>今吾即是舫以居也，人以为不能容也，吾不知其为小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1250253_comment'></div>且夫迹有去住而道无去住，形有小大而法无小大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1250253_comment'></div>身之进退迹也，舫之大小形也，吾出而化亿万众于人世间者，以无形之舫，行无量之法尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1250253_comment'></div>退而寄老病之身于故庐者，假有形之舫，藏无量之法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1250253_comment'></div>将使夫闻而化者，无贪于得，无嗔于不得，无痴于必求，其所欲得又焉有贿而求进、老而不休、讼而不去也，如子之所谓乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1250253_comment'></div>然则，吾之退也未尝无教化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1250253_comment'></div>兹舫虽小，孰谓其非无量无边法具乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1250253_comment'></div>某愧其言，退而记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1250253_comment'></div>绍兴乙亥三月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1250253_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　居家讲授，前往止斋拜望宝印大师。作品：潜涧严闍黎塔铭。<div id='poem_1250316' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250316' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250316?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潜涧严阇梨塔铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250316")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250316_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250316'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250316'>师讳处严，字伯威，姓贾氏，温州乐清人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250316_comment'></div>父靖，居乡以长者称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250316_comment'></div>母万，方娠，一夕梦黑龙自天跃而下，俄化为道人入其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250316_comment'></div>及产，师有异相，幼警悟不凡，经史过目辄成诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250316_comment'></div>舅东平先生规，邑之名儒也，试以对，随口应答，大奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250316_comment'></div>少长，忽不茹荤，母强之，卒不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250316_comment'></div>一日游精舍，归白其母曰：「儿蔬食居俗非所宜，愿出家学佛，惟夫人割爱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250316_comment'></div>遂往里之明庆院礼僧知性为师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250316_comment'></div>既落发受具，游历郡刹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1250316_comment'></div>初学律，未几习天台教观，慨然叹曰：「吾邦僻在海隅，见闻不广」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1250316_comment'></div>遂之钱塘，依南屏臻公，听天台大部，明《法华》诸经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1250316_comment'></div>时学者尚编录，务相诘难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1250316_comment'></div>师听法罢，端然默坐，同辈问之，发明师说，了无遗误，因谓之曰：「文字分别，驰骋法相，吾不能为」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1250316_comment'></div>遂远游禅林，访先辈老宿，叩击玄旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1250316_comment'></div>师志节高，学识超迈，杖锡所至，道眼相契为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1250316_comment'></div>会有以座首命之者，师曰：「吾宅心名利外，冀逍遥自适，讵能为人役耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1250316_comment'></div>于是西游帝都，观伊洛南，周旋江淮间，凡名山水、丛林巨刹，靡不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1250316_comment'></div>时道潜、思聪二僧与东坡居士游，声名籍甚，咸与师善，数以篇章往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1250316_comment'></div>师博学，诗文尤典重，且工书，有晋宋法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1250316_comment'></div>或劝以所作谒缙绅求知己，师笑曰：「古之桑门上首与士大夫游，非求之也，道自合焉尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1250316_comment'></div>故终身不以一字干谒，识者高之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1250316_comment'></div>元祐间还永嘉，寓净光、大云、开元诸寺，其徒翕然归之，扣门请益者屦相蹑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1250316_comment'></div>师训以本业外，复以诗书子史导之，凡经指授者咸见头角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1250316_comment'></div>时开元建护国天王殿，命师作记，文辞雄伟，太守范公见之，称叹良久，命刻石行于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1250316_comment'></div>元符初归故山，诛茅结芦，循除蓄流，自号潜涧，赋诗鼓琴以自娱，有古人林下风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1250316_comment'></div>师有辞辨，长于讲释，乡里巨室欲屈师讲经，莫能致，因具法筵，集广众，预设巍座，俟师至，与众迫之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1250316_comment'></div>师匆遽就席，阐扬舆旨，缘饰以文，音吐鸿亮，听者惊悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1250316_comment'></div>明庆自创业几七百年，无文迹可考，师首为撰记并书之，时称二绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1250316_comment'></div>郡守张公平闻其名，以礼致之，躬受《楞严》大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1250316_comment'></div>初以僧正命师，又命主禅席，皆力辞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1250316_comment'></div>每诣府，手提一笠，未尝肩舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1250316_comment'></div>人以师为府座所厚，因属以事，师正色峻拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1250316_comment'></div>府政有不便于民者，委曲以告，守改容听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1250316_comment'></div>瑞安令吕公勤自号湖海道人，邂逅师，喜甚，与俱还邑，筑庵于厅治后园，命师居之，为留三宿而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1250316_comment'></div>邑令丁公湛每访师谈道，终日忘返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1250316_comment'></div>晚景绝人事，惟精修净业，喜讽诵《楞严》、《圆觉》、《维摩》、《光明》、《法华》等经，精熟如流，静夜孤坐，焚香暗诵，琅琅之声出于林表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1250316_comment'></div>尝手书《法华》、《光明》二经以报母德，又书《华严经》八十卷，首末不懈，字法益工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1250316_comment'></div>弟子宗要游学姑苏，俄以书督其归，未几师得疾遽终，政和壬辰正月二十日也，享年五十四，僧腊三十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1250316_comment'></div>至三月，阇维得舍利数百颗，明莹如珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1250316_comment'></div>明年九月，植塔于故庐之后，以遗骨并舍利葬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1250316_comment'></div>师于佛学无不通晓，尤深于禅，而接物以教，故以阇梨著名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1250316_comment'></div>平生制述甚多，藁随毁失，圆寂后弟子收拾遗文，编成二卷，人有得其片纸皆宝藏之，其文翰见重于人如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1250316_comment'></div>弟子宗要师号宝印，传天台教，住永嘉之妙果，克世其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1250316_comment'></div>法孙德纯亦传法于郡之龙翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1250316_comment'></div>某大母氏师之同母姊也，宝印师盖某之叔父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1250316_comment'></div>师殁之岁而某始生，自儿时稔闻德名，恨不迨见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1250316_comment'></div>今四十馀载矣，始获以叔父之命铭师之塔，不敢以鄙陋辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1250316_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_1250316'>师之道，儒律禅教，咸臻其要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1250316_comment'></div>师之技，歌诗文翰，咸极其致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1250316_comment'></div>师之节，公卿大夫，不屈而谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1250316_comment'></div>师之训，子传教观，孙传心印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1250316_comment'></div>师之庐，左琴右书，山高涧迂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1250316_comment'></div>师之塔，明珠遗骨，千古不灭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1250316_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　居家讲授，闻秦桧已死，遂决定备考，作别大师。作品：次韵宝印叔题止斋三绝。<div id='poem_541459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵宝印叔题止庵三绝<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541459")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541459'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541459'>凿石依山作小庵，花香入座月侵檐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541459'>虽然眼界无多地，解使人天竞耸瞻。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541460?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541460'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541460_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541460'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541460_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541461' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541461' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541461?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541461_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541461'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541461'>晚学无由识道真，前贤未许继芳尘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541461'>道从何进从何止，敢叩无为绝学人。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年1月4日</a>　孙先觉母亲八十大寿，作诗以贺。作品：孙先觉母大人正月四日生时年八十。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　居家，开书会于郭路明庆寺。作品：明庆忏院上方地爽而幽盖精蓝之胜也予因会友託迹于其间一日探囊中得石刻诗一本乃王瞻叔国愽 先生题台人秀野堂也摹写景物颇类于此因置之壁间意有感触遂借其韵。<div id='poem_541715' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541715' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541715?labeling=true' target='_blank'>明庆忏院上方地爽而幽盖精蓝<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>之胜也予因会友托迹于其间一日探囊中得石刻诗一本乃王瞻叔国博先生题台人秀野堂也摹写景物颇类于此因置之壁间意有感触遂借其韵<span class='inlineComment2'>（二月二十五日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_541715_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_541715_0'>① 原作篮，据雍正本、光绪本改</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541715'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541715'>下帷<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>精舍远尘繁，境静心清事不关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541715'>案上忘机有黄卷，眼中得趣是青山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541715'>林泉欲共高僧老，事业未容吾辈闲。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541715'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_541715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_541715'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_541715_0'>⑴ 原作惟，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541715_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年10月1日</a>　居家。作品：孟夏十有一日时雨初霁晨登高阁极目四望烟销日出气象一新复用前韵。<div id='poem_541726' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541726' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541726?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孟夏十有一日时雨初霁晨登高阁极目四望烟锁日出气象一新复用前韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年10月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541726")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541726_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541726'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541726'>蝶梦惊回听残雨，鸟声唤起欣初晴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541726'>梵宫烟火带馀湿，黉舍几席生微清。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541726'>披衣登阁忽四顾，顿觉远目增双明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541726'>樵渔欸乃雾中出，舟楫荡漾田间行。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541726'>清和节物满眼界，柳垂暗绿花含情。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541726'>窗明几净日渐永，天开地廓阴不争。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541726'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_541726_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ad09e74de4ec41b3ac9c05f96ce562b3_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>，48岁</div><div id='ad09e74de4ec41b3ac9c05f96ce562b3' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>解官归家,游雁荡山。作品：题双峰资深堂。宿灵岩赠长老敏行。<div id='poem_542101' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542101' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542101?labeling=true' ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542101")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_542101_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_sentence_2_542101_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_542102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542102?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542102'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542102'>我到双峰寻宝月，为留一宿话资深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_542103_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542103'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542103'>雁山门户此中入，南北两峰相对尖。<div id='poem_title_542104_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542104'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542104'>千峰已见见双峰，瓯越山川在眼中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542104'>吾祖吹箫定何所，会须乘鹤访遗风<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：双峰之西南，亦有吹箫峰。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542104'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_542104_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_542105' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542105' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542105?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_542105_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542105'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542105'>堂名石刻两俱存，令我深怀旧长官。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542105'>学道资深更深处，居安能使庶民安<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542105'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_542105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_542105'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_542105_0'>⑴ 自注：周开祖昔令乐清。有遗爱堂，名乃开祖所命。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_542105_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_542106' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542106' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542106?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿灵岩赠长老敏行</a><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　回到乐清左原，遇旱灾。作品：种蔬。家食遇欠，有饭不足之忧，妻擎相勉以固穷，因录其语。<div id='poem_542285' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542285' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542285?labeling=true' target='_blank'>种蔬</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542285")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_542285_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542285'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542285'>归来日弹铗，食无肉与鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542285'>却将种花地，町畦毓嘉蔬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542285'>骄阳每抱瓮，时雨亲荷锄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542285'>青青有生意，令我颜色舒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542285'>宁忧馑与饥，亦有瓶中储。<div id='poem_sentence_4_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_542285'>前身老阇梨<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_6_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_542285'>蠹书仍食蔬，苦淡味有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_542285'>洗我腥膻肠<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，襟宇生清虚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_542285'>岂惟陶渊明，吾亦爱吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_11_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_542285'>荒园涉成趣，枯藤当安舆。<div id='poem_sentence_12_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_542285'>困枕案头卷，饥著盘中菹。<div id='poem_sentence_13_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_542285'>孔门陈蔡色，借问何如予。<div id='poem_sentence_14_542285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　闲居家乡，经春荒。作品：家食遇歉,有饭不足之忧,妻擎
相勉以固穷,因录其语。<div id='poem_542350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>家食遇歉有饭不足之忧妻孥<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_2_542350'>广文富才名，官冷饭不足。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542350'>少陵老风骚，橡栗拾山谷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542350'>嗟予何为者，处世真碌碌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_542350'>谋生一何拙，甔石无储蓄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_542350'>三年两去国，囊橐罄水陆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_542350'>还家索租苗，不了腊与伏。<div id='poem_sentence_7_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_542350'>乡邻苟不救，定恐填沟渎。<div id='poem_sentence_11_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_542350'>家藏千卷书，父子忍饥读。<div id='poem_sentence_12_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_542350'>一字不堪煮，何以充我腹。<div id='poem_sentence_13_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_542350'>细君笑谓我，子命难食肉。<div id='poem_sentence_14_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_542350'>子耕我当耘，固穷待秋熟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_542350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_542350'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_542350_0'>⑴ 雍正本、光绪本作祲</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_542350_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年5月</a>　集英殿修撰知饶州。作品：孝宗皇帝除王十朋为集英殿修撰，起知饶州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='63cfd834bf9943178c48bdfd7f9e8b9c_label'><a href='javascript: -----title
温州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4079b1368ee141eeb7d0ea8524a1eefd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4079b1368ee141eeb7d0ea8524a1eefd");'><span id='4079b1368ee141eeb7d0ea8524a1eefd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>，26岁</div><div id='4079b1368ee141eeb7d0ea8524a1eefd' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在温州江心寺学习，为江心寺钻鞋乐“云潮”名联。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>就读温州江心寺，投书请谒于太守李端明。作品：上太守李端明书。<div id='poem_1249936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249936?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上太守李端明</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249936")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249936'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249936'>某尝读前史，窃知李氏为天下甲门，世生大贤，角立杰出，皆天人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249936_comment'></div>自昔周柱下史先天地而生，指木为姓，博古知今，而道德为吾圣人之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249936_comment'></div>东都太尉禀元精之气，正色在列，杀身成仁，而节义为人臣之冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249936_comment'></div>唐翰林应长庚之梦，世号谪仙人，立马万言，而文章为天下之法，孰谓其非天人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249936_comment'></div>其间又有以声名自高，而天下有被其收接者，如登龙门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249936_comment'></div>隐居求志，而天下望其出仕者，如睹景星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249936_comment'></div>至若出秉旄钺，如临淮之元勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249936_comment'></div>入总台衡，如卫公之风采者，皆卓然为一代之名臣，中兴之贤佐，其风流馀韵，足以起万世之耸慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249936_comment'></div>某故曰李氏天下之甲门，而数公者真天人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249936_comment'></div>迨我国朝二百年间，宗工钜儒，背项相望，而李氏之门最号得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249936_comment'></div>有若文靖公在咸平、景德间，公忠直亮，深虑远识，尝戒王文正公与北虏和亲之议，断然有先见之明，天下至今称为贤相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249936_comment'></div>有若文定公在天禧、乾兴间，慷慨立朝，义形于色，尝伸救寇莱公之祸，以手板击奸邪，天下至今目为正人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249936_comment'></div>有若紫薇舍人在熙宁间，居代言之任，力持风裁，虽贬黜而气不挠，与苏、宋齐名，天下至今有三舍人之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249936_comment'></div>有若大丞相在政和间危言谠论，耸动四方，及重华受禅之际，垂绅正笏，不动声气而大议决，天下至今赖为社稷臣，而苍生犹冀其复起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249936_comment'></div>有若尚书公当靖康之难，得主辱臣死之义，力抗腥膻，碎首裂额而愤骂不绝，英烈言言，与赫日秋霜争严，艰难以来一人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249936_comment'></div>天下至今称为烈丈夫，而知与不知莫不为之流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249936_comment'></div>仰惟明公以英伟之才，刚方之气，挺生华裔，为当世羽仪，被遇三朝，终始一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249936_comment'></div>乃者上方兴衰拨乱，任贤使能，日不暇给，起明公于均逸中，付以喉舌之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249936_comment'></div>公卿大夫相与贺于朝，韦带布衣相与贺于下，咸谓明公体道德如柱下史，尚节义如汉太尉，工文章如唐翰林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249936_comment'></div>立天子前，披陈利害，论列可否，在廷竦慄，明公之谏诤，固不在谏议勃之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249936_comment'></div>屡典名藩，皆著声绩，奸赃望风解绶而去，明公之威声固不在河南尹之下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249936_comment'></div>至如临淮、卫公之勋烈，文靖、文定之事业，皆明公之所优为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1249936_comment'></div>诗人诵召虎曰：「惟其有之，是以似之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1249936_comment'></div>然则，明公岂非所谓天人者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1249936_comment'></div>然朝廷方视明公之出处以为安危之系，天下方视明公之进退以为治乱之分，夷狄问明公之安否而为之叛服，奸邪伺明公之行藏而为之喜惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1249936_comment'></div>舆议皆谓明公匪朝伊夕，正台鼎之司，慰苍生之望，中兴之功，指日可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1249936_comment'></div>今乃力辞柄任，出牧侯藩，虽一方得卧治之贤，而天下郁具瞻之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1249936_comment'></div>窃料明公固难久屈于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1249936_comment'></div>某蓬荜一贱生尔，自总角闻先生长者称颂明公盛德伟望，殆非一日，第恨生居遐陬，自处卑贱，邈无进见之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1249936_comment'></div>今幸明公父母吾桑梓之邦，适符夙昔景慕企仰之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1249936_comment'></div>比者千骑入境，道由僻邑，而某遂得与田夫野老奔走争先，瞻望于车尘马足间，已足少偿素愿矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1249936_comment'></div>然未获进拜黄堂，亲承謦咳之馀，少窥大人君子之高致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1249936_comment'></div>不日明公入秉洪钧，则某于此时当抱无穷之恨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1249936_comment'></div>是以不介于人，不谋于龟，朝斋而裁书，莫沐而修刺，曳裾麾戟，冀一瞻芝宇，退当誇大，自谓今日得见天人也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1249936_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0f370b788cf7482ebfb2d8cb70dc8bc3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0f370b788cf7482ebfb2d8cb70dc8bc3");'><span id='0f370b788cf7482ebfb2d8cb70dc8bc3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>，34岁</div><div id='0f370b788cf7482ebfb2d8cb70dc8bc3' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: id='poem_sentence_1_541761'>初冬天气佳，雁归山未寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541761'>有日照幽谷，无云翳层峦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541761'>入境见祥云<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：祥云峰。）</span>，振衣登马鞍<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：马鞍岭。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541761'>瀑水飞玉龙<span id='poem_sentence_5_541761'>石柱屹天外<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：天柱峰。）</span>，卓笔书云端<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：卓笔峰。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541761'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_541761", 541761, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>灵峰</span>观石室，杖屦穿巑岏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541761'>山禽知我来，好音若相欢<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541761'>群峰列春笋，丹青状尤难<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：灵峰新创丹青阁。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_541761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_541761'>行色愧匆匆，更约它时看。<div id='poem_sentence_9_541761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_541761'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_541761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_541761'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_541761_0'>⑴ 自注：登罗汉洞，有禽鸣绝顶，声极可爱。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541761_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0b4e2e433da64547b5f7903f38ca4a39_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0b4e2e433da64547b5f7903f38ca4a39");'><span id='0b4e2e433da64547b5f7903f38ca4a39_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，50岁</div><div id='0b4e2e433da64547b5f7903f38ca4a39' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>去国回乡，旧友林明仲迎接十朋至温州城西林明仲别院，留居一个月。作品：右赠明仲。右赠诸公。<br /></div>

绍兴

id='poem_content_541436'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541436'>土木涂金巧逼真，总随浮幻化埃尘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541436'>何人著意镌山骨，长现金刚不坏身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541436'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541436_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541438?labeling=true' "poem_title_541438")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_541438_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541438'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541438'>恸哭无寻处，投江竟得尸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541438'>风高烈女传，名重外孙碑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541438'>荒草没孤冢，洪涛舂古祠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541438'>怀沙为谁死，翻愧是男儿。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541438'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_541438_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　赴补太学，游绍兴。作品：过鉴湖。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='48539e3197404e41aa81b03a6b9c4853_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("48539e3197404e41aa81b03a6b9c4853");'><span id='48539e3197404e41aa81b03a6b9c4853_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>，42岁</div><div id='48539e3197404e41aa81b03a6b9c4853' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年3月</a>　应太学同舍周德远要求，前往剡溪书院任教。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年3月25日</a>　剡溪讲学。作品：葵酉三月二十五日至剡溪旅舍观曹梦良题壁有撩我思家第一篇之句业离家半月亦尝作诗因次其韵。<div id='poem_541579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541579?labeling=true' target='_blank'>癸酉三月二十五日至剡溪旅舍观曹梦良题壁有撩我思家第一篇之句仆离家半月亦未尝作诗因次其韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年3月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541579")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541579_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541579'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541579'>客舍那堪闻杜鹃，梦魂惊断竟无眠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541579'>定知此境撩乡思，我亦曾非第二篇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541579'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541579_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　剡溪讲学，作品：渊源堂记。<div id='poem_1250251' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250251?labeling=true' target='_blank'>渊源堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250251")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250251_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250251'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250251'>先儒孟子有言曰：「君子深造之以道，欲其自得之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250251_comment'></div>自得之则居之安，居之安则资之深，资之深则取之左右逢其源，故君子欲其自得之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250251_comment'></div>说者因孟子之言而论渊源之学，谓本乎自得，非师友传授之可能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250251_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250251_comment'></div>是见孟子之言而不究孟子之不必言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250251_comment'></div>夫欲造道于未得之前而不资诸师友，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250251_comment'></div>必深造而后能自得，非孟子有所不能言，未有舍师友而自能深造者，此又孟子之所不必言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250251_comment'></div>孟子知性为善，知道莫大乎仁义，发其素蕴，著为七篇之书，盖其自得有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250251_comment'></div>然考其师友渊源，岂无所自云？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1250251_comment'></div>世之学者多矣，而自得者鲜，盖由误观孟子之书而以不亲师友为自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1250251_comment'></div>且其父兄之教子弟也，固非无师友也，然其命之之意，殆不过欲其传句读、习文词，以求速化之术尔，鲜有及乎道学之渊源者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1250251_comment'></div>而望其深造自得，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1250251_comment'></div>剡溪周君某天资好善，而乐教子弟，尝命工制先圣十哲坐象及列画七十二子为一堂，即家塾而钦奉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1250251_comment'></div>又亲笔而诏其子孙曰：「亲师友之渊源」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1250251_comment'></div>噫，公之为家训过人一等矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1250251_comment'></div>其后诸孙日益长，师友日益亲，渊源日益叩，而事业日益修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1250251_comment'></div>推其绪馀以事进取，有隶天子学，登乡老书，擢进士第者凡数人，馀皆以学问自立而其进未艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1250251_comment'></div>由是剡之学者推周氏为盛，盖本于公一言之训而得师友渊源之力焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1250251_comment'></div>某与公之孙世修同舍上庠，遂获登公之堂而观其遗迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1250251_comment'></div>时公化去已二载矣，公长子仁泣谓某曰：「吾先子手泽在是，吾惧不能继志，又虑诸子若孙或懈而弗遵，以深吾罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1250251_comment'></div>子幸不吾鄙，辱临兹馆，又辱与吾儿游，幸为我名其堂且记其事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1250251_comment'></div>某辞鄙陋不获，因采公语以名之，并书其大略，俾后人毋忘贤祖之遗训焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1250251_comment'></div>绍兴癸酉四月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1250251_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　剡溪讲学，市人以崇奉东岳为名设盗跖以戏先圣，不忍观看，特作诗。作品：剡溪市人以崇奉东岳为名设盗跖以戏先圣不忍观因书以绝。<div id='poem_541580' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541580' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541580?labeling=true' target='_blank'>剡之市人以崇奉东岳为名设盗蹠以戏先圣所不忍观因书一绝</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541580")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541580_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541580'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541580'>里巷无端戏大儒，恨无司马为行诛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541580'>不知陈蔡当时厄，还似如今嵊县无。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541580'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541580_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年7月23日</a>　告别剡溪诸友，返乡。作品：别周德远诸友。<div id='poem_541642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别周德远诸友</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年7月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541642")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_541642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541642'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541642'>山城过疏雨，客馆生新秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541642'>乡心杂病思，浩荡不可留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541642'>忆昨初来时，园花弄春柔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541642'>俯仰节物<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>变，木杪风飕飕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541642'>旅食百日馀，故人情已周。<div id='poem_sentence_4_541642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_541642'>论文有深味，惜别添牢愁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_541642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_541642'>槐花物色老，琴书散交游。<div id='poem_sentence_6_541642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_541642'>暖律回南枝，相期泛仙舟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_541642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_541642'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_541642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_541642'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_541642_0'>⑴ 原缺，据四库本补，雍正本、光绪本作气</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_541642_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　离开剡溪返乡途中。作品：宿石佛洞。<div id='poem_541643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541643?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿石佛</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_541643")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_541643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541643'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541643'>脩径入幽壑，梵宫摩碧霄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541643'>仰头惊突兀，跬步怯岧峣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541643'>宝相石间涌，钟声云外飘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_541643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_541643'>明朝路南北，身世各尘嚣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_541643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_541643'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_541643_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d38726aaf53043628a8fc6b40c73450f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d38726aaf53043628a8fc6b40c73450f");'><span id='d38726aaf53043628a8fc6b40c73450f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a
