ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年9月</a>　抵达绍兴府就任佥判。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　绍兴府就任佥判，游览名胜风光作诗。作品：蓬莱阁。西园。鉴湖。<div id='poem_542023' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542023' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542023?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蓬莱阁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542023")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_542023_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542023'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542023'>祖龙车辙遍尘寰，只道蓬莱在海间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542023_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542023'>空上<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作向）</span>望秦山上望，不知此处是神山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542023_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542023'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_542023_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_542041' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542041' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542041?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西园</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542041")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_542041_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542041'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542041'>西园风物冠东州，飞盖纷纷烂熳游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542041'>惟有红莲幕中客，倚栏才得片时留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542041'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_542041_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_542045' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542045?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鉴湖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542045")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_542045_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542045'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542045'>胸中万顷元才子，方外孤标贺季真。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542045_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542045'>鉴水萦回三百里，风流何止两唐人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542045_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542045'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_542045_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　绍兴府就任佥判，考察风土人情作《会稽三赋》<div id='poem_1249833' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249833' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249833?labeling=true' target='_blank'>会稽风俗赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（并叙）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249833")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249833_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249833'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249833'>昔司马相如作《上林赋》，设<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/1/Comments/2")'>子虚</span>、乌有先生、亡是公三人相答难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249833_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>子虚</span>，虚言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249833_comment'></div>乌有先生者，乌有是事也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249833_comment'></div>亡是公者，亡是人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249833_comment'></div>故其词多夸而其事不实，如卢橘黄柑之类，盖上林所无者，犹庄生之寓言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249833_comment'></div>余赋会稽，虽文采不足以拟相如之万一，然事皆实录，故设为子真、无妄先生、有君答问之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249833_comment'></div>子真者，诚言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249833_comment'></div>无妄者，不虚也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249833_comment'></div>有君者，有是事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249833_comment'></div>以反相如之说焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249833_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1249833'>有客过越，自称子真，介于无妄先生，贽见于有君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249833_comment'></div>谒入，乃膝而前曰：「闻有君之名雅矣，今幸际颜色，聆话言，仆辄有请，君其听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249833_comment'></div>君世家于越，以风流自命，业传缃素，才播歌咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249833_comment'></div>越之山川人物、古今风俗，载在君腹，愿闻其略，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249833_comment'></div>有君乃歛衽肃容谢曰：「唯唯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249833_comment'></div>客姑坐焉，吾以语尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249833_comment'></div>越于九域，分曰扬州<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249833_comment'></div>仰瞻天文，度当斗牛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249833_comment'></div>在辰为丑，自夏而侯<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249833_comment'></div>郡于秦汉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>，霸于春秋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249833_comment'></div>州于隋而使于唐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>，公有素而王有镠<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑺</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249833_comment'></div>因种山而中宅<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑻</sup>，廓蠡成而外州<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑼</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1249833_comment'></div>龙楼翼而屹峙，石窦伏而巽流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1249833_comment'></div>法天门兮地户，惟昆崙兮是侔<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑽</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1249833_comment'></div>实东南之大府，号天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/63/Comments/1")'>无仇</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（天下本无仇。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1249833_comment'></div>其山则郁郁苍苍，岩岩嵬嵬，磅礴蜿蜒，嵂崒崥崹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1249833_comment'></div>若骞若奔，若阖若开，或凸或凹，或阜或堆，或断而联，或昂而低。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1249833_comment'></div>虎卧龟𥖁，龙盘雁徊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1249833_comment'></div>舒为屏障，峙为楼台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1249833_comment'></div>崦映江湖，明灭云霓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1249833_comment'></div>八山中藏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑾</sup>，千里周回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1249833_comment'></div>彭鲍名存<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑿</sup>，钜者南镇，是为会稽<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒀</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1249833_comment'></div>洞曰阳明，群仙所栖<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒁</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1249833_comment'></div>石伞如张<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒂</sup>，石帆如扬<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒃</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1249833_comment'></div>石篑如藏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒄</sup>，石鹞如翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1249833_comment'></div>石壁匪泥<span class='inlineComment2'>（并见石帆注。）</span>，石瓮匪携<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒅</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1249833_comment'></div>香炉自烟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒆</sup>，天柱可梯<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒇</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1249833_comment'></div>韫玉有笥<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(21)</sup>，降仙有台<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(22)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1249833_comment'></div>禹穴窅而叵探<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(23)</sup>，葛岩蜚而自来<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(24)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1249833_comment'></div>射堂丰凶之的<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(25)</sup>，宛委日月之圭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(26)</sup>，应天上之玉衡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(27)</sup>，直海中之蓬莱<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(28)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1249833_comment'></div>至若嵊山岿其东<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(29)</sup>，涂山屹其西<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(30)</sup>，阜至繇蜀<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(31)</sup>，龟来自齐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(32)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1249833_comment'></div>梅山乃隐吏之窟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(33)</sup>，纻罗盖西子之闺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(34)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1249833_comment'></div>五泄争奇于雁荡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(35)</sup>，四明竞秀于天台<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(36)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1249833_comment'></div>五云中令之故居<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(37)</sup>，十峰昙翼之招提<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(38)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1249833_comment'></div>故越为之首兮，剡为之面兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1249833_comment'></div>沃洲天姥，眉兮目兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(39)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1249833_comment'></div>金庭桐柏，仙子宅兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(40)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1249833_comment'></div>南明嵌崆，宝相涌兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(41)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1249833_comment'></div>南岩嵯峨，海迹古兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(42)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1249833_comment'></div>陟秦望而望秦兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(43)</sup>，登洛思而思洛兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(44)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1249833_comment'></div>采葛食蕺，敬吊前王兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(45)</sup>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1249833_comment'></div>脩竹茂林，缅想陈迹兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(46)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1249833_comment'></div>连山如珠，秦皇之所驱兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(47)</sup>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1249833_comment'></div>擪山如玦，亚父之所割兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(48)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1249833_comment'></div>北干隐兮明月在<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(49)</sup>，东山卧兮白云迷<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(50)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1249833_comment'></div>少微寂兮幽鸟怨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(51)</sup>，太白空兮野猿啼<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(52)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1249833_comment'></div>其水则浩淼泓澄，散漫萦迂，涨焉而大，风焉而波，净焉如练，莹焉如磨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1249833_comment'></div>溢而为江，潴而为湖，为沼为沚，为潢为污。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1249833_comment'></div>汇为陂泽，疏为沟渠，𥧲而田畴，淤而泥涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1249833_comment'></div>生我稻粱，溉我果蔬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1249833_comment'></div>集有凫雁，戏有龟鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1249833_comment'></div>实有菱芡，香有芙蕖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1249833_comment'></div>鹘舟如击<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(53)</sup>，马楫如驱<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(54)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1249833_comment'></div>船龙夭矫，桥兽睢盱<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(55)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1249833_comment'></div>堰限江河，津通漕输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1249833_comment'></div>航瓯舶闽，浮鄞达吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1249833_comment'></div>浪桨风帆，千艘万舻，大武挽繂，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/168/Comments/0")'>五丁</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/168/Comments/1")'>噪謼</span>，榜人奏功，千里须臾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1249833_comment'></div>境绝利博，莫如鉴湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1249833_comment'></div>有八百里之回环，灌九千顷之膏腴<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(56)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1249833_comment'></div>浮贺监之家<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(57)</sup>，浸允常之都<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(58)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1249833_comment'></div>人在鉴中，舟行画图<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(59)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1249833_comment'></div>五月清凉，人间所无<span class='inlineComment2'>（杜甫诗：「鉴湖五月凉。」）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1249833_comment'></div>有菱歌兮声峭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(60)</sup>，有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/182/Comments/1")'>莲女</span>兮貌都<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(61)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1249833_comment'></div>日出兮烟销，渔郎兮啸嘑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1249833_comment'></div>东泛曹江，哀彼孝娥<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(62)</sup>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1249833_comment'></div>西观惊涛，吊夫子胥<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(63)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1249833_comment'></div>槩浦思夫槩之封<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(64)</sup>，翁洲访偃王之庐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(65)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1249833_comment'></div>箪醪投兮沼吴国<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(66)</sup>，扁舟去兮变陶朱<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(67)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1249833_comment'></div>鼓樵风兮游若邪<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(68)</sup>，兴雪棹兮寻隐居<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(69)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1249833_comment'></div>禊事脩兮觞兰渚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(70)</sup>，陶泓沐兮池戒珠<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(71)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1249833_comment'></div>了溪凿兮禹功毕<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(72)</sup>，刑塘筑兮长人诛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(73)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1249833_comment'></div>酌菲泉兮怀古<span class='inlineComment2'>（会稽山大禹寺有泉，名曰菲泉。）</span>，饮清白兮自娱<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(74)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1249833_comment'></div>其物则有鱼盐之饶<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(75)</sup>，竹箭之美<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(76)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1249833_comment'></div>山涵海蓄，言其有几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1249833_comment'></div>贡入王室，利周遐迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1249833_comment'></div>耕焉以火，耨焉以水<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(77)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1249833_comment'></div>南风翼苗，翠浪千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1249833_comment'></div>𥝧稏一空，玉粒如峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1249833_comment'></div>炊粳酿秫，既甘且旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1249833_comment'></div>檿桑之奇，号为第一<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(78)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1249833_comment'></div>龙精㒩㒩，吐丝满室<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(79)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1249833_comment'></div>万草千华，机轴中出，绫纱缯縠，雪积缣匹<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(80)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1249833_comment'></div>木则枫梃千丈<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(81)</sup>，松封五夫<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(82)</sup>，桐柏合生<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(83)</sup>，檫棐异隅<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(84)</sup>，文梓楩楠<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(85)</sup>，栎柞槠榆<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(86)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1249833_comment'></div>连理之柯<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(87)</sup>，合抱之株，乃斧乃斤，以舆以庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1249833_comment'></div>乃有萧山陆吉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(88)</sup>，诸暨三如<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(89)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1249833_comment'></div>胡楠成林，贺瓜满区<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(90)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1249833_comment'></div>枣实全赤，檎腮半朱，火榧壳玉，樱桃荐珠，鸭脚含黄，鸡头去卢，百益七绝之奇<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(91)</sup>，双头四角之殊<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(92)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1249833_comment'></div>蔗有昆崙之号<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(93)</sup>，梅有官长之呼<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(94)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1249833_comment'></div>蔓生则马乳蘡薁，土实则凫茈慈菰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1249833_comment'></div>野蔌溪毛，园蔬木菌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1249833_comment'></div>湘湖之莼，箭里之笋<span class='inlineComment2'>（萧山湘湖出莼菜，会稽有美箭里。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1249833_comment'></div>可荐可羞，采撷无尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1249833_comment'></div>鳞虫水族，海生池养，丁首丙尾，皤腹缩项，赤鲩文鳢，玄𩺀黄𩺞<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(95)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1249833_comment'></div>䱷人骈集，以钩以网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1249833_comment'></div>羹金鲙玉，不数熊掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1249833_comment'></div>能言之鹜，善鸣之鹅<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(96)</sup>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_105_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/267/Comments/0")'>输芒</span>之蟹，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_105_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/268/Comments/0")'>孕珠</span>之蠃，文身合氏之子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(97)</sup>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_105_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/270/Comments/1")'>跛足从事</span>之徒<span class='inlineComment2'>（元微之诗：「鳖解称从事。」）</span>，街填巷委，与土仝多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1249833_comment'></div>异兽珍禽，屑铜吐绶<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(98)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1249833_comment'></div>猛虎负子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(99)</sup>，灵乌送𪆪<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(100)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1249833_comment'></div>凤栖鹿化<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(101)</sup>，鹤拾雁耨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(102)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1249833_comment'></div>熊罴狸豹，猴玃猿啼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1249833_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_110_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/281/Comments/1")'>鵁衔</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_110_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/281/Comments/2")'>鸬吐</span><sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(103)</sup>，莺求鹑斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1249833_comment'></div>鸥浮鹬浴<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(104)</sup>，鸦寒鳦瘦<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(105)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1249833_comment'></div>巧妇锥喙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(106)</sup>，舂锄雪脰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(107)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1249833_comment'></div>林栖水宿，脩尾长咮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(108)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1249833_comment'></div>江湖为笼，山林为囿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1249833_comment'></div>以牡以牝，以蜚以走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1249833_comment'></div>甲第名园，奇葩异香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1249833_comment'></div>牡丹如洛，芍药如扬<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(109)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1249833_comment'></div>木兰载新<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(110)</sup>，海榴怀芳<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(111)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1249833_comment'></div>菊山黄华<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(112)</sup>，兰亭国香<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(113)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1249833_comment'></div>天衣杜鹃<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(114)</sup>，东山蔷薇<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(115)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1249833_comment'></div>湖映香雪<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(116)</sup>，鉴生水芝<span class='inlineComment2'>（李白诗：「荷花鉴里生。」）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1249833_comment'></div>鸳梅并蒂<span class='inlineComment2'>（越有鸳鸯梅，双头千叶。）</span>，仙桂丹枝<span class='inlineComment2'>（越有丹桂）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1249833_comment'></div>司华骋巧，天女效奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1249833_comment'></div>桃李漫山，臧穫视之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1249833_comment'></div>药物之产，不知其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1249833_comment'></div>白术丹参，甘菊黄精，吴萸越桃<span class='inlineComment2'>（山栀子一名越桃。）</span>，禹粮石英<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(117)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1249833_comment'></div>蓟训鬻之以疗疾<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(118)</sup>，彭祖服之而延龄<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(119)</sup>，秦皇求之而莫致<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(120)</sup>，葛仙饵之而飞升<span class='inlineComment2'>（葛仙翁炼丹飞升，禹穴北有仙岩。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1249833_comment'></div>日铸雪芽<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(121)</sup>，卧龙瑞草<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(122)</sup>，瀑岭称仙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(123)</sup>，茗山斗好<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(124)</sup>，顾渚争先，建溪仝蚤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1249833_comment'></div>碾尘飞玉，瓯涛翻皓，生两腋之清风，兴飘飘于蓬岛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1249833_comment'></div>剡藤番番，管城斑斑<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(125)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1249833_comment'></div>冰敲嵊水<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(126)</sup>，竹剪顾园<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(127)</sup>，制于蒙、蔡之手，游于羲、猷之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1249833_comment'></div>友陈元与端紫，仝文字于人寰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1249833_comment'></div>至若龙护金书<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(128)</sup>，苔封石刻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(129)</sup>，苗山金玉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(130)</sup>，邪堇铜锡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(131)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1249833_comment'></div>黄帝之鉴<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(132)</sup>，神禹之璧<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(133)</sup>，欧冶之剑<span class='inlineComment2'>（见「邪堇铜锡」注。）</span>，蔡邕之笛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(134)</sup>，虞翻之床<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(135)</sup>，秦皇之石<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(136)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1249833_comment'></div>淳碑斯篆<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(137)</sup>，江笔肃墨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(138)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1249833_comment'></div>雷鼓铜漏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(139)</sup>，梅梁窆石<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(140)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1249833_comment'></div>罍金履铁<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(141)</sup>，罂铜印玉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(142)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1249833_comment'></div>胎草<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_138_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/355/Comments/1")'>蹄石</span><sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(143)</sup>，黄竹神木<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(144)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1249833_comment'></div>流黄汉簟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(145)</sup>，錞于周乐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(146)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1249833_comment'></div>活人之草<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(147)</sup>，止痛之木<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(148)</sup>，柘敷荣而华含戚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(149)</sup>，天雨钱而山储粟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(150)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1249833_comment'></div>皆希世之奇迹，盖欲言而不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1249833_comment'></div>其人则见于《吴越春秋》、《会稽典录》，图经地志，历代柬牍，大书特书，班班满目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1249833_comment'></div>孝者悌者，忠者义者，廉者逊者，智者健者，优于文词者，长于吏事者，擢秀科目之荣者，策名卿相之贵者，杀身以成仁者，隐居以求志者，埋光屠钓之微者，晦迹佛老之异者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1249833_comment'></div>虞翻之言有所不能尽，朱育之对有所不能既<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(151)</sup>，予亦焉能缕数之哉，姑摘其尤之一二：前则种、蠡、计𥓋，号贤大夫<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(152)</sup>，后则严助、买臣，直承明庐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(153)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1249833_comment'></div>孝悌则张万和之父子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(154)</sup>，韩灵敏之弟昆<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(155)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1249833_comment'></div>邓、斯、祁、樊自杀以代罪<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(156)</sup>，董黯、朱、魏报雠而名闻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(157)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1249833_comment'></div>或湿衣以障火<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(158)</sup>，或泣血以戢焚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(159)</sup>，或衔哀而庐墓<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(160)</sup>，或负土以成坟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(161)</sup>，或以行而名里<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(162)</sup>，或以义而旌门<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(163)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1249833_comment'></div>懿矣三女<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(164)</sup>，贤哉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_148_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/401/Comments/1")'>二娥</span><sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(165)</sup>，处子之孝，凛然可多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1249833_comment'></div>节义则黄公居四皓之列<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(166)</sup>，魏少英参八隽之俦<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(167)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1249833_comment'></div>蒙难卫主则有若丁潭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(168)</sup>，委身授命则有若王脩<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(169)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1249833_comment'></div>虞喜躬岁寒之操<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(170)</sup>，孔愉洪止足之谋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(171)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1249833_comment'></div>或一门死三世之义<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(172)</sup>，或一邑萃三康之㳅<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(173)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1249833_comment'></div>至若㮤杨柳朱，永宁瞿素，妇节峥嵘，蹈死不顾<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(174)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1249833_comment'></div>卓行则郑洪、韩说、钟离意、朱隽、戴就举于孝廉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(175)</sup>，虞潭、孔奂、沈融、朱仕明举于秀茂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(176)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1249833_comment'></div>虞寄起于对策<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(177)</sup>，赵晔推于有道<span class='inlineComment2'>（后汉赵晔，山阴人，举有道。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1249833_comment'></div>陈子公退侵地之藩<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(178)</sup>，钟离牧拒惭还之稻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(179)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1249833_comment'></div>循吏则有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_157_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/422/Comments/1")'>还珠</span>孟尝<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(180)</sup>，致雁虞国<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(181)</sup>，希铣遗四州之爱<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(182)</sup>，夏香著历任之绩<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(183)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1249833_comment'></div>儒学则王充以《论衡》显<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(184)</sup>，沈珣以《大义》称<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(185)</sup>，谢沉、谢承之史学<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(186)</sup>，孔佥、孔祛之明经<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(187)</sup>，贺孝先擅儒宗号<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(188)</sup>，虞伯施剸博学之名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(189)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1249833_comment'></div>文章则孙兴公掞金声之赋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(190)</sup>，徐季海挥玉堂之策<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(191)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1249833_comment'></div>晔若春荣则任奕、虞翔<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(192)</sup>，文不加点则四明狂客<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(193)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1249833_comment'></div>二贺、二虞蜚声籍籍<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(194)</sup>，吴融十诏成于俄刻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(195)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1249833_comment'></div>隐逸则严、谢、秦、方、述睿、充符<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(196)</sup>，方术则介象、吴范、严卿、夷吾<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(197)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1249833_comment'></div>丹青则孙遇、道芬<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(198)</sup>，笔札则孔琳、徐峤<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(199)</sup>，浮屠则道林、灵澈<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(200)</sup>，神仙则刘晨、阮肇<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(201)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1249833_comment'></div>乃有溪上浣纱之女<span class='inlineComment2'>（诸暨有西施浣纱石。）</span>，林间舞剑之姝<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(202)</sup>，色白天下<span class='inlineComment2'>（杜诗：「越女天下白。」）</span>，气雄万夫<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(203)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1249833_comment'></div>故勾践复国也，有六千君子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(204)</sup>，项氏崛起也，有八千子弟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(205)</sup>，霸有江浙，横行当代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1249833_comment'></div>彼二霸之得人，尚斗量而车载，矧历世之人材，亦足明其大槩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1249833_comment'></div>逮我国朝，尤号多士，二百年间，不可胜纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1249833_comment'></div>大则杜正献之勋德<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(206)</sup>，次则孙威敏之功名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(207)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1249833_comment'></div>姚石郎司元祐之直<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(208)</sup>，顾内相号江南之英<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(209)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1249833_comment'></div>万石云仍，匪建则庆<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(210)</sup>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1249833_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_171_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/468/Comments/0")'>二陆</span>棠棣，如云与衡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(211)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1249833_comment'></div>吴先生风高于贺老<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(212)</sup>，齐职方迹拟于渊明<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(213)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1249833_comment'></div>钱氏世贤科之盛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(214)</sup>，史门继衣锦之荣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(215)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1249833_comment'></div>刘求以义门显<span class='inlineComment2'>（会稽求氏、上虞刘氏，并号义门。）</span>，杜赵以处士称<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(216)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1249833_comment'></div>或览古以流咏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(217)</sup>，或编图而著名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(218)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1249833_comment'></div>至若联翩桂籍，焜耀簪缨，名登史策，足叠天庭，盖尝询之故老，往往莫识其名矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1249833_comment'></div>故千岩竞秀、万壑争流者，顾长康之言也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(219)</sup>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1249833_comment'></div>山转远转高、水转深转清者，李浙东之记也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(220)</sup>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1249833_comment'></div>瑰奇市井、佳丽闉阇者，白馀杭之诗也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(221)</sup>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1249833_comment'></div>忠臣系踵、孝子连闾者，虞功曹之对也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(222)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1249833_comment'></div>越之山川风物，其大略如此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1249833_comment'></div>子真始惊而疑，卒叹而敼曰：「壮矣哉，盛矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1249833_comment'></div>山川如斯，人物如斯，吾未之前闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1249833_comment'></div>然越在春秋，僻处东夷，夫子作经，𡬯为于越，其人材风俗，固未可与齐、晋、鲁、卫诸列国抗衡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1249833_comment'></div>今有君所称，几不容口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1249833_comment'></div>岂昔日远于京畿，含香未越，如王景兴之言邪<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(223)</sup>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1249833_comment'></div>抑山川降灵孕秀，固自有时邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1249833_comment'></div>抑亦因人作成而致然邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1249833_comment'></div>有君曰：「昔严朱二子，为汉名卿，昼绣故乡，夹道郊迎，争观快睹，歆艳其荣，故其俗始尚文学而敼功名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(224)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1249833_comment'></div>晋王右军为越内史，雅会兰亭，流觞曲水，临池墨妙，辉映千祀，能使遗文感槩君子，故其俗始尚风流，而多翰墨之士<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(225)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1249833_comment'></div>唐元微之一代奇才，罢侍玉皇，谪居蓬莱，宾窦邻白，唱酬往来，繇是鉴湖秦望之奇益闻，故其俗至今好吟咏，而多风骚之才<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(226)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1249833_comment'></div>不独此数君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1249833_comment'></div>任延、张霸以尚贤为治，而俗始贵士<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(227)</sup>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1249833_comment'></div>刘宠、车俊以洁己化下，而人斯尚清<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(228)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1249833_comment'></div>第五伦下令而淫祀之风革<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(229)</sup>，诸葛恢莅政而陵迟之俗兴<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(230)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1249833_comment'></div>至若李唐，刺史九十八公，首有庞玉，显有姚崇，图经十子，郡绩称雄<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(231)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1249833_comment'></div>国朝逮今，盖百馀政，前有文简，后有文正，题名所记，比唐为盛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(232)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1249833_comment'></div>承宣得人，风俗斯美，盖亦理之然也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1249833_comment'></div>子真曰：「是诚有之，然皆二千石之事尔，未足多也，愿闻其上者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1249833_comment'></div>有君曰：「昔勾践惩会稽之栖也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(233)</sup>，痛石室之辱也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(234)</sup>，蓼目水足，抱冰握火<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(235)</sup>，采蕺于山<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(236)</sup>，置胆于坐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(237)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1249833_comment'></div>葛妇兴歌，名曰《何苦》，其词曰：『尝胆不苦味若饴，令我采葛以作丝<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(238)</sup>』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1249833_comment'></div>二十年间，焦心苦志，卒灭强吴，以雪前耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1249833_comment'></div>《越绝》之称，权舆于此<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(239)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1249833_comment'></div>故其俗至今能慷慨以复雠，隐忍以成事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1249833_comment'></div>若是何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1249833_comment'></div>子真曰：「兹霸者之事也，传不云乎，『碎而王，驳而霸』，彼齐威、晋文之盛，犹不足称于大君子之门，况勾践乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1249833_comment'></div>有君曰：「昔禹治水之毕，与群后计功苗山，更名会稽，卒而葬焉，祠庙陵寝，于今尚存<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(240)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1249833_comment'></div>上有遗井<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(241)</sup>，下有菲泉，过而饮者，莫不发免鱼之叹，兴河洛之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1249833_comment'></div>不独勾践有其烈<span class='inlineComment2'>（《史记》：「勾践有禹之遗烈。」）</span>，马侯嗣其功<span class='inlineComment2'>（马臻创立鉴湖。）</span>，至今其俗勤劳俭啬，实有禹之遗风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1249833_comment'></div>若是何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1249833_comment'></div>子真曰：「美哉禹功！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1249833_comment'></div>宜其代舜而有天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1249833_comment'></div>游于是，穸于是，庙食于是，兹所以化被万世之久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1249833_comment'></div>然说者以为入圣域而未优，其必有大于此者乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1249833_comment'></div>有君曰：「舜生于诸冯，孟子以为东夷之人，历世逾远，流传失真，太史公以为冀州，然邪，否邪<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(242)</sup>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1249833_comment'></div>然越之邑则有上虞、馀姚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(243)</sup>，山有虞山、历山<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(244)</sup>，水有渔浦三怃<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(245)</sup>，地则有姚丘百官<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(246)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1249833_comment'></div>里焉有粟<span class='inlineComment2'>（上虞有粟里，舜时供储在此。）</span>，陶焉有灶<span class='inlineComment2'>（上虞有古陶灶，言舜所作。）</span>，汲焉有井<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(247)</sup>，祀焉有庙<span class='inlineComment2'>（舜庙在上虞县西三十五里。）</span>，皆其遗迹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1249833_comment'></div>意者，不生于是，则游于是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1249833_comment'></div>舜为人子，克谐以孝，故其俗至今烝烝是效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1249833_comment'></div>舜为人臣，克尽其道，故其俗至今孳孳是蹈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1249833_comment'></div>舜为人兄，怨怒不藏，故其俗至今爱而能容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1249833_comment'></div>舜为人君，以天下禅，故其俗至今廉而能逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1249833_comment'></div>若是如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1249833_comment'></div>子真矍然离席而立，拱手而对曰：「于戏，噫嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1249833_comment'></div>尽善尽美，虽甚盛德，蔑有加矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1249833_comment'></div>昔季札观乐而止于《韶》，自《韶》之外不敢观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1249833_comment'></div>余问风俗，亦极于舜，自舜之外不复问矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1249833_comment'></div>无妄先生粲然失笑于旁，曰：「固则子真之问、有君之答也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1249833_comment'></div>兹皆古之越，非今之越也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1249833_comment'></div>人死骨朽，世变风移，山川虽在，人物已非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1249833_comment'></div>前日淳朴变而浇伪，前日廉逊变而争敚，前日勤俭变而矫怠，前日忠孝变而凶悖，尚何执纸上陈迹而譊譊其颊舌邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1249833_comment'></div>有君曰：「先生之言是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1249833_comment'></div>然风俗不常美，亦不常弊，善焉恶焉，维人是系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1249833_comment'></div>今朝廷驻跸东南，越为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_234_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/687/Comments/0")'>钜藩</span>，密迩尧天，盖尺五间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1249833_comment'></div>帝命重臣，来镇是邦，入境问俗，登堂观风<span class='inlineComment2'>（卧龙山有观风堂。）</span>，因舜禹之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_235_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/694/Comments/0")'>遗化</span>，明吾君之至仁，布德教于黄堂，变薄俗而还淳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1249833_comment'></div>矧何世之无才，亦奚有于古今？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1249833_comment'></div>子不见夫衔命虏庭，死于王事，如陈公、张公者乎<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(248)</sup>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1249833_comment'></div>议礼靖康，赴难建炎，如华君、傅君者乎<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(249)</sup>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1249833_comment'></div>是岂异代之人邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1249833_comment'></div>又不见夫姚江陈公<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈公名橐）</span>，所临有声，亦克知退，身名两荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1249833_comment'></div>执政李公<span class='inlineComment2'>（李公名光）</span>，忤意权臣，老于沦落，世贤其人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1249833_comment'></div>悯孝蔡子，捐生可悲，同彼旌忠，庙食于兹<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(250)</sup>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1249833_comment'></div>隐吏王君<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(251)</sup>，斩雠著名，一门可称，贤父难兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1249833_comment'></div>兹固先生目所亲睹也，安知后之视今，不犹今之视古乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1249833_comment'></div>先生曰：「有君越人也，知越之风俗而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1249833_comment'></div>昔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_246_1249833", 1249833, "Clauses/729/Comments/0")'>子虚</span>夸云梦，乌有先生诧齐，亡是公折之以上林之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1249833_comment'></div>今越未足侔齐楚之大，尚何足以夸之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1249833_comment'></div>有君曰：「昔吴子问柳先生以晋国之事，而柳以晋对；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1249833_comment'></div>今子真问余以越国之俗，而余以越答，亦各因其所问而及之尔，余岂瞢然无闻无知于越之外哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1249833_comment'></div>今天子披舆地之图，思祖宗之绩，求治如不及，见贤而太息，文德既修，武事时阅，盖将舞干戚而服远夷，复侵疆而旋京阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1249833_comment'></div>余俟其车书仝，南北一，仿吉甫，美周室，赋《崧高》，歌吉日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1249833_comment'></div>招鲁公，命元结，磨苍崖，秃钜笔，颂中兴，纪洪烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1249833_comment'></div>迈三五，夐前牒，亘天地，昭日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1249833_comment'></div>于是穷章亥之所步，考神禹之所别，览四海九州之风俗，掩《两京》、《三都》之著述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1249833_comment'></div>腾万丈之光芒，有皇宋一统之赋出，回视会稽，盖甄陶中之一物」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1249833_comment'></div>无妄先生自知失言，色有馀愧，乃与子真逡巡而避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1249833_comment'></div>有君退而啸傲于南窗，有飘飘凌云之气<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>(252)</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1249833_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_258_1249833'>「登洛思」下原衍「兮」字，据雍正本、四库本、光绪本删。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1249833_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_259_1249833'>泫露：四库本同，雍正本、光绪本作「濯露」。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_259_1249833'></div><div id='poem_sentence_259_1249833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1249833'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_1249833_0'>⑴ 《禹贡》：「淮海惟扬州。」《周礼》：「东南曰扬州，山曰会稽。」《图经》：「大都督府越州，《禹贡》扬州之域。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_17_1249833_0'>⑵ 《汉书·地理志》：「吴地斗分野。」《晋书·天文志》：「自斗十三度至女七度为星纪，于辰在丑，吴越分，曰扬州，而会稽入斗一度。」白乐天诗云：「牛斗天垂象，台明地展图。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_18_1249833_0'>⑶ 《史记》：「越王勾践，其先禹之苗裔，夏少康之庶子也，封于会稽，以奉禹祀。」《图经》：「封少子无馀于越，是为越侯。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_1249833_0'>⑷ 秦始皇灭荆，置会稽郡。汉以其地属吴国，景帝诛吴王，复为会稽郡。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_1249833_0'>⑸ 《春秋》：「哀公十三年于越入吴。」《史记》：「勾践已平吴，兵横行于江淮，号称霸王。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_20_1249833_0'>⑹ 隋大业中改为越州，唐乾元中置浙江东道节度观察等使。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_20_1249833_0'>⑺ 隋杨素封越国公，唐末钱镠平董昌，封吴越国王。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_1249833_0'>⑻ 《图经》：「种山一名重山，即今卧龙山也。」《吴越春秋》：「越王葬文种于国之西山，一年，伍子胥自海上穿山胁持文种去，与之俱游于海。」今西山低处是也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_1249833_0'>⑼ 《吴越春秋》：「勾践自吴还，范蠡筑小城，周千一百二十二步，一员三方。西北立为龙翼之楼，以象天门。东南伏漏石窦，以象地户。陵门四达，以象八风。外郭筑城而缺西北，示服事吴也。」《图经》：「会稽治山阴以来，此城即为郡城。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1249833_0'>⑽ 《吴越春秋》：「范蠡曰：『臣之丛城也，其应天矣，昆崙之象存焉。』」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_30_1249833_0'>⑾ 府城之内有八山：种山、⿔山、蕺山、火珠山、鲍郎山、彭山、白马山、蛾眉山。今所存者惟四山耳，鲍郎、彭山、白马、蛾眉俱已湮灭，仅存其名。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1249833_0'>⑿ 《图经》：「彭山在会稽县北四里。」《典录》云：「彭祖所隐居之城。鲍郎山一名阳堂山，在今大能仁寺之前。」《郡国志》云：「山有鲍郎祠。」蛾马迹迷。蛾眉山不见于《图经》，父老云：在府桥之东，轩亭之西，形如蛾眉。白马山在会稽县北五里。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1249833_0'>⒀ 《史记》：「禹会诸侯江南，计力命曰会稽。会稽者，会计也。」《皇览》曰：「会稽山本名苗山。」唐开元十年封四镇为公，故会稽山为南镇永兴公。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_32_1249833_0'>⒁ 《⿔山白玉上经》曰：「会稽山周回一百二十里，名阳明洞天，皆仙圣天人都会之所。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_33_1249833_0'>⒂ 《图经》：「石伞山在会稽县东南十五里玉笥侧，状如伞。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_33_1249833_0'>⒃ 石帆山在会稽县东十五里。夏侯曾先《地理志》云：「射的山北有石壁，高数十丈，中央少纡，状如张帆。又有文石，状如鹞，人亦谓之石鹞山。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_34_1249833_0'>⒄ 《舆地志》云：「宛委山上有石篑，壁立干云，升者累梯而至。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_35_1249833_0'>⒅ 巨石三在照湖东，状如酒瓮，时人谓之秦皇酒瓮。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_36_1249833_0'>⒆ 会稽一峰状如香炉，人谓之香炉峰，一名覆釜山。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_36_1249833_0'>⒇ 《吴越春秋》：「九山东南天柱，号曰宛委。」《图经》：「望泰山一名天柱山。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_37_1249833_0'>(21) 《图经》：「玉笥山在会稽县东南十五里，出美玉，其形如笥，因以为名。一名茅岘。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_37_1249833_0'>(22) 《皇览》云：「宛委山上有一巨石，屹然如几台，尝有神仙降其上，号降仙台。苗龙先生于此台上升。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_38_1249833_0'>(23) 《史记》：司马迁登会稽，探禹穴。唐郑鲂有禹穴碑。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_38_1249833_0'>(24) 《龙瑞图经》：「禹穴北有石岩，高丈馀，南面侧平如削。」《真诰》云：「此石于赤乌二年天降，从安悉国飞来，上有索痕二条，名为飞来石。晋葛仙公曾筑坛炼丹，后人名葛仙岩、炼丹井。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_39_1249833_0'>(25) 孔晔《会稽记》云：「射的山半有石室，乃仙人射堂。东峰有射的，遥望山壁有白点如射侯。士人常以占谷贵贱，故语云：『射的白，米斛百；射壁玄，米斛千。』」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_39_1249833_0'>(26) 《遁甲开山图》云：「禹开宛委山，得赤圭如日，碧圭如月，长一尺二寸。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_39_1249833_0'>(27) 《舆地志》云：「会稽山一名衡山。」《吴越春秋》：「禹闻黄帝藏书于此，乃东巡，登衡岭。」《龙瑞图经》注云：「谓天文盖度中权，衡，星名，非南岳之衡岭。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_39_1249833_0'>(28) 旧志：「蓬莱山正属会稽。」沈绅《蓬莱阁》诗云：「三山对峙海中央。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_40_1249833_0'>(29) 《图经》：「嵊山在剡县东三十四里。」唐武德四年置嵊山，因山为名，今曰嵊县。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_40_1249833_0'>(30) 涂山在山阴西北四十五里。旧《图经》云：「禹会诸侯之所。」应劭云：「涂山在永兴北。」按永兴即萧山也。杜预注《左传》云：「在淮南寿春。」亦未详在何所。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_40_1249833_0'>(31) 蜀阜山在山阴县北三十五里。旧经按地志云：「昔自蜀飞来，带儿妇二十馀人，随山而至，善织美锦。自云：『家在西蜀，今忽至此。』」又云：「勾践将伐吴，置妇女于山上，以邀军士。」后讹为阜。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_40_1249833_0'>(32) ⿔山在山阴县东八十步，下有东武里，或谓之怪山。《吴越春秋》：「范蠡筑城既成，怪山自生琅玕，东武海中山也，一夕自来，故名怪山。」《越绝书》云：「勾践游台也，东南司马门所以灼⿔。又仰望天气，观天怪也，云，远望似⿔形。或名⿔山。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_41_1249833_0'>(33) 梅山一名巫山，在府城北一十八里，梅子真所隐之地也。其西则有梅市里、梅福里。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_41_1249833_0'>(34) 《舆地志》云：「诸暨县罗山，西施、郑旦所居，有方石，云是西施晒纱处。今名纻罗山。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_42_1249833_0'>(35) 《掇英集》：五泄，瀑布也。在诸暨西四十里，有两山夹溪，造云壁立，高二百丈、广数十丈，水泻五节，故曰五泄。山多奇峰，或比之雁荡云。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_42_1249833_0'>(36) 《图经》：「四明山在馀姚县。」孙绰《天台赋》云：「涉海则有方丈蓬莱，登陆则有四明、天台。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_43_1249833_0'>(37) 晋义熙三年，中书令王献之居是山，有五色祥云见，安帝诏建云门寺。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_43_1249833_0'>(38) 法华山在会稽县南四十里，晋僧昙翼栖此，诵《法华经》，因置寺焉。其山十峰，其水双涧，今天衣寺是也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_45_1249833_0'>(39) 白乐天《沃洲山记》云：「东南山水越为首，剡为面，沃洲天姥为眉、目。」二山今属新昌县。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_46_1249833_0'>(40) 金庭观在剡县东，王子晋学道登仙之所。《真诰》曰：「南岳真人云：『越有桐柏之金庭，养真之福地，升仙之灵墟也。』」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_47_1249833_0'>(41) 新昌南明山有宝相寺，梁建安王造石佛一躯，高一百尺。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_48_1249833_0'>(42) 南岩在新昌县西南。唐李绅《龙宫寺碑》云：「南岩海迹，高下犹存。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_49_1249833_0'>(43) 《史记》：「秦始皇二十七年，上会稽祭大禹，望于南海，立石刻颂。」《图经》：「秦望山在会稽南四十里。又有望秦山，始皇登山，群臣于此以望秦中。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_49_1249833_0'>(44) 洛思山在萧山县东。《舆志》云：「永兴县有洛思山，洛人朱隽来会稽，三年不得反，乃登山北顾而叹，因以为名。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_50_1249833_0'>(45) 蕺山在府治东北三里。赵璘直碑云：「蕺，蔬类，昔越王所嗜，常采于此，遂用名之。在晋为王逸少别址，尚留故池与祠堂。」葛山在会稽县东一十里。《吴越春秋》云：「勾践使女织布，以献吴王，采葛是山。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_51_1249833_0'>(46) 《舆地志》云：「山阴县西有兰亭。」王羲之序云：「此地有崇山峻岭，茂林脩竹。」又云：「俯仰之间，以为陈迹。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_52_1249833_0'>(47) 连山在萧山县西。夏侯曾先《志》云：「连山长冈九里，西北至定山，秦始皇欲置石桥渡浙江，今尚存石柱数十列于江际，世传始皇驱山塞海。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_53_1249833_0'>(48) 擪乌山在萧山县南。东方朔《神异志》云：「山是亚父割断萧山南岭，将擪断乌江。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_54_1249833_0'>(49) 北干山在萧山县北。孔灵符《地志》云：「许询家于此山之阳，询诗云：『萧条北干园。』刘真长叹曰：『清风明月，恨无玄度。』」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_54_1249833_0'>(50) 东山在上虞县西北三十里，谢安石高卧之处。李白《忆东山诗》云：「白云他自散。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_55_1249833_0'>(51) 少微山在会稽五云门外十里。《职方员外郎齐唐墓表》云：「公退居湖山日，少微依山有亭榭，独以书史音乐自适。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_55_1249833_0'>(52) 太白山在剡县西六十里，与少白山连。夏侯曾先《地志》云：「峻极于天岩崔嵬。赵广信炼丹登仙之处，上有白猿赤玃。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_62_1249833_0'>(53) 晋安《海物异名记》：「越人水战，凌波赴敌则有鹘，舟名。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_62_1249833_0'>(54) 《吴越春秋》：「越人以舡为车，以楫为马。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_63_1249833_0'>(55) 白乐天诗：「船头龙夭矫，桥脚兽睢盱。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_68_1249833_0'>(56) 《图经》：「后汉马臻字叔荐，山阳人，为太守，创立鉴湖。在会稽、山阴二界筑塘蓄水，水高田丈馀，田又高海丈馀。若水少则泄湖溉田，如水多则开湖泄田中水入海，所以无凶年。其塘堤周回三百十里，溉田九千馀顷。」一说鉴湖八百里，盖总言之。钱昭度诗云：「越国荷花八百里。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_69_1249833_0'>(57) 《唐书》：「贺知章以秘书监请为道士，诏许之，以宅为千秋观，赐《鉴湖剡州》一曲。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_69_1249833_0'>(58) 《史记》：「少康庶子封于会稽，后二十馀世，至于允常。」《吴越春秋》云：「越之兴霸，自允常始。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_70_1249833_0'>(59) 《舆地志》：「南湖萦带郊廓，款属峰岫，白水翠岩，互相映发，若鉴若图。」王逸少云：「从山阴上路行，如在鉴中游。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_72_1249833_0'>(60) 谢灵运诗：「菱歌调易急。」王翰诗：「不知湖上菱歌女，几个春舟在若耶。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_72_1249833_0'>(61) 西施采莲于若邪溪，李白有《采莲曲》。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_74_1249833_0'>(62) 曹娥江在会稽东四十里。娥，上虞人，父溺死不得尸，娥年十四，沿江恸哭，昼夜不绝，旬有七日，遂投江而死。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_75_1249833_0'>(63) 浙江在萧山县西十三里。《史记》：「吴王杀伍子胥，取其尸盛以鸱夷革，浮之江中。吴人怜之，为立祠于江上，命曰胥山。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_76_1249833_0'>(64) 槩浦在诸暨县北，吴阖闾弟之子夫槩所封之地，因以为名。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_76_1249833_0'>(65) 翁州属会稽，《郡国志》云：「徐偃王昔居于翁州。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_77_1249833_0'>(66) 箪醪在会稽南三里，勾践投醪之所。《左传》：「伍子胥曰：『吴其沼乎？』」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_77_1249833_0'>(67) 《史记》：范蠡事越，既灭吴，乃乘舟浮海以行，终不反，止于陶，天下称陶朱公。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_78_1249833_0'>(68) 若邪溪在会稽县东南。后汉郑洪字巨君，山阴人。孔灵符《会稽记》云：「射的山南有白鹤山，此鹤为仙人取箭。郑洪尝采薪，得一遗箭，顷有人觅，洪还之。问何所欲，洪识其神人也，曰：『常患若邪溪载薪为难，愿朝南风暮北风。』后果然，故溪风至今犹尔，呼为郑公风，亦名樵风。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_78_1249833_0'>(69) 剡溪一名戴溪。《晋书》云：「王子猷尝居山阴，夜雪初霁，四望皓然，忽忆戴逵，时在剡，便夜乘小船诣之。经宿方至，造门不前而反。人问其故，子猷曰：『乘兴而来，兴尽而反，何必见戴！』」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_79_1249833_0'>(70) 兰渚即兰亭也。羲之序云：「会于山阴之兰亭，修禊事也。有清流激湍，引为流觞曲水。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_79_1249833_0'>(71) 戒珠寺在蕺山，本王羲之别业，有鹅池、砚池、题扇桥在焉。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_80_1249833_0'>(72) 了溪在剡县东北，源出了山。《越绝书》云：「禹疏了溪，人方宅土。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_80_1249833_0'>(73) 刑塘在会稽县北。《越绝记》：「大禹会诸侯于涂山，执玉帛者万国，防风后至，禹乃诛之于塘。」贺循《会稽记》云：「防风氏，其身三丈，刑者不及，乃筑高塘临之，故曰刑塘。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_81_1249833_0'>(74) 卧龙山下州宅之西隅，有清白堂、清白泉，太守范文正公命名，有记。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_82_1249833_0'>(75) 沈立《越州图序》：「濒海居人以鱼盐为生。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_82_1249833_0'>(76) 《尔雅》：「东南之美者，则有会稽之竹箭。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_85_1249833_0'>(77) 《汉书·地理志》云：「江南地广，火耕水耨，民食鱼稻。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_89_1249833_0'>(78) 《吴录》、《太康地记》并云：「诸暨境土诸山第一产，檿桑文采如博綦，方正骈次，有如画作，可为屐鞒。上品者一两至数十万。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_90_1249833_0'>(79) 《蚕书》曰：「蚕为龙精。」荀卿《蚕赋》云：「有物于此㒩㒩兮，其状，屡化如神。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_91_1249833_0'>(80) 《图经》：「越贡花纱白编绫、轻交梭绫、轻容生縠、吴绢十样绫、大花绫、编文纱花罗。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_92_1249833_0'>(81) 《名山志》云：「天姥山有枫木千馀丈。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_92_1249833_0'>(82) 上虞有地名五夫，始皇封松木为五大夫之处。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_92_1249833_0'>(83) 嵊县金庭观，《道经》云：「上有桐柏合生。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_92_1249833_0'>(84) 《舆地志》云：「馀姚有太平山，四角各生一种木，不杂他木。一角纯檫，一角纯梓，一角纯棐。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_92_1249833_0'>(85) 《吴越春秋》：「吴王好起宫室，越王使工入山伐木，天生神木一双，大二十围，阳为文梓，阴为楩楠，以献吴王。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_92_1249833_0'>(86) 《郡国志》：「若邪溪有栎木，谢客儿、惠连作诗联句刻于其上。上虞有历山，山下多柏木，吴越名柞为历，故曰历。」诸暨有槠山，剡有榆木山。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_93_1249833_0'>(87) 诸暨有木连院，因有连理木，故得名。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_94_1249833_0'>(88) 东坡《黄甘陆吉传》：「吉隐萧山。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_94_1249833_0'>(89) 《图经》：「诸暨出三如，谓如锦之桑，如拳之栗，如丝之苧。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_95_1249833_0'>(90) 《尔雅》：「梅，楠。」任昉《述异记》：「中有王氏橘园、胡氏梅山、贺氏瓜丘、陵家白莲。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_96_1249833_0'>(91) 《尔雅》：「楙，木瓜。」《埤雅》：「梨百损一益，楙百益一损。」隐居云：「山阴兰亭、尤多木瓜，人以为良果。」《酉阳杂俎》：「材有七绝，一寿，二多阴，三无鸟巢，四无蛊，五霜叶可爱，六嘉实，七落叶肥大。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_96_1249833_0'>(92) 越多双头莲，《埤雅》云：「俗言菱芰、而不分别，惟《武陵记》云：「四角三角曰芰，两角曰菱。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_97_1249833_0'>(93) 《本草注》：「甘蔗有两种，赤色名昆崙蔗，白色名萩蔗，赤蔗出江东会稽。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_97_1249833_0'>(94) 越有杨梅二种，绝佳，一曰官长梅，一曰棱梅。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_102_1249833_0'>(95) 以上鱼名并载于《图经》，越所有者，余皆类此。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_105_1249833_0'>(96) 陆龟蒙养能言之鹜，王羲之爱善鸣之鹅。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_105_1249833_0'>(97) 蛤有文，故谓之文蛤。元微之诗：「乡味尤珍蛤。」合氏子见东坡《江瑶柱传》。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_106_1249833_0'>(98) 铜牛山在会稽县，夏侯曾先《地志》云：「昔有铜牛见于灵汜桥，人逐之，奔入此山，掘地视之，悉铜屑也。」《图经》：「太白山有鸟，尾似鸡，文采五色，口吐绿绶，长数尺，号吐绶鸟。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_107_1249833_0'>(99) 萧山有去虎山，本名虎子山，有猛虎伤人。景德四年六月晦日，虎负一子而渡浙江而去，知县杜守一因改名焉。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_107_1249833_0'>(100) 法华山有双乌鹡，长则送出之，故惟此乌在焉。唐万《齐融守碑》云：「双乌所以示北。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_108_1249833_0'>(101) 会稽有凤林乡。按《吴越春秋》：「禹会诸侯于稽山，因传国政。凤凰栖于木，百鸟伺于泽」。华公《凤林诗》：「苗山会计图书曰，威凤曾栖璧玉枝。」《龙瑞图经》：「葛仙翁有桐木，隐几化为白鹿，三足，号为鹿迹山。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_108_1249833_0'>(102) 孔灵符《会稽记》云：「射的山西南有白鹤，为仙人取箭，因号箭羽山。」上虞有雁田，州志云：「夏禹与诸侯虞乐于此，化感鸟兽，故其地雁为民田春拔草根，秋除其穗。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_110_1249833_0'>(103) 《埤雅》：「鵁鶄子衔母翅。」「鸬鹚吐而生子。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_111_1249833_0'>(104) 《禽经》曰：「凫善没，鸥好浮。」《埤雅》：「鹬翡翠也，衒其毛羽，日浴登阑洄渊之间。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_111_1249833_0'>(105) 越多寒鸦，秦少游词「寒鸦万点」，黄岩叟词「寒鸦如豆」，俱得其实。鳦，燕也，有二种：有胡燕，有越燕，胡燕肥，越燕瘦。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_112_1249833_0'>(106) 《埤雅》：「鹪鹩性巧，故俗呼巧妇。其喙尖利如锥，巢至精密。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_112_1249833_0'>(107) 《尔雅》：「鹭舂锄。」《埤雅》：「步于浅水，好自低昂，故曰舂锄。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_113_1249833_0'>(108) 《禽经》曰：「陆鸟曰栖，水鸟曰宿。」又曰：「山禽之咮多短，水禽之咮多长，山禽之尾多修，水禽之尾多促。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_117_1249833_0'>(109) 欧阳公《花品序》：「牡丹西出丹州、延州，东出青州，南出越州，出洛阳者为天下第一。」扬州出千叶芍药。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_118_1249833_0'>(110) 吴蜕《镇东军监军使院记》云：「大厦之前，木兰特异，越城之中，称为一绝。当前政不轨之际，忽焉凋零，逮彭城王之镇临也，绿叶紫苞，载新阳艳也。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_118_1249833_0'>(111) 州宅旧有海榴亭。唐李绅诗：「怀芳不作翻风艳，列萼犹含泫露妍。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_119_1249833_0'>(112) 《图经》：「菊山在萧山县西，山多甘菊。唐县令李萼、尉丘丹目之曰菊山。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_119_1249833_0'>(113) 《越绝书》：「兰亭在山阴，越王种兰处。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_120_1249833_0'>(114) 天衣寺有杜鹃花最奇，每岁盛开，观者竞集。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_120_1249833_0'>(115) 李白诗：「不到东山久，蔷薇几度花。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_121_1249833_0'>(116) 越多梅花，又馀姚有梅澳湖，以梅得名。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_126_1249833_0'>(117) 嵊县了山出禹馀粮，诸暨乌带山出紫石英。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_127_1249833_0'>(118) 《图经》：「古废市在州南。」《舆地志》曰：「昔蓟训卖药于此市中。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_127_1249833_0'>(119) 彭山在会稽县北。《典录》云：「彭祖隐居之城。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_127_1249833_0'>(120) 《史记》：「始皇令方士徐韨等入海求神药，数岁不得。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_128_1249833_0'>(121) 日铸山在会稽东南五十五里，欧冶铸剑之所。《览古集》云：「会稽日铸洪崖双井不在建腊之后。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_128_1249833_0'>(122) 卧龙山亦产奇茗。范文正公《清白堂记》：「以建溪、日铸、卧龙、云门之茗试之，甘液华滋，悦人襟灵。」张伯玉云：「卧龙茶冠吴越。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_128_1249833_0'>(123) 《茶经》云：「馀姚县茶生瀑布岭者号仙茗。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_128_1249833_0'>(124) 《图经》：「茗山在萧山县西，其上多奇茗。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_130_1249833_0'>(125) 越纸出于剡，舒元舆有《悲古剡藤》文。《图经》：「越出笔管。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_131_1249833_0'>(126) 张伯玉诗：「敲冰呈巧手。」注云：「越俗呼敲冰纸为巧手。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_131_1249833_0'>(127) 《述异记》：「越中有顾家斑竹。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_133_1249833_0'>(128) 《龙瑞图经》：「黄帝藏金简玉字书于宛委山，禹探得之。唐开元二年，投金笼于禹穴，俄有一龙自穴出，现于坛上，赐号龙瑞宫。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_133_1249833_0'>(129) 《齐书》志云：「会稽剡县刻石山相传于名，不知文字所在。宋升明本县名家儿，袭祖行猎，忽见石上有文，凡三处，苔生其上，字不可识，刊笞去之，有大石文、立石文、小石文云云。或云卫夫人碑堕此中，因以为名。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_133_1249833_0'>(130) 《山海经》：「会稽山上多金玉，下多珠石。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_133_1249833_0'>(131) 《吴越春秋》云：「欧冶子为越王铸剑，破赤堇之山而出锡，涸若邪之溪而出铜。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_134_1249833_0'>(132) 《述异记》：「世传黄帝铸鉴于此，故名鉴湖。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_134_1249833_0'>(133) 绍兴丁丑，禹祠之前有光见，人即其处得圭璧。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_134_1249833_0'>(134) 《舆地志》：「蔡邕避难于越，宿千秋亭，仰见榱竹，知有奇响，因取以为笛，遂为宝器。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_134_1249833_0'>(135) 《图经》：「五官省相传有虞翻床，翻为吴长沙王所礼，特设此床，以表贤客。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_134_1249833_0'>(136) 《舆地志》：秦始皇刻石，前有方石，广十丈，云是始皇座，两边有方石八所，云是丞相已下座。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_135_1249833_0'>(137) 汉邯郸淳作《曹娥碑》，蔡邕题曰：「黄绢幼妇，外孙齑臼。」秦望山有始皇《颂德碑》，李斯篆。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_135_1249833_0'>(138) 府治之北有笔飞巷，江淹梦笔之所也。汉王肃随父在郡东斋，夜有女子从地中出，与肃语，将晓辞别，赠墨二员，时肃方注《周易》，多有凝滞，旦用此墨，觉才思开敏。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_136_1249833_0'>(139) 《汉书·王尊传》：「母持布鼓于雷门。」注云：「雷门，会稽城门也，有大鼓，声闻洛阳。」会稽黄閤故有铜漏，古制甚精，王羲之书陆机《漏赋》，镌刻于上，历代以为宝。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_136_1249833_0'>(140) 《越绝书》：「少康立禹祠于陵所」，梁时修庙，少一梁木，夕有风雨，漂一木至，乃梅梁也，今存。窆石在禹陵之前，旧经云：禹葬会稽，取此石为窆。秦少游诗云：「一代衣冠埋窆石，千年风雨锁梅梁。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_137_1249833_0'>(141) 晋太康中，上虞县于道观井中获金罍，故县以金罍名驿。《郡国志》云：涂山有石舡，长一丈，云禹所乘来。宋元嘉中于舡侧掘得铁履一双，梁初又得青玉印。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_137_1249833_0'>(142) 晋太元年中，谢輶为郡守，掘郡厅柱下深八尺，得古铜罂，可容数斗，封题作「越王」字，文甚分明，是今隶书，馀不可识，輶以为范蠡厌胜之术，遂埋之，今不识处。玉印见上注。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_138_1249833_0'>(143) 《图经》：「猎士陈惠度于剡山射孕鹿，既伤，产下一子，以舌舐子，身乾而后鹿母乃死，惠度弃弓矢为僧，鹿死之处生草，号鹿胎草。诸暨有马蹄石，传云始皇东巡，马蹄践此，其迹存焉。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_138_1249833_0'>(144) 萧山，黄竹山。《越绝记》云：「范蠡遗鞭于此，生笋为林，竹色皆黄，状如刀割。」神木见「文梓楩楠」注。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_139_1249833_0'>(145) 《西京杂记》：「会稽贡竹簟，号流黄簟。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_139_1249833_0'>(146) 《会稽记》：「涂山庙中有周时乐器，名錞于。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_140_1249833_0'>(147) 《郡国志》云：「会稽横山有草，茎赤叶青，人死覆之，更活。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_140_1249833_0'>(148) 《图经》：「郡王官廨两杉梁，相传勾践听事之旧梁，历代虽远，材质不异，俗谚云『千年之木，能止心痛』，有削服者，多愈。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_140_1249833_0'>(149) 《石氏宗谱》：新昌石昉墓前有柘木，生而内向，覆坟如盖然。守墓者言，每有登科者，则柘有枝特生，一枝一人，或二三枝则二三人云。《会稽览古集》：「四明山有双石如笋，高数尺，野花丛生其顶，杜鹃鸣时，烂若霞锦。」国朝祖宗遏密，皆三年不荣。职方齐唐尝为之赞。华镇诗云：「鼎湖龙去苍髯断，三载丛花不记春。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_140_1249833_0'>(150) 剡有禅房寺，旧经云：齐安南将军黄僧成有德政，感天雨钱数亿万，遂舍造寺，号钱房院。梁天监中改禅房寺。储山在会稽，东南有粟山。周处《风俗记》：「舜时供储在此。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_144_1249833_0'>(151) 《会稽典录》云：「孙亮时，山阴朱育少好奇字，仕郡门下书佐。太守濮阳兴正旦宴见掾吏，问：『昔王景兴问士于虞仲翔，而未睹仲翔对也，书佐宁识之乎？』育对云云。府君称善。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_144_1249833_0'>(152) 按《吴越春秋》，越王有八臣四友，文种、范蠡、计𥓋最显。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_144_1249833_0'>(153) 《汉书》：严助、朱买臣皆会稽、吴人，武帝时，俱为侍中，后皆为会稽守。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_145_1249833_0'>(154) 唐张万和，诸暨人，遭父母丧，兄弟庐墓二十馀年。万和终，子亦庐墓。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_145_1249833_0'>(155) 齐韩灵敏，剡人，早孤，与兄灵珍并有至性。母亡，无以营凶，共种瓜半亩，朝暮生，遂办葬事。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_146_1249833_3'>(156) 朱育对曰：「处士邓卢叙弟犯公宪，自杀乞代。吴宁斯敦、山阴祁庚、上虞樊正咸代父死罪。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_146_1249833_2'>(157) 虞翻对曰：「句章董黯尽心色养，丧致其哀，怨亲之辱，白日报雠，海内名闻。又魏朱恭明，永兴人，父为乌伤长陈硕所杀，恭明志在报雠。未间，硕病亡，刺杀其子，遂奔魏。后汉魏少英，上虞人，兄为乡人所杀，少英报雠讫，遂亡命。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_147_1249833_0'>(158) 丁兴，会稽人，家近荒野，野火沿烧，兴母老病，乃湿衣覆母，以身障火，身死母存。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_147_1249833_0'>(159) 许伯会，萧山人，遭母丧，结庐墓侧。野火将及坟所，乃悲号恸哭，天忽降雨，火则随灭。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_147_1249833_0'>(160) 山阴钟离表、剡郑僧保、诸暨张万和、萧山许伯会、戴恭，皆以庐墓著名。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_147_1249833_0'>(161) 诸暨张孝和、申屠氏女、萧山郭世道、许伯会，并负土成坟。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_147_1249833_0'>(162) 剡王知元父丧，哀毁卒，高宗改为孝义里。诸暨贾思会母亡，以至孝闻，有司奏改其里为孝义里。永兴郭世道负土成坟，袁愉表其行，敕改所居里为孝行里。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_147_1249833_0'>(163) 山阴严世期好施慕善，有司奏榜其门曰义行。剡公孙达居丧事母，名闻郡县，诏表门闾。萧山俞仅一门四代，兄弟十五人，老幼八十馀口，为乡里所称，观察使孟简书于《图经》，以励风俗。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_148_1249833_0'>(164) 《齐书》：「会稽陆氏有三女，无男，祖父母年八九十，相继卒，三女自营坟葬，为庵，舍墓侧。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_148_1249833_0'>(165) 曹娥见「曹江」注。国史：朱娥，上虞朱回女也，母亡，养于祖媪。娥十岁，里中朱颜与媪竞，持刀欲杀媪，一家惊溃，独娥号呼而前，拥蔽媪，手挽颜刀曰：「宁杀我，毋杀媪也。」媪脱，娥死，事闻，赐其家粟帛。其后会稽令董偕为娥立像于曹娥庙，四时配享。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_149_1249833_0'>(166) 虞翻对曰：「鄞大里黄公絜己，暴秦之世，高祖即祚，不能一致。惠帝恭逊，出则济难。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_149_1249833_0'>(167) 少英见《后汉·党锢传》。虞翻曰：「少英遭此屯蹇，忘家忧国，列在八隽，为世英彦。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_150_1249833_0'>(168) 晋丁潭字世康，山阴人。苏峻乱，成帝蒙尘于石头，潭随从不离帝侧。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_150_1249833_0'>(169) 虞翻曰：「句章王脩，委身授命，垂声来世。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_151_1249833_0'>(170) 晋虞喜字仲宁，馀姚人。太康中诏曰：「喜洁静其操，岁寒不移。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_151_1249833_0'>(171) 晋孔愉字敬康，山阴人。史赞曰：「愉洪止足之分，有廉逊之风。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_152_1249833_0'>(172) 虞翻曰：「决曹掾上虞孟英三世死义。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_152_1249833_0'>(173) 山阴孔愉敬康、张茂伟康、丁潭世康，齐唐时人，号会稽三康。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_153_1249833_0'>(174) 朱育对：「其女则松杨柳朱，永宁瞿素，或一醮守节，丧身不顾，或遭寇劫贼，死不亏行。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_154_1249833_4'>(175) 后汉郑洪、韩说、钟离意皆山阴人，朱隽、戴就皆上虞人，并举孝廉。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_154_1249833_3'>(176) 晋虞潭，馀姚人，陈孔奂，山阴人，唐沈融，会稽人，并举秀才。齐朱仕明，剡人，举茂才。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_155_1249833_0'>(177) 虞寄，馀姚人，弱冠对策，高第起家。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_156_1249833_0'>(178) 会稽陈嚣，字子公，以逊为行，与纪伯为邻。伯窃嚣蕃地自益，嚣见之不言，移一丈以润纪伯。伯觉知患，俱乃还所侵之地。两边俱退，乃为一路。鸿嘉二年，太守右扶风周府君刻石旌表，号曰义里长詹路。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_156_1249833_0'>(179) 吴钟离牧，山阴人，居永兴，种稻二十亩，临熟，民认之，牧遂与稻，后民惭还牧，闭门不受。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_157_1249833_0'>(180) 《后汉·循吏》：孟尝，字伯周，上虞人。为合浦太守。郡无耕稼，所资珠玑，前政贪残，珠徙交趾，尝清洁无求，珠乃还郡。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_157_1249833_0'>(181) 孔晔记云：虞国，馀姚人，汉时为日南太守，有惠政。行部有双雁随轩翔舞，及还馀姚，雁奔随归国。卒，雁栖于墓侧，后遂成群，今馀姚有双雁乡。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_157_1249833_0'>(182) 唐康希铣，会稽人，为饶、海、台、睦四州刺史。颜鲁公撰碑，今断碑犹存。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_157_1249833_0'>(183) 夏香字曼卿，萧山人。《会稽典录》云：「香历任邑长，皆有声绩。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_158_1249833_2'>(184) 后汉王充，字仲任，上虞人，著《论衡》八十五篇。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_158_1249833_2'>(185) 唐沈珣，会稽人，撰《九经大义》百卷。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_158_1249833_1'>(186) 晋谢沉字行思，山阴人，明练经史，撰《晋书》三十馀卷。承字伟平，亦山阴人，博学洽闻，撰《后汉书》一百馀卷。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_158_1249833_1'>(187) 梁孔佥，山阴人，通五经，尤明三《礼》，生徒数百人，三为五经博士。孔子祛亦山阴人，讲《尚书》，听者尝数百人，著《尚书义》二十卷。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_158_1249833_0'>(188) 晋贺循字孝先，山阴人，经学第一，为江东儒宗。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_158_1249833_0'>(189) 唐虞世南字伯施，太宗称世南有五绝，其一博学也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_159_1249833_0'>(190) 晋孙绰字兴公，会稽人，作《天台赋》，谓友人曰：「卿试掷地，当作金声。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_159_1249833_0'>(191) 唐徐浩字季海，为中书舍人，诏令诰策，皆浩为之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_160_1249833_1'>(192) 朱育对曰：「文章之士则任奕、虞翔，齐驰文檄，晔若春荣。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_160_1249833_0'>(193) 唐贺知章字贵真，永兴人，自号四明狂客，醉后属词，动成篇卷，文不加点。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_161_1249833_1'>(194) 唐贺德仁，山阴人，与从兄德基以文辞称，人为语曰：「学行可师贺德基，文质彬彬贺德仁。」虞世南与兄世基俱善属文，时人方之二陆。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_161_1249833_0'>(195) 唐吴融，山阴人，昭宗时，为翰林学士、中书舍人，帝曾指授叠十许藁，融跪作诏，少选成，语当意详。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_162_1249833_5'>(196) 后汉严光字子陵，馀姚人。晋谢敷，会稽人。月犯少微，星占者以隐士当之，俄而敷死。唐秦系会稽人，初隐于剡，后居泉州南安，人号其山为高士峰。方干字雄飞，今五云门外有方干岛、登波坊，有方干池，皆隐所也。唐孔述睿山阴人，与兄充符皆隐嵩山。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_162_1249833_3'>(197) 吴介象字元则，学气术，能于茅屋上煮物而火不焚。吴范字文则，明历数，知风气。晋严卿善卜筮。皆会稽人。后汉谢夷吾字尧卿，山阴人，学风角占候，克日卒。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_163_1249833_1'>(198) 《名画录》：孙遇、僧道芬皆会稽人，以善画著名。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_163_1249833_1'>(199) 宋孔琳之山阴人，徐峤之会稽人，皆善草隶书。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_163_1249833_1'>(200) 晋僧支遁字道林，居沃焦山，与王谢诸公游，唐僧灵澈，会稽汤氏子也，工诗，与刘柳善。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_163_1249833_1'>(201) 《续齐谐记》：汉永平十五年，剡县有刘晨、阮肇，入天台山采药，因遇女仙，半年还家，并无相识，验得七代孙，至太康年失二人所在。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_164_1249833_0'>(202) 《吴越春秋》：越有处女，出于南林，越王聘之，问以剑戟之术。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_164_1249833_0'>(203) 越女论剑曰：「闻斯道者，一人当百，百人当万，王欲试之，其术即见。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_165_1249833_0'>(204) 《史记》：「越伐吴，发教士四万人、君子六千人。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_165_1249833_0'>(205) 《史记》：「项羽起会稽，得精兵八千人渡江。」今山阴有项里，乃羽与叔父梁避仇之地。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_168_1249833_0'>(206) 杜祁公衍，字世昌，会稽人，谥曰正献。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_168_1249833_0'>(207) 孙大资沔，字元规，会稽人，谥曰威敏。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_169_1249833_0'>(208) 姚给事劬，字辉中，山阴人，元祐中为谏官，有直声。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_169_1249833_0'>(209) 顾内翰临，字子敦，会稽人。东坡赠诗云：「君为江南英，面作河朔伟。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_170_1249833_0'>(210) 新昌石氏为东南名族，国朝登第者几三十人。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_171_1249833_0'>(211) 陆左丞佃字农师，弟傅字岩老，俱有才名，比晋二陆。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_172_1249833_0'>(212) 吴先生名孜，嘉祐、治平间名士，舍宅为泮宫。今有祠堂存，君子以为贤于贺监一等。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_172_1249833_0'>(213) 齐贤良唐字祖之，仕至职方员外郎，退居湖山，名曰少微，自为诗云：「直当山面开三径，平截波心种绿杨。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_173_1249833_0'>(214) 钱内翰易，会稽人，景德三年中制科。子明逸庆历二年、彦远庆历六年并中制科。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_173_1249833_0'>(215) 剡中史氏兄弟相继登科，乡号继锦。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_174_1249833_0'>(216) 王荆公有《赠越中处士杜醇》诗。赵处士仲渊，祥符中被召，不赴。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_175_1249833_0'>(217) 故朝奉大夫华君名镇字安仁，尝著《会稽览古诗》百馀篇。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_175_1249833_0'>(218) 诸葛深字通甫，总集历代帝王年纪，自三皇至于大宋，编之为图，名曰《绍运》。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_177_1249833_0'>(219) 刘义庆《世说》云：「顾长康从会稽还，人问山川之美，顾云：『千岩竞秀，万壑争流。』」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_178_1249833_0'>(220) 唐李逊《游妙喜寺记》：「越州好山水，山转远转高，水转深转清。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_179_1249833_0'>(221) 白乐天《和元稹阳明洞天》诗云：「瑰奇填市井，佳丽溢闉阇。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_180_1249833_0'>(222) 虞翻对王府君曰：「海岳精液，善生俊异，是以忠臣系踵，孝子连闾，下及贤女，靡不育焉。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_186_1249833_0'>(223) 王景兴问虞翻曰：「闻玉出昆山，珠生南海，远方异域各生珍宝，曾闻士人叹美贵邦，旧多英俊，徒以远于京畿，含香未越尔。功曹雅好博古，宁识其人邪？翻对云云。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_189_1249833_0'>(224) 严助、朱买臣贵显汉朝，文辞并发，上拜买臣会稽太守，谓曰：「富贵不归故乡，如衣绣夜行，今子何如？」买臣顿首辞谢。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_190_1249833_0'>(225) 晋王羲之除右将军、会稽内史，以上巳日与谢安、孙绰、许询之流会于兰亭，流觞曲水，自为之序，其末云：「后之君子，亦将有感于斯文。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_191_1249833_0'>(226) 唐元稹字微之，罢相为浙东观察使，辟窦巩为副，巩工于诗，与之酬和，故鉴湖秦望之奇益传，时号兰亭绝唱。微之《州宅》诗云：「我是玉皇香案吏，谪居犹得小蓬莱。」时白乐天守杭，常以诗筒往来，后白赴阙，留赠云：「从此舟人应省事，寂寥无复递诗筒。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_193_1249833_0'>(227) 后汉任延为郡尉，会稽称多士，延皆聘请高士，如董子仪、严子陵，待以师友之礼，郡中贤士大夫争往附焉。张霸为守，表用处士顾奉、公孙松等，其馀有业行者皆见擢用，郡中争厉志节，习经者以千数。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_194_1249833_0'>(228) 后汉刘宠为太守，郡中大化，召为将作大匠，山阴五六老叟人赍百钱送宠，宠为人选一大钱受之。吴车俊为太守，在公清忠。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_195_1249833_0'>(229) 后汉第五伦为太守，俗多淫祀，常椎牛祭神，财产困匮，其自食牛肉而不以荐祠者发病且死，先为牛鸣，前后郡将莫敢禁。伦到官，移书属县，晓告百姓，后遂断绝。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_195_1249833_0'>(230) 诸葛恢为太守，元帝谓曰：「今之会稽，昔之关中，政之所先，君为言之。」恢曰：「今天下丧乱，风俗陵迟，宜尊五美，屏四恶，进忠实，退浮华。」帝纳之，以政绩第一增秩。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_196_1249833_0'>(231) 《唐太守题名记》凡九十八人，总管庞玉为首，其最显者姚元之，后为开元贤宰相。其以名见于图经者十人：李大亮、窦怀正、薛平、陆亘、杨于陵、李逊、薛成、元稹、王式、式弟⿔。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_197_1249833_0'>(232) 《宋太守题名记》始于毕文简公士安，其间显者非一，而尤贤者范文正公。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_200_1249833_1'>(233) 《史记》：「越王伐吴，吴败之夫椒，越王乃以馀兵五千人保栖于会稽。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_200_1249833_0'>(234) 《吴越春秋》：「越王入臣吴，拘于石室胆之中，越王服犊鼻、著樵头，斫剉养马。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_200_1249833_0'>(235) 越王念复吴雠，苦身劳心，夜以接日，目卧则切之以蓼，足寒则渍之以水，冬常抱冰，夏还握火。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_200_1249833_0'>(236) 越王为吴王尝恶，遂病口臭，范蠡乃令左右皆食岑草以乱其臭，越人至今以为俗。岑草，蕺也，见前注。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_200_1249833_0'>(237) 《史记》：「勾践反国，置胆于坐，坐卧即仰胆，饮食亦尝胆也，曰：『汝忘会稽之耻邪？』」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_201_1249833_1'>(238) 《吴越春秋》：「越王使国中男女入山采葛作布，以献吴王，吴王大悦。葛妇伤越王用心之苦，乃作《何苦》之诗云云。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_203_1249833_0'>(239) 《越绝书》：闻者曰：何谓越绝？越者国之氏也，绝者绝也，谓勾践时也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_207_1249833_0'>(240) 《图经》：「禹陵在会稽山。」《吴越春秋》：「禹到越，因病死，葬焉，苇椁桐棺，穿圹七尺，下无及泉，坟高三尺，土阶三等。」《越绝书》：「少康立祠于禹陵所。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_208_1249833_0'>(241) 贺循《地志》云：「会稽山有禹井，去禹穴二十五步，谓禹穿凿，故因名之。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_215_1249833_0'>(242) 《史记》：「舜，冀州人」，冀在河南，非东夷也，与孟子之说异。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_216_1249833_1'>(243) 《图经》：夏禹与诸侯会计，因相虞乐于此，故曰上虞。周处《风土记》云：「舜后支庶所封，舜姓姚，故曰馀姚。一曰谓邑有姚丘，即舜母握登感大虹生舜之地。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_216_1249833_1'>(244) 《图经》：虞山在馀姚西三十里。一云在上虞之东。太康《地志》云：舜避丹朱于此。历山在会稽东南八十四里。旧《图经》云：「昔舜耕之所。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_216_1249833_0'>(245) 《图经》：上虞县北有渔河，是舜渔之处。又上虞有地名渔滨，虞滨。《水经》：妫石入东海，江里有上中下三怃，言二女降，时妫地高险回曲，使者至险，辄怃然而叹，故曰三怃。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_216_1249833_0'>(246) 《风土记》：「舜生于姚丘，去上虞四十里有姚丘，即姚丘也。《新记》云：「《书》『平章百姓』，今上虞有百官里。」《会稽记》：「百官者，丹朱从舜于此。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_217_1249833_0'>(247) 舜井在上虞西北三十五里，又有舜水，在县南二百五十步。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_237_1249833_1'>(248) 陈公名过庭，张公名宇发，靖康间为和议使，咸死于虏中。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_238_1249833_1'>(249) 华君名初平，靖康初为太常博士，议礼不屈，事见李参政所作墓志。傅君名崧卿，建炎间虏犯浙东，越守以城降，公举兵赴难，越人赖之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_242_1249833_0'>(250) 蔡孝子名定，父以罪系狱，请代弗许，遂自沉于河，竟脱父罪。事闻乎朝，立庙号悯孝。建炎间，越守以城降虏，班直唐琦奋砖击虏酋，慢骂而死，庙号旌忠。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_243_1249833_0'>(251) 王君名公衮，手斩发冢之雠，自投于府。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_257_1249833_0'>(252) 《梅溪先生后集》卷一。又见单刻本《会稽三赋》卷上，《山堂肆考》卷一二九，《历代赋汇》卷三七，《古今图书集成》职方典卷九三四，雍正《浙江通志》卷二六九，《南宋文录录》卷一。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1249833_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　绍兴府任职，游蓬莱阁。作品：蓬莱阁赋。<div id='poem_1249839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蓬莱阁赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（并叙）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249839")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249839'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249839'>越中自古号嘉山水，而蓬莱阁实为之冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249839_comment'></div>昔元微之作《州宅诗》，世称绝唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249839_comment'></div>近代张公伯玉三章，脍炙人口，好事者从而和之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249839_comment'></div>独未闻有赋之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249839_comment'></div>某筮仕之初，辱为蓬莱客，乃者中秋之夕，与同僚会饮于兹阁，览湖山之胜，玩月于樽俎间，即席赋诗，诸公皆和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249839_comment'></div>既而念之，阁不可以常登，一诗不足以尽意，遂从而赋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249839_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1249839'>王子游会稽，客莲幕，登卧龙之山，蹑巨鳌之阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249839_comment'></div>秀阅千岩，流观万壑，纵远目于东州，畅幽怀于廖阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249839_comment'></div>于时天高气肃，秋色平分，簪盖良朋，把酒论文，俯仰湖山，怀古伤今，登高赋诗，以写我心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249839_comment'></div>周览城闉，鳞鳞万户，龙吐成珠，龟伏东武，三峰鼎峙，列障屏布，草木茏葱，烟霏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1249839", 1249839, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>雾吐</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249839_comment'></div>栋宇峥嵘，舟车旁仵，壮百雉之巍垣，镇六州而开府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249839_comment'></div>东望稽山，思禹之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249839_comment'></div>乔松郁乎故陵，丹青俨于祠宫，藏丹书于䰠穴，流遗画于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249839_comment'></div>南目秦望，哀秦之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249839_comment'></div>方镵石以颂德，骄颜色以相贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249839_comment'></div>嗟仙药之不来，俄腥风之已播。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249839_comment'></div>西望夕阳，送目兰亭，怀王谢之风流，感斯文而涕零，徒观夫茂林脩竹，锁烟霭而冥冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249839_comment'></div>北望沧海，渺其无涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249839_comment'></div>方吴门之画龙，视越国其如蛇，轰雷鼓于一震，虚吴国而成洼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249839_comment'></div>访丽谯之故址，第见乎古木之号鸦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249839_comment'></div>前瞻鉴湖，满目云水，嘉马侯之伟绩，慕贺监之高轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249839_comment'></div>祠荒兮遗迹半湮，宅冷兮黄冠无几，徒有渔舟贾楫，风樵航苇，往来乎鸥鹭之乡，欸乃乎烟波之里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1249839_comment'></div>仰瞻高阁，翚飞崔嵬，俯瞰州宅，缅怀高才，面无时之屏障，家终日之楼台，长湖山之价于几席之上，惜斯人之安在哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1249839_comment'></div>言未毕，客有指斯阁而谓予曰：「子亦知夫阁之所以得名者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1249839_comment'></div>盖始于元和才子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1249839_comment'></div>以玉皇案吏之尊，拥旌麾于千里也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1249839_comment'></div>蓬莱隔弱水三万里，以笔刀坐移于是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1249839_comment'></div>齐名有白，从事有巩，胸中有万顷之湖，真一代之奇伟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1249839_comment'></div>诗章一出，遂能发秦望之精神，增鉴湖之风采，《兰亭绝唱》亘古今而莫拟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1249839_comment'></div>子亦读夫才子之传否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1249839_comment'></div>姑问讯其从何而来、集乎彼而至于此也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1249839_comment'></div>才子之才，固足以起吾子数百年之耸慕，才子之所以获侍玉皇者，亦吾子之所喜攻而深耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1249839_comment'></div>夫何昔之有」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1249839_comment'></div>予于是引客之手，扬袂而起，言契予心，诺诺唯唯，有是哉，斯人也而至于斯也，尚忍言之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1249839_comment'></div>俄而鼓角作于人间，明月出于林端，妙三弄之梅花，烂十分之银盘，釂一觞而径醉，有不尽之馀欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1249839_comment'></div>顷之阴云忽兴，点缀青天，渐山川之蒙笼，若有妒乎婵娟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1249839_comment'></div>倚危阑而感槩，觉兴尽而思旋矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1249839_comment'></div>于是相与啜茗于清白之堂，漱齿于清白之泉，阅唐宋之题名，终夕为之慨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1249839_comment'></div>呜呼噫嘻，死者可作，吾与谁归，其无出乎文正范公之贤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1249839_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　绍兴府就任佥判，代写札子。作品：又代上五札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年12月7日</a>　秩满解官归里。作品：留别民事堂。<div id='poem_542100' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542100' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542100?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留别民事堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年12月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542100")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_542100_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542100'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542100'>二年宦东州，民事了无补。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542100'>俯仰愧斯堂，何以报明主。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542100'>故家萧峰下，归耕及春雨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542100'>平生畎亩心，感槩聊自许。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542100'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_542100_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2de90c9d520147e6892623ff46a0b986_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2de90c9d520147e6892623ff46a0b986");'><span id='2de90c9d520147e6892623ff46a0b986_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，50岁</div><div id='2de90c9d520147e6892623ff46a0b986' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年5月</a>　迁大宗正丞，供职绍兴府，未赴任。累疏乞祠。<br /></div>

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年8月</a>　归至会稽复还临安,追补太学。作品：戊辰闰八月归临安观旧题修竹黄杨丁香慨然有感复书三绝于后。<div id='poem_541456' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541456' class='poemTitle
