id='poem_sentence_0_541456'>吾家风物富檀栾，最爱青青耐岁寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541456'>千里归来面苍玉，不烦时复报平安。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541456'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541456_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541457?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541457'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541457'>同日种松今合抱，后来栽柳已参天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541457'>笑看轩外黄杨树，我亦如君厄闰年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541457'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541457_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_541458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_541458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/541458?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_541458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_541458'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_541458'>蕙兰憔悴菊萎秋，叶底藏春已数头。<div id='poem_sentence_0_541458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_541458'>诗客不知花韵别，却言空结雨中愁<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《梅溪先生文集》卷三）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_541458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_541458'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_541458_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='17fc96d098124a7e92d88c874fe65713_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("17fc96d098124a7e92d88c874fe65713");'><span id='17fc96d098124a7e92d88c874fe65713_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>，39岁</div><div id='17fc96d098124a7e92d88c874fe65713' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　升上舍。作品：升补上舍谢宰相。<div id='poem_1249941' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249941' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249941?labeling=true' target='_blank'>升补上舍谢宰相</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249941")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249941_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249941'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249941'>业肄贤关，滥预千人之列；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249941_comment'></div>名叨舍选，愧居群俟之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249941_comment'></div>嗟小人得福以非常，痛私门钟衅之何亟！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249941_comment'></div>有稽伸谢，徒切衔恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249941_comment'></div>窃以兴庠序于不遑暇给之秋，见圣贤相与致太平之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249941_comment'></div>惟有道主，能散马牛而包干戈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249941_comment'></div>非大仁人，孰明俎豆而辟军旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249941_comment'></div>洪惟上圣，笃任真儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249941_comment'></div>不求矢石之功，专务衣裳之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249941_comment'></div>矢其文德，虽灏灏尔噩噩尔之书无以加；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249941_comment'></div>烝我时髦，岂济济乎洋洋乎之世所能及！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249941_comment'></div>自槐坛之载建，纷银袍而遝来，仰追唐、虞之盛时，祖述熙、丰之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249941_comment'></div>谓科举取士于一时也，非所以造士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249941_comment'></div>而舍法作人于平日也，斯足以得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249941_comment'></div>必将试之以积累之勤，故可期之以远大之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249941_comment'></div>非得行艺两全之美，曷副君相旁求之诚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249941_comment'></div>选既至艰，得宜无滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249941_comment'></div>如某者受才猥琐，赋命穷奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249941_comment'></div>齿才及壮，而遽失所天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249941_comment'></div>仕岂欲干，而盖缘有母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249941_comment'></div>辄施鼠技，妄习麟经，徒专记问之工，莫识谨严之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249941_comment'></div>不束高阁，兼取左丘明、公羊高、谷梁赤之长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1249941_comment'></div>未得美泉，姑为啖先生、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1249941", 1249941, "Clauses/49/Comments/2")'>赵夫子</span>、陆文通之凿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1249941_comment'></div>辞亲故里，鼓箧上庠，幸厕迹于裒衣，获执经于绛帐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1249941_comment'></div>半世仅一名之得，壮心早衰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1249941_comment'></div>匹夫获千金之资，大祸俄及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1249941_comment'></div>未副倚门之望，遽罹枕块之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1249941_comment'></div>三釜之志既孤，五鼎之心何有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1249941_comment'></div>念孝子为亲而求禄，自伤无禄以及亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1249941_comment'></div>思忠臣致主以忘身，或可以身而事主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1249941_comment'></div>退惟畴昔之侥冒，实由在上之作成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1249941_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官命世大才，迪民先觉，躬阿衡惟一之德，为成汤自得之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1249941_comment'></div>靖康之节人所难，绍兴之政古未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1249941_comment'></div>既以其身致中兴之烈，又将与国贻有永之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1249941_comment'></div>广辟成均，兼收士类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1249941_comment'></div>传吾道于孟轲之后，率天下为仲尼之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1249941_comment'></div>二尺短檠，犹念儒生之日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1249941_comment'></div>万间广厦，俱欢多士之颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1249941_comment'></div>遂致缪庸，亦蒙教育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1249941_comment'></div>某敢不益脩操履，力探渊源？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1249941_comment'></div>入大匠之准绳，资哲人之鼓铸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1249941_comment'></div>傥离场屋，粗有进身之阶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1249941_comment'></div>仰戴陶钧，莫知报德之所。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1249941_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='499e91240c14466cab47004f9d9ab0f5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("499e91240c14466cab47004f9d9ab0f5");'><span id='499e91240c14466cab47004f9d9ab0f5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>，40岁</div><div id='499e91240c14466cab47004f9d9ab0f5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>　第五次赴太学，升上舍。作品：中秋前一日舟过山阴，晚稻方熟，忽动相思，呈先之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年10月</a>　为万中祖母墓前亭作文。作品：追远亭记。<div id='poem_1250250' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250250' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250250?labeling=true' target='_blank'>追远亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250250")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250250_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250250'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250250'>儒与墨其道本相为用，故世谓之孔墨，然先师孟子独然辟之，以为无亲，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250250_comment'></div>盖二家皆尚俭，儒俭于其身而厚其亲，墨氏身亲俱俭焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250250_comment'></div>儒治丧以厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250250_comment'></div>墨治丧以薄，儒谓养生不足以当大事，惟送死可以当大事，又谓君子不以天下俭其亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250250_comment'></div>而墨氏乃以薄为其道，宜其得罪于名教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250250_comment'></div>孟子之学出于子思，子思之学出于曾子，而曾子游孔门以孝称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250250_comment'></div>夫子为参作经，其末章有曰：「卜其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1250250", 1250250, "Clauses/20/Comments/1")'>宅兆</span>而安措之，为之宗庙以鬼飨之，春秋祭祀以时思之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250250_comment'></div>参发明夫子之意而为之言曰：「慎终追远，民德归厚矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250250_comment'></div>伋又广曾子之意而为之言曰：「丧三日而殓，三月而葬，凡附于身与棺者必诚必信，勿之有悔焉耳矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1250250_comment'></div>孟子行其所学于师者，尽棺椁衣衾之美以葬亲，富踰于前而葬亦踰于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1250250_comment'></div>其辟夷子之言，足以为万世人子之法，师友渊源得有所自也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1250250_comment'></div>吾徒钱生万中年少而好学，居家以孝谨称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1250250_comment'></div>其丧祖母氏也，能竭力以佐父，其奉窀穸之事，得吉地于黄奥之原以为藏室，极其工力而不计其费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1250250_comment'></div>又筑亭于其前以飨之，名曰「追远」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1250250_comment'></div>将葬，来告于予曰：「大事有日，亭无文以记之，敢请」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1250250_comment'></div>予曰：「予孝以事亲，而厚其所逮事，用孟子不俭之训以治丧，又采曾子『追远』之语以名亭，将不忘于春秋之享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1250250_comment'></div>子之存心如是之厚，谓子非儒者流，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1250250_comment'></div>予敢以荒迷芜陋辞耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1250250_comment'></div>于是乎书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1250250_comment'></div>绍兴辛未十月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1250250_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年11月</a>　为周公宝写行状。作品：周府君行状。<div id='poem_1250315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1250315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1250315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周府君行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1250315")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1250315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1250315'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1250315'>公讳瑜，字公宝，先世姑苏人也，高祖避五代乱，徙居于剡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1250315_comment'></div>曾祖荀、祖惟、父过，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1250315_comment'></div>公为人纯厚质直，介然能自立，以孝友闻于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1250315_comment'></div>治家有法，遇长幼以礼，闺门之内肃如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1250315_comment'></div>宣和中魔寇犯邑，人仓遽奔匿，公独拥亲柩噭号，声彻闾里，冒兵刃扶护以毕窀穸，朝夕悲涕，不忍去墓侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1250315_comment'></div>凶徒相戒曰：「无惊周孝子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1250315_comment'></div>贼平，卒无恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1250315_comment'></div>公喜儒学，尝辟家塾数十楹，延四方名士以淑诸孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1250315_comment'></div>又制夫子暨十哲坐像，画七十二子于一堂，俾崇奉之，大书其侧曰：「尔其亲师友之渊源，就功名之烜赫」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1250315_comment'></div>浃日必设具以集之，亲究其能否，有励业者喜见颜间，面加奖谕，冀其成就，稍怠惰则谆谆戒敕，俾之自勉，由是咸自力于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1250315_comment'></div>绍兴庚申秋，孙汝士预荐书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1250315_comment'></div>乙丑岁，世修肄籍大学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1250315_comment'></div>丁卯秋，汝士、汝能、世则联名乡荐，明年汝士登进士弟，乡人荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1250315_comment'></div>公喜周急，视饥渴者如己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1250315_comment'></div>每盛夏，分命皂隶当往来之冲，烹泉以救暍，穷冬集境内饥民，施以金谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1250315_comment'></div>遇岁歉，发廪赈贷，命诸子悉宽逋负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1250315_comment'></div>剡之南有钜溪，实为要津，行者病涉，公首创浮梁以济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1250315_comment'></div>其子继之，至今蒙其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1250315_comment'></div>初，先君嗜佛，公嗣志弥笃，凌晨焚香端坐，披阅藏经，历四十寒暑，手录因缘几百卷，每以所得语诸子，借示劝戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1250315_comment'></div>剡有名刹，遭兵寇燔毁无馀，公割己赀一新其栋宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1250315_comment'></div>时私第犹未筑，家人以为言，公曰：「兹邑人植福之所，渠可后耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1250315_comment'></div>僧徒德之，祠公于佛舍旁，钦事以报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1250315_comment'></div>公又辟别馆，饭贫士及缁黄之流，滋久不厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1250315_comment'></div>其乐善好施出于至诚，初不求人知，而称道者不容口，其见重于人如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1250315_comment'></div>公状貌魁伟，见者以为异人，自中年鳏居，不再娶，屏嗜欲，务养精神，平生未尝服药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1250315_comment'></div>既老，颜如婴儿，视听不衰，好事者争欲求见，以叩养生之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1250315_comment'></div>晚苦足疾，诸子和药以进，公却之曰：「死生命也，何以药为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1250315_comment'></div>儿女涕泣以请，恝然弗顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1250315_comment'></div>会孙婿高世絪以赴调告违，公曰：「吾某月日行矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1250315_comment'></div>至期，沐浴易衣而坐，神色如平时，谓诸子曰：「吾即行，若辈宜自勉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1250315_comment'></div>言毕奄然而逝，实绍兴二十一年十一月十有六日也，享年八十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1250315_comment'></div>公薄于世利，初以勤俭自守，不广赀产，自诸子既壮，悉以家事付之，积数年富甲一邑，公视之恬然，不以经意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1250315_comment'></div>晚景门阑益盛，身寿康宁，每岁旦暨诞辰，宴坐高堂，子孙诜诜，环列戏䌽，甥婿无虑数十人，争先为寿，剡中以周氏为庆门，言五福者以公为备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1250315_comment'></div>公娶里人孙氏，先公三十二年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1250315_comment'></div>男三人：长仁，承节郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1250315_comment'></div>次侁，承信郎，婺州永康县监酒税，后公一年卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1250315_comment'></div>季亿，先公七年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1250315_comment'></div>女四人：长适同邑吴宗，次适刘升，次适房先厚，次适过谔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1250315_comment'></div>其夫皆早死，诸女孀居，终不改志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1250315_comment'></div>男孙九人：世光、汝贤、汝士，左从政郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1250315_comment'></div>汝弼早卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1250315_comment'></div>世修、汝能、世则、汝砺、世南，皆业儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1250315_comment'></div>女孙六人：长适同邑进士盛卞，次适泰州助教过焌，次适成忠郎、通州支盐高世絪，次适进士商汝霖，次适右迪功郎徐与夔，次适右修职郎、潭州醴陵县慰姚寔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1250315_comment'></div>曾男孙十有二人，曰之元、之纯、之文、之纲、之彦、之茂、之奇、之翰、之才、之望、之邵、之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1250315_comment'></div>曾女孙十有二人：长适进士史之才，次适左迪功郎、明州慈溪县主簿陈嘉善，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1250315_comment'></div>某无似，获与公之孙世修同舍上庠，道出剡溪，尝登公堂，获承謦欬之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1250315_comment'></div>他日再至，而公逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1250315_comment'></div>癸酉秋，公长子仁移书谓某曰：「吾将以十二月十八日葬吾父于邑之方山乡马鞍山之原，祔先夫人之陇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1250315_comment'></div>子辱与吾儿游，知其平生之详，愿状其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1250315_comment'></div>吾将乞铭于士大夫以藏诸幽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1250315_comment'></div>某辞鄙陋，不获，谨撰次所闻如右，谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1250315_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0ef2ba0086324ca296b7cd118ce1c0c9_label'><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_542115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542115'>月良阴剥阳欲旋，蓂馀八荚时半千。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542151'>著鞭先几日，不及送君行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' DetailSwitch("8e013192a8214205aae7a9e9ed292462");'><span id='8e013192a8214205aae7a9e9ed292462_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1163')">1162-1163年</a>，51-52岁</div><div id='8e013192a8214205aae7a9e9ed292462' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年10月</a>　九月离家赴临安，十月到达。除任司封员外郎兼国史院编修崇政殿说书。作品：上殿札子三首。<div id='poem_1249871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除知湖州上殿劄子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249871")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249871'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249871'>臣尝闻先儒孟轲称周武王曰：「不泄迩，不忘远」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249871_comment'></div>是言非止为一武王设，盖为后世帝王治天下之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249871_comment'></div>国家全有吴、蜀之地，蜀去行在万里，远而易忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249871_comment'></div>臣昨蒙恩出帅夔府，二年之间，有所闻见，姑言其大者三事：一曰监司，二曰虚额，三曰马纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249871_comment'></div>今朝廷但知蜀之重权在宣抚、制置二大帅臣尔，而不知四路监司事权之不轻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249871_comment'></div>彼去朝廷既远，威福得以自恣，傲视僚属，有同皂隶，动摇州县，人不聊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249871_comment'></div>监司之中漕臣尤重，一路铨选咸出其手，非若他路止掌金谷之事，苟非其人，则州县受害，无所赴诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249871_comment'></div>地远之害如此，其可忽耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249871_comment'></div>臣愿陛下戒敕宰相，宜于四川监司尤加精择，务得循良恺悌之吏为之，以安远方，不必专取其能办事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249871_comment'></div>臣在夔门，每见蜀之士夫往来，咸言西州诸郡困于虚额，盖是积年拖欠，催科不停，虽屡经赦恩，有司不与放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249871_comment'></div>又昔之监司好聚歛者，取诸州积年酒税、诸色无名科歛之数，以一年最多者立为定额，其后酒税、诸色之数不登，而有名无实之额常存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249871_comment'></div>为总司者以有名无实之数督漕司，而不得其实，漕司亦以有名无实之数督州郡，州郡迫总、漕之威而无钱以输，遂预借民间常赋以充之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249871_comment'></div>后之郡守到官，欲催常赋，闻已预借矣，于预借之外又借焉，有借及二三年者，如邛、彭诸州，困乏尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249871_comment'></div>朝廷知其弊，亦尝有旨减放，总、漕之臣不能奉行德意，而催科如故，州县不堪，凋瘵日甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249871_comment'></div>今之为宣、制二帅及总领者皆一时重臣名士，必能以抚字为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249871_comment'></div>臣愿陛下亲赐御札，俾条陈虚额之弊，而速降诏罢之，庶使远方之民复有生意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249871_comment'></div>臣至夔州，而马适行水，大为夔、峡诸路之害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249871_comment'></div>其端起于吴璘，小人从而迎合之，以行水为便，欺罔朝廷以求官职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249871_comment'></div>臣尝两奉御札，非不欲率先奉行，盖知陛下爱民甚于爱马，而夔、峡之民贫尤甚，故不避罪诛，力陈其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249871_comment'></div>今茶司之马自五十纲后虽不经由，然朝廷未有明文罢之，有一二提举之臣犹以奉行为名，沿江州县治厩造船之役犹未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249871_comment'></div>臣愿速降圣旨，令复行旧路，罢提举马纲之名，诸州所差牵挽之兵各还其所，槽厩舟船不必修治，乃见圣治之不忘远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249871_comment'></div>臣又谓朝廷于蜀非特以远而不可忘，今日之所以立国者，正赖蜀以为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1249871_comment'></div>昔三国之时，吴、蜀为二家，故不能进取中原尺寸地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1249871_comment'></div>今天以吴、蜀全付陛下，正是经营天下、恢复境土之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1249871_comment'></div>今传闻虏人积粮宿兵于境上，有窥蜀意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1249871_comment'></div>蜀，天险也，非虏可得而窥，正恐民心或离，衅由内起为可忧尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1249871_comment'></div>抚绥固结，在今日为尤急，臣故敢献其狂言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1249871_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　迁国子司业，曾于太学参加升舍监试。作品：宿学呈同官。<div id='poem_542264' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542264' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542264?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿学呈同官<span class='inlineComment2'>（时为司业，宿学私试）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542264")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_542264_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542264'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542264'>不听梧桐雨，回头已六年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542264'>齑盐谙旧味，灯火结前缘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542264'>进学思韩愈，同襟有郑虔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542264'>诸生不待劝，忠孝素惓惓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542264'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_542264_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　应诏上书。作品：应诏陈弊事。<div id='poem_1249849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249849' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249849?labeling=true' target='_blank'>应诏陈弊事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249849")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249849_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249849'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249849'>厥今天下之弊安在哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249849_comment'></div>在乎中外小大之臣，各居其官而不知其职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249849_comment'></div>居其官，食其禄，因循苟且，旷职不修，欲望弊事之革、治道之兴，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249849_comment'></div>臣请言其大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249849_comment'></div>夫进退百官者，大臣之职也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249849_comment'></div>献纳论思者，侍从之职也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249849_comment'></div>为天子之耳目、正朝廷之纪纲者，台谏之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249849_comment'></div>内之卿监百执事，外之监司守令，莫不各有其职焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249849_comment'></div>比年以来，为大臣者果能尽进退百官之职乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249849_comment'></div>臣见其进百官，不见其退百官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249849_comment'></div>今日召某人赴行在，明日除某人为某官，是固能进百官矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249849_comment'></div>其所进者未必皆贤才，率一二岁，或半岁，或踰月，类皆迁之，初不问其职事之修与否也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249849_comment'></div>其或有罪，必待台谏论列，然后从而出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249849_comment'></div>或人主之意有所不悦，则谕之使去，而大臣未尝自退百官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249849_comment'></div>居进贤退不肖之职，而所进者未必皆贤，其不肖者又不能自退之，臣知其故矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249849_comment'></div>是己欲收恩而不敢任怨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249849_comment'></div>先正王曾有言曰：「恩欲归己，怨使谁当」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249849_comment'></div>为大臣而不敢退不肖，宁不愧王曾之言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249849_comment'></div>此大臣失职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249849_comment'></div>为侍从者又果能尽献纳论思之职乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249849_comment'></div>臣见其各司其局，而未闻献纳论思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249849_comment'></div>熙宁初，司马光以论新法不从，力辞副枢之命，神宗曰：「枢密，兵事也，不当以他事辞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1249849_comment'></div>光曰：「臣未受命，犹侍从也，于事无不可言者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1249849_comment'></div>是则居侍从者事皆可言，是谓献纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1249849_comment'></div>掌内外制者不止于代言，为给事中者不止于封驳，为尚书侍郎者又不止于各董六官之属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1249849_comment'></div>今之居是官，以各司其局为了官事，以献纳论思为越职，宁不愧司马光之言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1249849_comment'></div>此侍从之失职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1249849_comment'></div>为台谏者又果能尽其所以为耳目、正纪纲之职乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1249849_comment'></div>臣闻欧阳修有言曰：「天子曰是，谏官曰非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1249849_comment'></div>立<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1249849", 1249849, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>殿陛</span>之前，与天子争是非者，谏官也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1249849_comment'></div>又闻苏轼之言曰：「言及乘舆则天子改容，事关廊庙则宰相待罪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1249849_comment'></div>今之为台谏者果能争是非于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1249849", 1249849, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>殿陛</span>之前，如修之言否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1249849_comment'></div>又果能批人主逆鳞而使之改容，如轼之言否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1249849_comment'></div>臣往岁备员馆职，窃闻台谏有论事不行者，而同列不为之助，乃曰我自有体，又有缄默不言者，闻侍从百官言时事则怒而逐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1249849_comment'></div>台谏之职果如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1249849_comment'></div>祖宗时台谏论事，或一章不从，至于十馀章而未尝但已，言苟不行，则继之以去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1249849_comment'></div>赵抃为御史，言陈升之不当除枢副，凡十有六章，于是乞郡而得虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1249849_comment'></div>司马光为谏臣，论刺义勇及乞降黜，凡十有三章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1249849_comment'></div>今之论事者或一再不从，遂不敢复言，宁不愧光、抃等乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1249849_comment'></div>此台谏之失职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1249849_comment'></div>至若内之卿监百执事、外之监司守令，其失职之弊有不胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1249849_comment'></div>臣窃谓欲尽革今日之弊，宜首诏大臣修进贤退不肖之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1249849_comment'></div>内之侍从卿监百执事，孰为贤为才，拔其尤者一二人而进用之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1249849_comment'></div>孰为愚为不肖，亦取其尤者一二人而斥退之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1249849_comment'></div>外之监司、郡守孰为贤才而称职者，拔其尤者一二人而进之于朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1249849_comment'></div>孰为愚不肖而为民害者，亦取其尤之一二而置之于罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1249849_comment'></div>诏下旬日之间，必责大臣以进贤退不肖，而必欲其当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1249849_comment'></div>如是，则进一二人而中外莫不劝，退一二人而中外莫不惧，是则大臣之职举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1249849_comment'></div>于是又诏侍从，宜修献纳论思之职，凡朝廷阙失，知无不言，而不止于各司其局。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1249849_comment'></div>又诏为台谏者，宜尽所以为耳目、正纪纲之职，拾遗补过，纠肃官邪，凡有论列不可但已，宜以祖宗台谏为法，而痛革前日缄默不言之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1249849_comment'></div>虽然，此特人臣之职也，而人主有大职事，陛下不可以不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1249849_comment'></div>一曰任贤，二曰纳谏，三曰赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1249849_comment'></div>臣闻诗人美宣王曰：「任贤使能，周室中兴焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1249849_comment'></div>任贤乃人主之职，而尤急于兴衰拨乱之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1249849_comment'></div>陛下迩日召元老正人，或寘之政府，或寘之台谏，或寘之侍从，天下翕然称为治表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1249849_comment'></div>臣愿陛下既来之则宜力留之，既留之则宜推诚委任之，勿责以繁文，勿待以虚礼，勿贰之以小人，延之岁月，可以责治效矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1249849_comment'></div>又陛下既以疆埸之事委之重臣良将，宜若宪宗之任裴度，断然勿疑，无惑乎纷纷之议而事从中制，以失其机会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1249849_comment'></div>臣窃闻张浚欲守淮，而议者欲其守江，吴璘屯兵德顺，而议者欲其退保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1249849_comment'></div>夫守淮乃所以守江也，舍淮而守江，则长江之险与虏共之矣，江其可守乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1249849_comment'></div>唐韦陟欲李光弼退保潼关，光弼曰：「两军相攻，尺地必争，今委五百里而守潼关，贼得地，势益张矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1249849_comment'></div>力破其说，而成战功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1249849_comment'></div>三路之地陷没久矣，今幸力战而复之，乃欲无故而弃之，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1249849_comment'></div>陛下宜诏之曰：「阃外之事将军制之，可进则进，可退则退」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1249849_comment'></div>如是则事不中制，而机会不失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1249849_comment'></div>臣闻傅说告高宗曰：「木从绳则正，后从谏则圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1249849_comment'></div>高宗命之朝夕纳诲，而中兴有商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1249849_comment'></div>听谏乃人主之职，而尤急于兴衰拨乱之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1249849_comment'></div>陛下自即位以来，虽擢用正人以为台谏，然听纳之美犹未彰闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1249849_comment'></div>臣窃闻近有以酤榷之利而持使命于浙东西者，谏官论列不听，陛下又亲批圣语以谕之，有识咸以为疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1249849_comment'></div>《易》曰：「开国承家，小人勿用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1249849_comment'></div>陛下嗣位之始，何急于用言利之臣，又何以知此曹之名，至于咈谏而用之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1249849_comment'></div>又闻谏官有以尽言而去职，御史有以振职而出台，此必奸臣有以误陛下者，不可不察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1249849_comment'></div>陛下比尝下诏求直言矣，未闻赏一敢言之臣以劝言者，乃闻交结左右者得官，迎合时事者免解，赏谏如此，其何以劝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1249849_comment'></div>夫听谏之道在乎博询广览，不可昵于偏听，而蔽其四达之聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1249849_comment'></div>臣愿陛下亲君子，远小人，推诚听纳，养成圣德，则纳诲者皆傅说，而高宗不独圣矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1249849_comment'></div>臣尝闻汉史赞宣帝曰：「综核名实，信赏必罚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1249849_comment'></div>明赏罚者乃人主之职，尤急于兴衰拨乱之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1249849_comment'></div>臣窃见迩年以来，有姑息之政，无惩戒之罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1249849_comment'></div>去岁逆亮之死，盖上皇圣德所感，天假手其徒以诛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1249849_comment'></div>诸将非唯无毫发之功，虏未退则逗留观望，已退则乘势虏掠，既不干斧钺之诛，而又受无名之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1249849_comment'></div>有盗节钺者，有为两府者，有为三公者，传呼道路，取笑闾阎，名器之滥未有甚于今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1249849_comment'></div>又有爵位已崇而迁犹未已，官曹已冗而员又复增，政或出于多门，命或从于中降，是皆为新政之累，不可不革也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1249849_comment'></div>至若有罪者不诛而恶无以惩，又今日之大弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1249849_comment'></div>秦桧专权误国二十年，而乃生极宠荣，死封王爵，天下莫不切齿扼腕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1249849_comment'></div>纵不剖棺戮尸，其可不行追贬之诛乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1249849_comment'></div>又前日阉寺有弄权纳贿紊乱朝纲者，大将有聚歛交结败坏军政者，大臣有进不由正迷误国家者，台谏有朋奸罔上恶直丑正者，或依城社以自安，或盘根错节以自固，或以去位而幸免，典刑不正，非大舜所以去四凶而服天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1249849_comment'></div>臣闻太上皇即位之初，任用贤相，追贬元恶，窜殛奸邪，天下称快，所以能中兴我宋，致治三纪者，由其能大明刑赏于体元居正之初也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1249849_comment'></div>陛下宜奋乾刚之断，法虞舜之明，继述太上皇故事，先正首恶之罪而追贬之，馀则次第施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1249849_comment'></div>如是，则可以揽威福之权，而陛下之职举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1249849_comment'></div>夫欲救今日之弊，非至诚任贤纳谏，大明赏罚以劝惩之，虽商高宗、周宣王、汉宣帝复出，不可以致中兴之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1249849_comment'></div>故臣愿陛下先举其职，以率百僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1249849_comment'></div>如是，则中外大小之职罔有不举，而弊宁有不革者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1249849_comment'></div>弊事既去，内治既修，则夷狄有不足攘，祖宗之境土指日可复矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_92_1249849_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　春，除起居舍人，升侍讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年5月</a>　由起居舍人任侍御史，肃正纲纪，廷辩奏弹。作品：论史浩札子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年6月19日</a>　自劾，辞官归故里。作品：同登和乐楼韵酬胡邦衡送别兼简刘韶美秘监。<div id='poem_542275' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542275' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542275?labeling=true' target='_blank'>用<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>登和乐楼韵酬胡邦衡送别兼简刘韶美秘监</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年6月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542275")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_542275_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_542275_0'>① 原作周，据四库本改</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542275'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542275'>未访鄱阳范与颜<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：颜鲁公范文正公俱守鄱阳。）</span>，雁山深处且投閒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542275'>紫泥长记曾同召，丹陛何繇更对班。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542275'>我愧未行平日志，公应不创昔时艰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542275'>笔端能制人生死，兼有刘郎在道山<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542275'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_542275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_542275'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_542275_0'>⑴ 自注：予与邦衡、韶（原作诏，据四库本改）美尝同为编修官，予既入台，即罢史职，而二公如故。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_542275_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9cc4956bcd564033a22a86585da17076_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9cc4956bcd564033a22a86585da17076");'><span id='9cc4956bcd564033a22a86585da17076_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>，56岁</div><div id='9cc4956bcd564033a22a86585da17076' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年9月</a>　抵达临安，孝宗召见，上书。作品：除知湖州上殿札子三首。<div id='poem_1249870' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249870' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249870?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除知湖州上殿劄子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249870")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249870_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249870'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249870'>臣闻圣人以无难而畏，贤君以无灾而惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249870_comment'></div>国多难而天有灾，此天心仁爱人君，以灾异而警惧之，欲其恐惧修省，举天下而措之安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249870_comment'></div>昔尧有九年之水，汤有七年之旱，周宣王外有四夷之交侵，内有太甚之旱魃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249870_comment'></div>天灾国难，有若不易支持者，然尧以帝、汤以王、宣王以中兴者，岂非天以灾难启之，一帝二王，能修德以应之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249870_comment'></div>恭惟陛下即位以来，六年于兹矣，躬揽权纲，厉精政事，虽汉宣帝、光武无以加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249870_comment'></div>然天灾流行，无岁无有，旱于夏，涝于秋，饥馑荐臻，疾疫继作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249870_comment'></div>去八月海溢于温，死者以数万计，今岁川蜀荆南赤地千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249870_comment'></div>迩者天作淫雨，害于粢盛，江浙之间被害尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249870_comment'></div>陛下遇灾而惧，遣官分祷，疏决滞狱，减放房缗，诏答大臣，归过于己，可谓能恐惧修省矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249870_comment'></div>臣来自远，不知左右前后论思献纳之臣，亦尝有以修德之说献忠于陛下否乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249870_comment'></div>《书》曰：「惟德动天，无远弗届」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249870_comment'></div>《传》曰：「皇天亲有德，享有道」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249870_comment'></div>尧、汤、宣王之所以应天者，盖在乎是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249870_comment'></div>臣窃谓陛下宜法尧之尽道，汤之自责，宣王之侧身修行，早夜孜孜，惕然自念曰：天道不远，灾异胡为而来哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249870_comment'></div>岂吾心有所未正，意有所未诚，欲明明德于天下者有所未至乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249870_comment'></div>忠直者未用，謟谀者未去，有以害吾之治乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249870_comment'></div>聚敛之臣未斥，奸赃之利未除，有以蠹吾之民乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249870_comment'></div>议法或失之深，用刑或失之过，有以伤吾之仁乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249870_comment'></div>旨酒之嗜，声色之迩，毬马驰骋之娱，有以累吾修身之德乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249870_comment'></div>责己以诚，应天以实，而无事乎虚文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249870_comment'></div>孔子曰：「丘之祷久矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249870_comment'></div>盖言出入起居之间罔不钦，颠沛造次之际必于是，不在乎区区祷祈祭祀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1249870_comment'></div>如是，不惟可以弭灾难于一时，古先帝王之治效功业当复见于今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1249870_comment'></div>孰谓灾异非天所以开陛下耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1249870_comment'></div>学识浅陋，惟陛下采择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1249870_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1249871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249871?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249871'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249871'>臣尝闻先儒孟轲称周武王曰：「不泄迩，不忘远」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249871_comment'></div>是言非止为一武王设，盖为后世帝王治天下之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249871_comment'></div>国家全有吴、蜀之地，蜀去行在万里，远而易忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249871_comment'></div>臣昨蒙恩出帅夔府，二年之间，有所闻见，姑言其大者三事：一曰监司，二曰虚额，三曰马纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249871_comment'></div>今朝廷但知蜀之重权在宣抚、制置二大帅臣尔，而不知四路监司事权之不轻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249871_comment'></div>彼去朝廷既远，威福得以自恣，傲视僚属，有同皂隶，动摇州县，人不聊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249871_comment'></div>监司之中漕臣尤重，一路铨选咸出其手，非若他路止掌金谷之事，苟非其人，则州县受害，无所赴诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249871_comment'></div>地远之害如此，其可忽耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249871_comment'></div>臣愿陛下戒敕宰相，宜于四川监司尤加精择，务得循良恺悌之吏为之，以安远方，不必专取其能办事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249871_comment'></div>臣在夔门，每见蜀之士夫往来，咸言西州诸郡困于虚额，盖是积年拖欠，催科不停，虽屡经赦恩，有司不与放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249871_comment'></div>又昔之监司好聚歛者，取诸州积年酒税、诸色无名科歛之数，以一年最多者立为定额，其后酒税、诸色之数不登，而有名无实之额常存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249871_comment'></div>为总司者以有名无实之数督漕司，而不得其实，漕司亦以有名无实之数督州郡，州郡迫总、漕之威而无钱以输，遂预借民间常赋以充之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249871_comment'></div>后之郡守到官，欲催常赋，闻已预借矣，于预借之外又借焉，有借及二三年者，如邛、彭诸州，困乏尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249871_comment'></div>朝廷知其弊，亦尝有旨减放，总、漕之臣不能奉行德意，而催科如故，州县不堪，凋瘵日甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249871_comment'></div>今之为宣、制二帅及总领者皆一时重臣名士，必能以抚字为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249871_comment'></div>臣愿陛下亲赐御札，俾条陈虚额之弊，而速降诏罢之，庶使远方之民复有生意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249871_comment'></div>臣至夔州，而马适行水，大为夔、峡诸路之害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249871_comment'></div>其端起于吴璘，小人从而迎合之，以行水为便，欺罔朝廷以求官职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249871_comment'></div>臣尝两奉御札，非不欲率先奉行，盖知陛下爱民甚于爱马，而夔、峡之民贫尤甚，故不避罪诛，力陈其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249871_comment'></div>今茶司之马自五十纲后虽不经由，然朝廷未有明文罢之，有一二提举之臣犹以奉行为名，沿江州县治厩造船之役犹未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249871_comment'></div>臣愿速降圣旨，令复行旧路，罢提举马纲之名，诸州所差牵挽之兵各还其所，槽厩舟船不必修治，乃见圣治之不忘远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249871_comment'></div>臣又谓朝廷于蜀非特以远而不可忘，今日之所以立国者，正赖蜀以为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1249871_comment'></div>昔三国之时，吴、蜀为二家，故不能进取中原尺寸地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1249871_comment'></div>今天以吴、蜀全付陛下，正是经营天下、恢复境土之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1249871_comment'></div>今传闻虏人积粮宿兵于境上，有窥蜀意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1249871_comment'></div>蜀，天险也，非虏可得而窥，正恐民心或离，衅由内起为可忧尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1249871_comment'></div>抚绥固结，在今日为尤急，臣故敢献其狂言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1249871_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1249872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249872?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249872'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249872'>臣尝谓君子小人常相为消长，人君未尝不欲进君子而退小人也，然小人常见用、君子每见疏者，盖君子小人之难知，虽尧舜犹以为病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249872_comment'></div>君子目小人为小人，小人亦指君子为小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249872_comment'></div>当孔、颜、桀、蹠相鬨于前，左右佩剑，彼此相笑之际，人君以一人之聪明，诚有不易辨者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249872_comment'></div>况君子直而疏，小人巧而佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249872_comment'></div>直则动多忤意，疏则不能无过，故人主反疑君子为小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249872_comment'></div>巧则能以智术自将，佞则能迎合上意，故人主反以小人为君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249872_comment'></div>自古所以治少而乱多，盖由君子小人之不辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249872_comment'></div>恭惟陛下禀聪明绝人之资，行帝王正大之道，历古兴亡治乱之迹，皆洞然在圣学中，君子小人之情状固已备知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249872_comment'></div>然天下所谓君子者，或未能尽用，或暂用而卒弃之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249872_comment'></div>所谓小人者，或未能尽去，或暂去而复合得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249872_comment'></div>非知人之哲，亦犹尧舜之难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249872_comment'></div>夫君子小人虽不易知，而亦有可知之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249872_comment'></div>君子孤立如松柏，小人附丽如萝蔓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249872_comment'></div>君子进必繇直道，小人进必繇邪径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249872_comment'></div>往者潜藩二使令之臣窃弄陛下之威福，士大夫无耻而好进者莫不奔走其门，陛下赫然震怒，奋自英断，斥而远之，天下莫不鼓舞圣德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249872_comment'></div>然附丽而进者犹未正典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249872_comment'></div>唐宪宗既诛王叔文，并斥八司马之徒，终身不用，元和威令复振，号称中兴，盖由此举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249872_comment'></div>今之附丽者初无八司马之才，而恶则过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249872_comment'></div>附叔文者官止为郎，未有若今之窃高位达官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249872_comment'></div>小人朋比之迹固不逃圣鉴，宜择其一二之尤者薄正其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249872_comment'></div>又取其能自卓立不附炎于炙手可热之时，与尝言其罪恶者，稍进用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249872_comment'></div>如是，则君子小人知所劝惩矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1249872_comment'></div>《语》曰：「君子喻于义，小人喻于利」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1249872_comment'></div>君子之进必以道谊自奋，小人之进未有不以利求合者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1249872_comment'></div>前日朝廷以财赋不足为忧，小人遂献羡馀以求进，朝廷不惜名器，以美官要职处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1249872_comment'></div>诸路监司郡守翕然胥效，为剥下益上计，州县骚然，民不聊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1249872_comment'></div>近者臣僚论列，陛下尝罢一监司，固足以为后来之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1249872_comment'></div>然其尤者方进用未已，全其大而治其细，又何足以惩耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1249872_comment'></div>臣所谓君子小人有可辨者，陛下第观其自何门而来，以何术而进，因可以灼知其为人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1249872_comment'></div>宰执大臣，天下之选，固不可使小人杂处其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1249872_comment'></div>侍从之臣以论思献纳为职，即异日之宰执大臣也，又其可使小人居之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1249872_comment'></div>治道在知邪正，然邪正难于尽知，陛下宜于宰执侍从台谏之臣精加识择，自卿监而下，与外之监司帅守，责之宰相可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1249872_comment'></div>臣言狂妄，惟陛下察之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1249872_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ddfd4a82d2714a5daa0ad79735eec2d3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ddfd4a82d2714a5daa0ad79735eec2d3");'><span id='ddfd4a82d2714a5daa0ad79735eec2d3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>，60岁</div><div id='ddfd4a82d2714a5daa0ad79735eec2d3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年3月</a>　任太子詹事。殿上陛对。作品：除太子詹事上殿札三首。<div id='poem_1249873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除太子詹事上殿劄子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249873")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249873'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249873'>臣恭闻陛下断自宸衷，首建国本，天下相贺，以为社稷无疆之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249873_comment'></div>臣初至阙下，闻太子有尹京之议，臣窃以为未然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249873_comment'></div>臣闻三王之教世子也，不过教之以礼乐，乐以治内，礼以治外，俾知父子君臣之义而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249873_comment'></div>成王之为太子也，召公为保，周公为傅，太公为师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249873_comment'></div>保保其身体，傅傅之德义，师导之教训，未闻其尹京也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249873_comment'></div>国朝虽有真宗故事，至仁宗为太子则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249873_comment'></div>当时左右前后罔匪正人，养成仁厚之性，四十二年之治，虽尧舜亡以加，初不由尹京然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249873_comment'></div>况今天府事繁，其所委任之臣未必有如毕士安者，使太子裁决事事皆善，亦不足以为太子之聪明，增太子之盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249873_comment'></div>万一少有过差，十手所指，小人易得浮议，传闻四方，所损非细，非所以爱太子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249873_comment'></div>大抵太子之职在于问安视膳而已，至于抚军监国，皆非得已事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249873_comment'></div>陛下但与之遴择师友僚属，俾日与端人正士游，养成德性，相与讲论古今治乱之理，他日民情吏事，不患不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249873_comment'></div>臣愿陛下与一二大臣议之，寝尹京之议，以安国本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249873_comment'></div>社稷之福，天下之幸也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1249873_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1249874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249874?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249874'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249874'>臣尝谓官冗之患莫如今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249874_comment'></div>汉唐之时，部刺史之职于今为甚简，而事无有不举者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249874_comment'></div>今之监司有漕、有宪，常平茶盐则有提举，坑冶铸钱则有提点。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249874_comment'></div>其职甚备而治不加于昔，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249874_comment'></div>监司之职愈多，而州县之扰愈甚，于治无益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249874_comment'></div>迩者提点刑狱增置武臣，臣窃以为赘矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249874_comment'></div>且是官之设，臣不知其所为者何事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249874_comment'></div>以详刑之任耶，则一道之使固有其职，未见其废事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249874_comment'></div>曰训练士卒，则总管、钤辖、路分都监者，即武臣之监司也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249874_comment'></div>置之而无用，废之而不为阙，是官之设岂不为冗哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249874_comment'></div>一监司之建，增州县之大扰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249874_comment'></div>臣窃考之，祖宗虽尝有武臣同提点刑狱矣，至嘉祐则罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249874_comment'></div>其诏之大略，以谓武臣或出将阀，或由军功，文墨期会，未必深究，监司项背，适以为烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249874_comment'></div>夫既置之矣而继罢之，知其无益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249874_comment'></div>昔罢之，今复置之，在朝廷则冗于官，在州县则扰于民，则其置之也甚无谓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249874_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈断然察其无用，罢去勿置，庶几官不虚设，事得其当，而人各安其职矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249874_comment'></div>臣不胜至愿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1249874'>谓：雍正本、四库本俱作「闻」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1249874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1249874'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_1249874_0'>⑴ 《梅溪先生奏议》卷四。又见《历代名臣奏议》卷一六七。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1249874_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1249875' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249875' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249875?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249875_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249875'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249875'>臣尝谓人心险于山川，难于知天，谓其不可测也，况狼子野心之人，乌能保其久而无患也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249875_comment'></div>唐太宗教射于殿廷，群臣谏之曰：「律不可以兵刃至御在所，今以卑碎之人张弓挟矢于殿陛之侧，万一狂夫窃发，出于不意，非所以重社稷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249875_comment'></div>诚哉，忧国爱君之言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249875_comment'></div>亲卫将卒且犹不可，而谓归附之人信其终无害也难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249875_comment'></div>近者归明、归正之将，陛下旌其忠义，壮其勇略，擢而用之，日与之亲，使效其力，所谓推赤心置人腹中者，固足以见大有为之志矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249875_comment'></div>然天下之人凡有爱君之心者莫不疑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249875_comment'></div>谓自古以来莫难于用斯人，而用之者罕见其久而不为吾患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249875_comment'></div>其弃彼归我，心已二矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249875_comment'></div>今乃使之朝夕以侍左右，设或不饱其欲，其谋之深、计之久，而心之不能保，则将若之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249875_comment'></div>至于斯时，虽悔无及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249875_comment'></div>臣请择其灼然忠诚可以任用、陛下素所知者，属之以事权，厚之以爵禄，勉之以功名，亦足以示无疑之意，而激其图报之心矣，何必日亲之而后为待遇之至哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249875_comment'></div>臣愿陛下考之于往古，虑之于将来，特加宸念，毋惮一时之难从，而置久远于无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249875_comment'></div>不胜社稷生灵之愿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1249875_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　太子詹事任上，得知张栻上章弹劾张说，写信张栻。作品：与张佐司。<div id='poem_1249934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与张佐司</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249934")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249934'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249934'>比闻盗窃枢柄，甚于阳虎取宝玉大弓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249934_comment'></div>公首摧其奸，与先正忠献公斩范琼、曲端等何异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249934_comment'></div>天下无贤愚远迩，莫不称快，知大贤之有后，况我辈耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249934_comment'></div>不有君子，其能国乎，真可为社稷贺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249934_comment'></div>某卧病半年，日与死迫，忽被误恩，已力辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249934_comment'></div>更望力赐一言，俾遂所请，甚幸甚幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1249934_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
桐庐
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1b5569ace9a64697920e6c0a05bd03a7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1b5569ace9a64697920e6c0a05bd03a7");'><span id='1b5569ace9a64697920e6c0a05bd03a7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，50岁</div><div id='1b5569ace9a64697920e6c0a05bd03a7' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>去国回乡，过桐庐，游严陵钓台。<div id='poem_542152' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542152' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542152?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钓台</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542152")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_542152_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542152'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542152'>汉高嫚骂四皓隐，周武干戈伯夷饿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542152'>南阳故人幸无失，先生胡为亦高卧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542152'>清风却在夷皓上，千古真能激贪懦<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作儒，据四库本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542152'>客星夜向钓滩明，想像年时临帝座。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542152'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_542152_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>去国回乡，过桐庐，游严陵龙门院。作品：严州龙门院满散天申节。<div id='poem_542153' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542153' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542153?labeling=true' target='_blank'>严州龙门院满散天申节</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542153")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_542153_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542153'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542153'>棹弭龙门下，诚驰天阙边。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542153'>平生畎亩意，祝圣更惓惓。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542153'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_542153_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永康
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='492e7ad7f8304eef8e4b2d11beab7a7a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("492e7ad7f8304eef8e4b2d11beab7a7a");'><span id='492e7ad7f8304eef8e4b2d11beab7a7a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，50岁</div><div id='492e7ad7f8304eef8e4b2d11beab7a7a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　去国回乡，过永康。作品：宿永康县黄塘店观稼有感。<div id='poem_542154' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542154' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542154?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿永康县黄塘店观稼有感</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542154")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_542154_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542154'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542154'>路入黄塘喜更疑，地名虽是里闾非<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542154'>眼中禾稼已如许，薄有田园宜早归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542154'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_542154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_542154'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_542154_0'>⑴ 自注：予家之东十里，地名亦曰黄塘。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_542154_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
丽水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8079803e100a420abe6df760c40ac387_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8079803e100a420abe6df760c40ac387");'><span id='8079803e100a420abe6df760c40ac387_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，50岁</div><div id='8079803e100a420abe6df760c40ac387' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　去国回乡，经婺州、缙云、处州到青田，游石门洞。<div id='poem_542157' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542157' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542157?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游石门洞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542157")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_542157_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542157'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542157'>雁山饱见两龙湫，洗眼新观石洞流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542157'>欲向故乡寻白鹿，先来仙隐访青牛<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：青牛道士隐于石门。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542157'>破荒喜诵刘郎句，跻险思从谢客<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542157'>天下林泉看未足，分将身世早休休。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542157'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_542157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_542157'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_542157_0'>⑴ 原作容，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_542157_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='08b98308fd4e4b0194aa01436cda7fbc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("08b98308fd4e4b0194aa01436cda7fbc");'><span id='08b98308fd4e4b0194aa01436cda7fbc' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>返乡游缙云仙都。作品：游仙都。<div id='poem_542280' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542280' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542280'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542280'>皇都归客过<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>仙都，厌看西湖看鼎湖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542280'>洞接龙泓片云近<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，山分雁荡一峰孤<sup class='reference -----title
金华
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='50e4cc03f66c4af28886f5396ae6a19b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("50e4cc03f66c4af28886f5396ae6a19b");'><span id='50e4cc03f66c4af28886f5396ae6a19b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>，52岁</div><div id='50e4cc03f66c4af28886f5396ae6a19b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　返乡经桐庐重游钓台，与同年及同乡会饮双溪楼。<div id='poem_542279' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542279' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542279?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过婺女同年王节推<span class='inlineComment2'>（夷仲）</span>黄教授<span class='inlineComment2'>（万顷）</span>乡人华主簿<span class='inlineComment2'>（子周）</span>会饮双溪楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542279")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_542279_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542279'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542279'>年时尝泛婺溪舟，未上清风八咏楼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542279'>天为故人偿夙愿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，水知吾辈喜清流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542279'>沈郎不为吟诗瘦，王粲长怀去国忧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542279'>明日山川共人远，乡情年契两悠悠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542279'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_542279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_542279'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_542279_0'>⑴ 自注：辛巳五月至婺溪，夷仲诸同年有登楼之约，忽闻钦宗讳遂止。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_542279_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
鄱阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3696884e7b3548e5a9799dcac5ba138e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3696884e7b3548e5a9799dcac5ba138e");'><span id='3696884e7b3548e5a9799dcac5ba138e_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年7月</a>　饶州任职。作品：饶州到任谢表。<div id='poem_1249892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>饶州到任谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249892")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249892'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249892'>遭时遇主，协五百世之昌期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249892_comment'></div>共理分符，叨二千石之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249892_comment'></div>试之民事，简在帝心<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249892_comment'></div>伏念臣奋身诸生，隶业太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249892_comment'></div>上皇亲策，擢居多士之先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249892_comment'></div>陛下误知，眷出群臣之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249892_comment'></div>方御天之十日，畀近地之一麾，旋蒙召还，屡辱赐对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249892_comment'></div>魏徵之蕴几展尽，贾谊之言略施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249892_comment'></div>曾未阅于三时，已遍更于数职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249892_comment'></div>遽从宪府，擢贰天官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249892_comment'></div>人言遭际之非常，臣惧宠荣之过分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249892_comment'></div>力辞成命，果获俞音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249892_comment'></div>荣联书殿之名，假守便藩之郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249892_comment'></div>身获全于进退，恩不替于初终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249892_comment'></div>况此楚东之故邦，实为江左之奥壤，颜真卿英风如在，范仲淹遗爱犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249892_comment'></div>臣实何人，可预兹选！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249892_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下法舜受禅，体尧宅天，广收众正而首及滞淹，乐听谠言而不罪狂直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249892_comment'></div>遴选朝廷之士，畴咨岳牧之臣，虽地分内外之殊，而心蔑轻重之异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249892_comment'></div>知臣本出乎白屋，谓臣可牧夫细民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249892_comment'></div>札命十行，忧分千里，臣敢不仰奉德意，叨宣教条？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249892_comment'></div>虽才非太公，不能五月报政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249892_comment'></div>然忠犹杜甫，未尝一饭忘君。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1249892_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年7月</a>　饶州任职，于饶水南僧寺拜会张浚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　饶州任职，修建颜鲁公、范文正祠。作品：追和范文正公都阳诗，郡斋即事。<div id='poem_542358' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542358' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542358")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_542358_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542358'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542358'>理郡端如理乱丝，范公往矣欲谁师。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542358'>典刑犹有堂中像，光艳长存壁上诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542358'>未报国恩嗟老去，不逢人杰恨生迟。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年7月</a>　自饶州改知夔州知州兼元帅，并除敷文阁待制。作品：同官酌别。<div id='poem_542490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
