-----title
九江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bf5017cc0cb84461b339a022b76df347_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bf5017cc0cb84461b339a022b76df347");'><span id='bf5017cc0cb84461b339a022b76df347_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>，54岁</div><div id='bf5017cc0cb84461b339a022b76df347' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　自饶州卸任,从间道去往夔州，逗留庐山，乞辞不允。作品：庐山纪游四十韵。<div id='poem_542542' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542542' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542542?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐山纪游四十韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542542")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_542542_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542542'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542542'>我性好山水，思向庐山庐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542542'>五老招我游，有约芝山初。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542542'>兹行适所愿，孰曰非天与。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542542'>入眼庾公楼，兴已先篮舆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542542'>云开圣治峰，石扣仙人居<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_542542'>香炉望烟霭，净社观芙蕖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_542542'>虎溪聊自笑，天池步宜纾<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：天池最高不及游。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_542542'>半月圆通留，幽亭乐有馀<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：寺有至乐亭。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_542542'>趣如六一翁，境似山环滁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_542542'>侯溪煮月泉，石耳供岩蔬<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：峰以生石耳得名。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_542542'>破戒戏鱼酒，踏园梦羊猪。<div id='poem_sentence_10_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_542542'>贤关得家音<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，天恩拜新除。<div id='poem_sentence_11_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_542542'>抗章复辞免<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，行色仍踌躇。<div id='poem_sentence_12_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_542542'>遂作南山游，首过荆林虚。<div id='poem_sentence_13_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_542542'>凌云入康谷，临流清可渔。<div id='poem_sentence_14_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_542542'>欲饮第一水，山深足趑趄。<div id='poem_sentence_15_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_542542'>汤泉本何来，忽从龙口嘘。<div id='poem_sentence_16_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_542542'>鸾溪寻故家<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：归宗寺本王右军宅。）</span>，墨沼波犹潴。<div id='poem_sentence_17_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_542542'>石镜不可见，悬崖照谁梳。<div id='poem_sentence_18_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_542542'>寻真到简寂，入观惊丘墟。<div id='poem_sentence_19_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_542542'>缅怀黄与陆，何处飘霞裾<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_20_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_542542'>眼明见飞瀑，涧壑鸣琼琚。<div id='poem_sentence_21_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_542542'>何<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>落句思李，练飞诗陋儒。<div id='poem_sentence_22_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_542542'>新桥跨虹霓，出月明蟾蜍。<div id='poem_sentence_23_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_542542'>两州劳五马，同日传双鱼<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_24_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_542542'>神光照万杉，飞白留天书。<div id='poem_sentence_25_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_542542'>遥瞻星子城，青山点舂锄。<div id='poem_sentence_26_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_542542'>我行未及西，三峡知何如。<div id='poem_sentence_27_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_542542'>登桥阅天险，奋地轰雷车。<div id='poem_sentence_28_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_542542'>壮哉五丁力，凿此千尺渠。<div id='poem_sentence_29_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_542542'>群峰列耆老，深渊蓄璠玙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑺</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_30_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_542542'>古刹依朱砂，穿林骇猿狙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑻</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_31_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_542542'>万卷已空阁，三竹犹扶疏。<div id='poem_sentence_32_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_542542'>肩舆足茧卒，传诗手疲胥。<div id='poem_sentence_33_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_542542'>佳境尚无穷，雅兴良已摅。<div id='poem_sentence_34_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_542542'>身随禽往还，兴逐云卷舒。<div id='poem_sentence_35_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_542542'>重寻讷庵老，细论无言予。<div id='poem_sentence_36_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_542542'>节物变炎凉，迟留费居诸。<div id='poem_sentence_37_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_542542'>在路何悠悠，归梦频蘧蘧。<div id='poem_sentence_38_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_542542'>秋风雁还荡，缄封寄乡闾。<div id='poem_sentence_39_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_542542'></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_542542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_542542'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_542542_0'>⑴ 自注：太平兴国宫有圣治峰、刘仙石。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_542542_0'>⑵ 自注：三儿时在太学，一日得两书。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_542542_0'>⑶ 自注：前辞夔州，今辞入（原作穴，据四库本改）对。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_20_542542_0'>⑷ 自注：简寂观乃陆修静道场，有黄石公岩观，今荒废。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_22_542542_0'>⑸ 四库本作月，雍正本、光绪本作河</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_24_542542_0'>⑹ 自注：至开先，得唐江州、李南康书。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_30_542542_0'>⑺ 自注：五老诸峰，及三峡、玉渊并在栖贤。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_542542_0'>⑻ 自注：楞伽在朱砂峰下，自栖贤寺（原作子，据四库本改）路穿荆棘而行。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_542542_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
奉节
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c7d85df63b8d45eab5a2f77ca7a18af1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c7d85df63b8d45eab5a2f77ca7a18af1");'><span id='c7d85df63b8d45eab5a2f77ca7a18af1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1167')">1165-1167年</a>，54-56岁</div><div id='c7d85df63b8d45eab5a2f77ca7a18af1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年11月</a>　抵达夔州，出任知州。作品：夔州到任谢表。<div id='poem_1249893' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249893' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249893?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夔州到任谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249893")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249893_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249893'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249893'>地易夔门，难敢辞于蜀道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249893_comment'></div>心倾尧日，远尤甚于长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249893_comment'></div>祗拜训词，惟深感涕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249893_comment'></div>臣顷由御史，出守番阳，任甫及于期年，报蔑闻于五月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249893_comment'></div>慕言言之烈于颜鲁国，学优优之治于范仲淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249893_comment'></div>扰切戒于庸人，第务近民之易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249893_comment'></div>罪或得于巨室，方知为政之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249893_comment'></div>比因有疾而丐祠，不谓误恩而分阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249893_comment'></div>况鱼复素称岩邑，在坤维实为要冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249893_comment'></div>苟非文武之长才，曷副蕃宣之重寄，岂臣庸缪，可称使令？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249893_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下德方日新，仁若天覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249893_comment'></div>悯鸟道乌蛮之险，有刀耕火种之劳，非善治不可以怀柔，谓微臣或勤于抚字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249893_comment'></div>录其寸效，畀以雄藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249893_comment'></div>臣敢不究疾苦于闾阎，布教条于州郡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249893_comment'></div>观武侯八阵，居安未免于忧边；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249893_comment'></div>诵杜甫百篇，有志不忘于爱主。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1249893_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　抵达夔州，知州任上，除敷文阁待制，因马纲改从水路上书。作品：夔州论马纲状。<div id='poem_1249868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1249868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1249868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夔州论马纲状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_1249868")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1249868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1249868'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1249868'>准枢密院劄子：枢密院奏，知夔州张震申，所有四川宣抚司措置川蜀马纲，改移水路事件，委有未便去处，申乞详酌施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1249868_comment'></div>奉圣旨：除打造舟船外，其馀事件并令吴璘管办，其舟船令王某疾速应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1249868_comment'></div>臣契勘马纲利害，前知夔州张震及诸司论列已详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1249868_comment'></div>其中利害之大者莫过于财与力，二者皆出于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1249868_comment'></div>臣自入境以来，切见夔、峡之间土狭民贫，面皆菜色，衣不蔽体，非江浙、荆湖诸路之比，为监司守令者傥能皆劳心抚字，无一毫之扰，犹恐不能活之，况今马纲之害极重，财力必当大困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1249868_comment'></div>臣滥居牧民之任，不敢不以实闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1249868_comment'></div>今来茶马司及宣抚司所买马，每岁计一万八百馀匹，约计二百一十六纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1249868_comment'></div>本州若循环起发，合用船三十馀只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1249868_comment'></div>每只打造约费八百馀千，马舡易坏，势须一年一易，计一岁之费为钱二万六千缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1249868_comment'></div>自夔至归，水路二百四十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1249868_comment'></div>每纲梢工水手约九十人，较一岁之终为工一万八千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1249868_comment'></div>每人口食雇钱约五百文，上下水约一十五日，通一岁计之，当费钱十二万贯，草料批券亦不下二万馀缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1249868_comment'></div>较一岁之间，费于马纲者盖十五六万贯矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1249868_comment'></div>本州三县，所管梢工水手不满四五百人，若循环不替，所少犹半，必当役农民而为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1249868_comment'></div>而夔之民力既困如此，若又从而役之，必有流离转徙之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1249868_comment'></div>本州每年财赋之入不满二十万，合起上供、折估、经总制及官兵请给皆在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1249868_comment'></div>今马纲之费侔于所入之赋，虽曰令吴璘管办，岂能偿所费十之一二？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1249868_comment'></div>财非天降地出，又必取之于民，而夔之民贫如此，财何自而出耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1249868_comment'></div>以一州推之，则一路、诸路之困又可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1249868_comment'></div>况水路正行瞿唐、滟滪之险，又有恶滩二十馀节，水势湍急，濆漩颇多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1249868_comment'></div>马性善惊，闻滩声汹涌，必致跳跃，不可控驭，撼动舟船，必有覆溺之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1249868_comment'></div>臣昨在饶州，亲见马纲经过，涉咫尺之渡，中流遇风，十死八九，况千里之至险耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1249868_comment'></div>若舍舟用陆，则自夔至峡皆重岗复岭，上倚绝壁，下临断崖，行人攀缘，鼓慄汗下，遇雨泥滑尤不可行，非特有害于人，兼亦非马之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1249868_comment'></div>若欲削平险阻，便马之行，非惟重困民力，又恐有害控扼之险，非所以保护全蜀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1249868_comment'></div>臣所论利害，皆是目见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1249868_comment'></div>苟坐视一路生灵之困不以奏闻，则上孤陛下任使之意，将负不忠之罪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1249868_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈特降睿旨，令马纲复行旧路，以安远人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1249868_comment'></div>不胜大幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1249868_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年12月19日</a>　夔州任上，得长孙。作品：闻诗得男名之曰夔诗。<div id='poem_542694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻诗得男名之曰夔<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年12月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542694")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_542694_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_542694_0'>① 夔乙酉十二月十九日生，诗以二月二十四日作</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542694'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542694'>巫邑初传鲤<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：是日巫山送双鲤。）</span>，吾家遂得夔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542694'>遥来如马地，却应梦熊诗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542694'>官忝二千石，孙看第一枝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542694'>欣同君子抱，祝汝似吾儿。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542694'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_542694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_542694'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_542694_0'>⑴ 自注：闻诗在鄱阳日，梦熊入书院。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_542694_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　知夔州，与查元章别。作品：周漕行可和诗复用前韵并简元章。又酬元章。又用行可韵。<div id='poem_542663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周漕行可和诗复用前韵并简元章</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542663")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_542663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542663'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542663'>重闻鸣凤瑞岐阳，不比清斋老太常。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542663'>帝里别离头并白，夔门邂逅日初长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542663'>诗篇照眼腾光艳，兰友倾心蔼国香。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542663'>天遣西来端有意，要令我辈共壶觞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542663'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_542663_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_542666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又酬元章</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542666")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_542666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542666'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542666'>叱驭西来愧子阳，旧交重见白眉常。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542666'>伤心鬼录人何短<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：怀冯员仲。）</span>，回首蓬山话更长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542666'>夔府并游容倚玉，计台高选辍含香。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542666'>我非逸少君如谢，聊继兰亭曲水觞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542666'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_542666_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_542664' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_542664' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/542664?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又用行可韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28586, "南宋", "王十朋", "poem_title_542664")'>王十朋</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_542664_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_542664'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_542664'>二公海内姓名闻，我亦追随到蜀门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542664'>龙卧庐中叹诸葛，蛙居坎底陋公孙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542664'>雨听巫峡梦时滴，花看杜鹃啼处痕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542664'>酬唱又成夔府集，论文欣对少陵尊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542664'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_542664_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　知夔州，与刘韶美会别。作品：次韵韶美失舟闵书。夜与韶美饮酒瑞白堂，秉烛观跳珠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_542721'>儒生嗜底物，书卷挂口齿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_542721'>刘侯西南来，岁月十首尾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542721'>闭门阅古今，过眼分亥豕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542721'>异书照神藜，奇字哭妖鬼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_542721'>许身如蠹鱼，文字共生死。<div id='poem_sentence_5_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_542721'>风流反得罪，去国果谁耻。<div id='poem_sentence_6_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_542721'>仙舟载秘阁，便腹贮名理。<div id='poem_sentence_7_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_542721'>江神亦世情，逐客多不喜。<div id='poem_sentence_8_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_542721'>厄同焚书秦，恶类灭邢燬。<div id='poem_sentence_9_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_542721'>沾濡遍箱箧，痛惜到骨髓。<div id='poem_sentence_10_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_542721'>我初闻为惊，终夜成坐起。<div id='poem_sentence_11_542721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_542721'>得君诗细读，罪己不罪水。<div id='poem_sentence_2_542719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_542719'>毫端写出万斛珠，共向炎天作冰雹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_542719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_542719'>妃子名园荔子丹，绛囊初摘堆金盘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_542719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_542719'>细擘轻红唱君曲，咀嚼水晶牙颊寒。<div -----title
湖州

<div class='label1' id='5fcbcbd210dc45b993b55aab29c82517_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5fcbcbd210dc45b993b55aab29c82517");'><span id='5fcbcbd210dc45b993b55aab29c82517_link' -----title
瑞安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6f4697b4817d48d1ab660f52416648a9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6f4697b4817d48d1ab660f52416648a9");'><span id='6f4697b4817d48d1ab660f52416648a9_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　赴泉州，途经瑞安，好友相邀，留宿一夜。作品：过瑞安。<div id='poem_543145' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_543145' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_543145'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_543145'>我家古乐成，老未识安固。<div id='poem_sentence_0_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_543145'>偶把清源麾，首问南塘路。<div id='poem_sentence_1_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_543145'>解维日已晏，入境天欲莫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_543145'>张子自陶山<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：子猷。）</span>，扁舟惠然顾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_543145'>沈君壮年别<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：敦谟。）</span>，相见发垂素。<div id='poem_sentence_4_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_543145'>访旧多不存，来观莫知数。<div id='poem_sentence_5_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_543145'>平原二十人，邂逅喜相遇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_543145'>谓我宜少留，欲敕不腆具。<div id='poem_sentence_7_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_543145'>我驱不敢疾，曲为一宵住。<div id='poem_sentence_8_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_543145'>临江有高阁，登览可以赋。<div id='poem_sentence_9_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_543145'>澜同孟子观，目作少陵注。<div id='poem_sentence_10_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_543145'>灯火照鱼龙，谈笑惊鸥鹭。<div id='poem_sentence_11_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_543145'>衔杯乡意浓，窃食君恩误。<div id='poem_sentence_12_543145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_543145'>晨起酒未醒，潮来报催渡。<div -----title
泉州
-----detail

id='poem_title_543248_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_543248'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_543248'>君以民脂膏，禄尔大夫士。<div id='poem_sentence_3_543248'>指呼有鹰犬，嗜欲肆蛇豕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_543248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_543248'>但言民至愚，孰谓天在迩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_543248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_543248'>昭然甚可畏，殃必反乎尔。<div id='poem_sentence_5_543248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_543248'>清源庭中石，整顿自今始。<div id='poem_sentence_9_543248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_543248'>何敢警同僚，兢兢惟敕己。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年12月</a>　知泉州,夫人贾氏病故。作品：哭令人。<div id='poem_543167' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_543167' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_543167'>钟情正是我辈事，鼓缶忍同方外人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_543167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_543167'>熊胆未酬平昔志，牛<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_3_543167'>闽山满眼同来路，木落风号泪满巾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_543167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_543167'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_543167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_543167'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_543167_0'>⑴ 原作午，据四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　知泉州，乞祠归隐。作品：悼亡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　知泉州，修筑“七首塘”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年8月</a>　知泉州，立韩魏公祠，率同僚祭祀。作品：韩魏公生于泉南州宅故未有祠于典为阙，郡圃有庵名大隐即之以祠八月戊子率同僚祀之。<div id='poem_543270' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_1_543270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_543270'>梦符蚌腹生珠夜，事应台躔捧日时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_543270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_543270_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　知泉州，张孝祥卒，作诗悼念。作品：悼张舍人安国。<div id='poem_543310' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　知泉州，浚洑田塘，建放生池。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　孝宗以敷文阁直学士、左朝奉郎命王十朋知台州军事，王十朋以病辞，乃复提举太平兴国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　离任泉州，迁知台州，力辞，并再乞致仕。作品：闻胡邦衡改知泉州复用前韵。<div id='poem_543367' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_543367' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_543367'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_543367'>上念温陵为择人，知公名节世无邻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_543367_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
